12TH-01 河岸静悄悄 / Quiet is the River Bank

谢尔盖：看见土匪了吗？
Sergey: Did you see the bandits?

红弩箭：我看见了几只金花鼠，除此之外就什么都没有了。
Lilya: Not even a sign; just some chipmunks.

谢尔盖：那我们就在这里休息吧，中尉，天气很热，得让马喝口水。
Sergey: *sigh* Think we should take a rest, Lieutenant? Sun's beating down, and we need to get the horses watered.

谢尔盖：我们到的地方比预定的侦察点要远很多，它们一定都累坏了。你绝不能累坏自己的马。
Sergey: We've gone quite a way farther than the assigned watchpoint. Even if we can push on, the horses can't. Never exhaust your horse, remember.

红弩箭：那就按你说的，休息一下。
Lilya: Fine. Take a break, team.

红弩箭：对了——下次拿着望远镜的时候别对天瞎看。
Lilya: And Sergey, if you shine the light off that telescope into my eyes one more time ...

红弩箭：要是反光再晃到我的眼睛，我就用导弹轰你。
Lilya: The last thing you'll see is a missile to the face. Understood?

谢尔盖：好、好吧，我下次一定不会了。
Sergey: Ahh. Understood, Lieutenant.

中尉收起望远镜，交给身旁的谢尔盖。她敏捷地翻身下马，从鞍袋中拿出一捧事先备好喂马用的燕麦。
Lieutenant Lilya retracts the telescope and hands it to Sergey. She hops off her horse and pulls a handful of oats from her saddlebag.

战马：咴。
War Horse: *neigh*

马儿喘着气吃完了一捧燕麦，随后又贪婪地用鼻子使劲蹭上红弩箭的颈窝。
The horse snorts as it eats, then nudges Lilya's neck affectionately with its nose.

红弩箭：嘿——你还想吃吗？
Lilya: Hey, soldier, you want some more?

正当她打算再取一些食料的时候，谢尔盖靠上前来。
Just as she reaches for more feed, Sergey leans in.

谢尔盖：这匹马是你第一次骑吧，中尉？
Sergey: This your first time riding this horse, Lieutenant?

红弩箭：没错，我想它要饿坏了。
Lilya: Yeah. He's a hungry fella.

谢尔盖：没有这样的事，它是个狡猾的贪吃鬼，别把它喂得太好了。它得学会自己去嚼草根。
Sergey: *chuckle* No, he's just greedy. Uses the same trick on all the new riders. If he wants something else to eat, he'll have to find it himself.

红弩箭：你听见了，这可不能怪我——去喝水吧。
Lilya: Oh, little liar, you heard him. No more oats for you. Go get some water.

红弩箭稍微用力地拍了拍马脖子，遭到拒绝的马儿垂头丧气地摇晃着脑袋，冲着谢尔盖打响鼻。
Lilya pats its neck a little harder. Denied another bite, the horse lowers its head before giving Sergey a dejected snort.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：把它交给我吧，中尉。
Zeno Cavalryman I: Leave him to me, Lieutenant.

另一位士兵上前来，卸下被固定在马背上的飞行扫帚，随后将闹脾气的马牵去河边饮水。
Another soldier steps forward, unfastens the flying broomstick from its saddle, and leads the disgruntled horse down to the river for a drink.

飞行女巫将扫帚安放在身边，在与季节不符的温暖空气中，她嗅到尤为浓烈的河水腥气与苦艾的干涩气味。
Lilya sets the broom down beside her. In the unseasonably warm air, she catches a dry scent, sharp with river water and wormwood.

谢尔盖：这真的很不对劲，十一月的日子不应该这么暖和——你见过这样的冬天吗？
Sergey: This feels wrong, doesn't it? It really shouldn't be this warm. Ever seen a November like this, Lieutenant?

红弩箭：我在十一月见过夏天，但那是在地球另一头。现在这儿的天气确实有些怪。
Lilya: Yeah, but on the other side of the world. This is weird for sure.

谢尔盖：没错，早就该下雪了，可天气还像刚入秋那样。
Sergey: Usually, the snow would be thick by now. But this feels like early autumn still.

青年抬手，抹去额头的汗水，指着面前泛着青光的河流。
The newly enlisted cavalryman lifts a hand to wipe the sweat from his forehead, then points to the river, its surface glowing with a greenish light.

谢尔盖：如果不是这样的天，再过几个星期，河面应该要上冻了，我们可以直接从浅滩走过河。
Sergey: The Don would usually be frozen over in the shallower parts, too. We'd be able to walk right over it.

谢尔盖：过河之后，再往前走一点就可以看见顿河的拐点，到那时，沿着河流往上走，就到了别列格勒。
Sergey: The meander's just a little farther. Bereggrad would be too, if we could just cross it.

谢尔盖：你去过城里吗？
Sergey: You been to the city?

城里——对生活在这片草原上的人来说，这座城指的就是别列格勒。
The city. To the people of this steppe, these words mean Bereggrad.

红弩箭：基金会在城里有分部，我偶尔会去送些信件，或者处理一些烦人的手续。
Lilya: Yeah. To go to the Foundation branch. Delivering letters, dealing with procedures. *sigh* Annoying stuff like that.

谢尔盖：说起信件——一些上前线的同村人给家人来信了，听说他们正在回家的路上。
Sergey: Oh, speaking of letters, my townsfolk sent some back from the front. Seems they're on their way home.

谢尔盖摇摇头，似乎并不太认同同乡返家这件事。
Sergey shakes his head, seemingly unhappy with the idea.

红弩箭：怎么，和你邻里关系不好，不想见他们？
Lilya: What, they beat on you or something?

谢尔盖：怎么能这么说呢，我和谁的关系都好，我很开心他们能活着回来。
Sergey: Why'd you say that? I couldn't be happier to have them home safe.

谢尔盖：我是在想，就算这时候回家，也没有地可以种了。
Sergey: It's just ... It should be farming season, but they'll come back to find nothing to farm.

年轻的哥萨克就地蹲下，用力抓了一把脚边的牧草。
He squats down and grabs a fistful of the grass beneath his feet.

谢尔盖：天气是暖和，但这小麦像中邪了一样，还没到新年呢，秆子就蹿得老高，眼瞧着都要枯了——但它偏偏又不结穗。
Sergey: The weather was just right last year, but something went seriously wrong. It grew fast, tall too, but didn't make any seed at all.

谢尔盖：夏天那茬粮食收成又差得没眼看，我们村里的谷仓都快空了……留在边境至少饿不死。
Sergey: Our summer harvest was a complete disaster. The barns are almost empty. At least they won't starve to death at the front.

红弩箭：你想得太简单了，重塑之手的军队可能会出现在任何地方，没有地方是安全的。
Lilya: But Manus Vindictae could strike at any time out there. Probably safer for them to come back.

谢尔盖：重塑之手会打到顿河来吗？
Sergey: Do you think the Manus will reach the Don?

红弩箭：现在他们的主力都在西欧，但他们就像老鼠一样，在你觉得很干净的地方，突然冒出来一大窝。
Lilya: Hard to say. The main force is in Western Europe for now, but the Manus are like rats. Who knows where they might show up next.

新入伍的骑兵有些毛躁地抓着还没个影子的胡须。
The young Cossack scratches at the few thin hairs on his upper lip—the boy's best attempt at any kind of moustache.

谢尔盖：自从加入芝诺以来，我还没有打过一场像样的仗。
Sergey: Ugh, I swear I did more fighting during training than in actual service.

谢尔盖：成天只等长官一声令下——“嘿，谢尔盖，去找找那些土匪藏在哪里？”可怜的谢尔盖就要跑断腿了。
Sergey: All I do is wait around for orders, and this one's just stupid. "Find out where the bandits are hiding." Are you serious?

谢尔盖：土匪哪里是那么好找的，又不像咱们骑兵军有个大营地。那都是些缩在林子里的几十号人，到了夜里就去打家劫舍。
Sergey: You're telling me we have to find just a few dozen people who only come out at night somewhere in all this forest? They may as well have us search for a needle in a haystack.

红弩箭：那你觉得打仗是怎么回事？
Lilya: Hm. So what do you think real war is like?

谢尔盖：我知道打仗是怎么回事。我的爷爷，我的父亲，还有我哥哥，都上过战场。
Sergey: Oh, I know what it's like. All the men in my family have fought on the battlefield: my grandfather, my father, and my brother.

青年并没有很好地回答红弩箭的问题，他尴尬地移开视线，看向红弩箭一直放在身边的飞行扫帚。
He dodges the question, fixing his eyes on the flying broom Lilya always carries.

谢尔盖：下一个渡河的浅滩还要再走几里才能到，为什么你不飞过去看一眼呢，中尉？
Sergey: Next ford's a few kilometers off yet. Why don't you just fly over and take a look?

谢尔盖：这样我们的侦察任务就算完成了，天黑之前就可以回营，不需要在外面过夜。
Sergey: It'll be a heck of a lot faster. Be able to return to camp before dark.

红弩箭：红色38吃的可不是草料，我没有多少燃料用来浪费。另外，它的飞行时长是按分钟计算的。
Lilya: Red 38 isn't fueled by grass like one of your horses, and its flight time is measured in minutes, not hours.

红弩箭：我可不想在真正遇到敌人的时候，驾驶一架超过保养寿命的扫帚。
Lilya: Or are you trying to keep me grounded if we get into a fight?

谢尔盖：如果你教会我怎么用飞行扫帚，是不是就能多申请一架Su-01ве？我们可以轮流飞行。
Sergey: I know! Why don't you teach me to fly a broomstick and apply for a new Su-01ве? Then we can take turns scouting.

红弩箭：我很想看你从天上掉下来的样子，可我不想和军长说你手底下的骑兵在我的扫帚上摔断了一条胳膊。
Lilya: Oh, I'd love to see your face when you fall from the sky, but I'd rather not tell your commander that his cavalryman broke a leg flying my broom.

谢尔盖：别忘了，你刚来的时候也不会骑马，是斯捷尔诺娃上校教你才没有从马上摔下来。
Sergey: *chuckle* It's not like you're any better. If it weren't for Colonel Sternova, you'd have gone face-first in the dirt your first day on a horse.

谢尔盖：而我在年龄只有你一半的时候，就能从村子里骑马去别列格勒卖甜菜了。
Sergey: I, on the other hand, was regularly riding from my village to Bereggrad with sacks full of beets at half your age.

红弩箭：这可要比马难驾驭多了。我说不行就是不行，也不要在晚上来偷我的扫帚。
Lilya: Broomsticks aren't horses. And if I catch you sneaking in to steal it at night, you're a dead man. Got it?

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：没错，他从小就喜欢偷别人东西。
Zeno Cavalryman I: You're right to warn him, Lieutenant! Sergey's been stealing since he was a kid.

饮马归来的骑兵加入了争吵。
The cavalryman returns with the horse just in time to join the verbal beating.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：他去年想偷我们家的渔网，被我爷爷抓到，差点打断了手。
Zeno Cavalryman I: Just last year, he tried to nab our fishnet. My grandpa caught him, of course. Nearly broke Sergey's hand when he wrestled it from him!

芝诺骑兵Ⅱ：哈哈——
Zeno Cavalryman II: Hahahahaha!

同行骑兵哄笑起来，被轻易揭穿的青年涨红了脸，随即别过脸，移开了视线。
The other cavalrymen burst into laughter as Sergey's face flushes beet red. He turns away but barks a hasty rebuttal.

谢尔盖：闭嘴！——反正你们家老爷子从来不用那张网。
Sergey: Shut up! It's not like he ever used it anyway.

不良行为被揭穿的人没能制止同伴的嘲弄。骑兵们趁着兴头，一件件揭露谢尔盖的旧日丑闻。
But he can't stop the taunts. The cavalrymen take obvious delight in dredging up his old scandals one by one.

谢尔盖：该死的，我绝对不要再和你们这帮净会诽谤的蠢小子待在一个队伍。
Sergey: Damn it! Stop making things up about me! Ugh, I can't stand it here!

谢尔盖：回去我就要申请调到老土岗村的那个连去。
Sergey: You know what? When I get back, I'm going straight to the commander to get transferred to the Prisklonnaya company.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：老土岗村，你是说五连？那不是你老情敌指挥的部队吗？
Zeno Cavalryman I: You mean the fifth company? Isn't their commander your old rival in love?

哥萨克中爆发出一阵更加猛烈的嘲笑。
Even louder laughter erupts from the Cossacks.

红弩箭：呵……
Lilya: Heh!

飞行女巫不再理会嬉闹的骑兵，她抬头，望向河对岸高空中滚动的厚重云团——那些悬空的、洁白的堡垒。
Ignoring their rowdy banter, Lilya lifts her gaze to the heavy clouds drifting beyond the river like white fortresses floating in the sky.

干燥而温暖的气流掠过高空与原野，缓缓推动浮空的城堡，也卷起红弩箭被汗水沾湿的头发。
Dry, warm air sweeps across the plain, driving the floating castles forward and tugging at Lilya's sweat-soaked hair.

红弩箭：啧，这温度是真不对劲，走两步都能闷出一身汗，我就知道基金会永远抽不出人来管这里的怪事。
Lilya: Tsk, already sweating. This heat's not normal. No one in the Foundation got the time to look into this?

红弩箭：也许会把维尔汀放出来？……那倒也不错。
Lilya: Maybe they'll send Vertin? That wouldn't be so bad.

她的注意力逐渐被天地交接处的平缓线条所吸引，这是在深藏于群山中的基金会里永远无法看见的景物。
Her eyes are drawn to the merging line between earth and sky—a view she could never have seen from the Foundation, hidden away in the mountains.

当视线顺着坡道游走时，一些似乎是在跳动的黑点突兀地破坏了地平线的流畅感。
Then, along the slope, black figures burst into view, tearing ragged gaps into the horizon.

红弩箭：……嗯？谢尔盖？
Lilya: Hm? Sergey?

谢尔盖：怎么啦？
Sergey: Someone call me?

红弩箭：刚才是不是你把望远镜拿走了？把它拿来。
Lilya: Me. You got the telescope, right? Hand it over.

谢尔盖：你说什么，中尉？他们现在可要把我脑袋都给吵晕了！
Sergey: What's that, Lieutenant? I can't hear you!

红弩箭：我说——
Lilya: I said—

谢尔盖：唔——！
Sergey: Urgh!

一颗子弹——像是对放松警惕者的责罚——穿透了谢尔盖的血肉。
A bullet tears through Sergey—the price for a moment of carelessness.

红弩箭：见鬼！
Lilya: Damn it!

谢尔盖：啊、啊……啊啊啊——
Sergey: Ah, ah! Ahhhhhh!

谢尔盖在同伴们惊愕的目光中仰面倒下，随之而至的是枪声、马匹嘶鸣、杂乱难辨的叫喊——
Before the cavalrymen can even react, Sergey has collapsed onto his back. The plain explodes into gunfire, screaming horses, and panicked shouts.

——以及红色38的神秘学引擎紧急启动的尖啸。
Among the chaos, Red 38 roars to life.

飞行女巫已然升空，她在低空兜着圈子，暂且充当着引人注目而难以命中的靶子。
Lilya kicks off, circling low to draw the enemy's fire.

红弩箭：是匪军！他们在河对岸。萨沙，你把谢尔盖拖到石头后面去！
Lilya: Bandits! Across the river! Sasha, get Sergey behind the rocks!

红弩箭：其他人朝我指的方向开枪，掩护萨沙和谢尔盖，每人打光五发子弹之后找机会上马！
Lilya: The rest of you, cover fire in this direction! Empty a clip, and mount your horses!

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：是、是，中尉！你要到哪儿去？
Zeno Cavalryman I: C-Copy! What about you, Lieutenant?

红弩箭：我当然要飞到他们背后去捅一刀——离我远点，别被掀翻了！
Lilya: I'll take a little trip to their rear. Stand back! Wouldn't want to swallow my exhaust!

五秒后，久经战阵的Su-01ве成功载着它的飞行员冲上100英尺的高度，轻而易举地从敌人头顶飞越。
Seconds later, the battle-tested Su-01ве soars a hundred feet in the air, effortlessly carrying its pilot over her enemies.

红弩箭：好吧，让我看看你们都是些什么东西。
Lilya: Alright, let's see what you got.

这场隔河对射的小规模冲突，在一方拥有空中优势的情况下迅速结束。河畔复归宁静。
The brief exchange of fire ends quickly under air superiority. The riverside grows quiet again.

红弩箭悬停在半空中，将地面的局势尽收眼底。
Lilya hovers above, keeping a bird's-eye view of the area.

红弩箭：土匪损失了两个人，剩下三人在往北逃……噢，他们想钻到树林里去。
Lilya: Two bandits down, last three heading north. Looks like they're taking cover in the woods.

红弩箭：骑兵军只有谢尔盖一人受伤，萨沙留下来照顾他了，看样子无大碍。
Lilya: Only one injured, and Sasha's with him. Nothing to worry about there.

红弩箭：剩下的人已经上马，正在往渡河的浅滩去。那这两个被抛下的土匪就交给他们负责吧。
Lilya: Rest are headed to the ford. They can deal with the downed two.

飞行女巫调转方向。此刻她还能看见骑马逃亡的匪军的背影。
Lilya turns in the direction of the fleeing bandits.

红弩箭：——我看看能不能揪出他们的老巢。
Lilya: I'll find their hideout.

重重树影当然能遮蔽地面追击者的视野，但对于空中的鹰隼来说不是很起作用。
The shadows of the trees may veil the ground below, but they cannot stop the eagle that soars above.

枯黄的叶片已被秋风吹走了大半，如今只有细瘦的树杈胡乱地刺向天空，织成一片稀疏的网。
Most of the yellowing leaves have been swept away by the autumn wind, leaving their slender branches thrusting out in all directions, like a sparse web strung up into the sky.

红弩箭：加把劲，跑得再快点吧，别浪费我的时间。
Lilya: Come on. Can't you run faster? Wasting my time.

对习惯了高速掠空的飞行员来说，这种“追击”几乎和放牧没有太大的区别。
For a pilot accustomed to the high speeds of the Su-01ве, this hunt is closer to herding livestock.

红弩箭：照这么飞下去，我看我还有时间停下来喝一杯……
Lilya: At this rate, I'll have time to spare for a drink.

红弩箭：——！
Lilya: ...!!

一朵黑云在她的耳旁炸开。
A black cloud explodes beside her ear.

紧接着，是第二朵——第三朵——数百枚细碎的金属碎片在她的衣服上撕开了数不清的裂口。
Then another. And a third. Hundreds of tiny metal fragments slice countless cuts into her clothes.

红弩箭：见鬼了，是防空炮？！——他们从哪里搞来这种东西？
Lilya: Triple-A? How the hell did they get that?

飞行女巫没有掉头。她压低高度，几乎擦到了树梢，执拗地以规避姿态向防空火力的来源飞去。
She drops down, flying so low that the tips of the branches nearly catch her as she presses on toward its source.

红弩箭：开火的声音很近了，还差一点——让我看看你们在林子里都藏了些什么东西！
Lilya: Just a little closer. Let me see what you're hiding in there!

干枯交错的枝条将她眼前的景物切成碎片，四处爆炸的黑色硝烟又让一切都染上模糊不清的暗色。
Bare branches slice her view into fragments. Black smoke smears everything dark.

但她的勇气还是为她换来了一个电光石火般的瞬间。鹰隼的目光敏锐地捕捉到一块架设着防空炮的林中空地。
But her determination grants her a fleeting instant, just enough for her to catch sight of a small glade where an anti-aircraft gun stands.

红弩箭：这就够了！
Lilya: Gotcha!

她拉起Su-01ве，以几乎是与地面垂直的角度刺入高空厚重的云团。
She pulls the Su-01ве upward, driving it into the heavy clouds at a near-vertical angle.

红弩箭：那门高射炮不是这个时代的东西，土匪绝对搞不到手。至于型号……不，就算只瞄一眼我也不会认错——
Lilya: Weapon's not from this era. No way bandits could get their hands on it. Yeah, there's no mistaking the model.

红弩箭：——AZP-37高射炮，是芝诺的武器。
Lilya: Automatic anti-aircraft gun 37—AZP-37. It's Zeno.

红弩箭：得把这事告诉军长。也许维尔汀也会感兴趣，可以给她捎条留言。
Lilya: Need to report this to the commander. Vertin will want to know, too.

“喀咯咯——”
*eek-eek-eek*

红弩箭：哈？
Lilya: Huh?

身下的扫帚发出松散的破碎声，精密的飞行器早已在防空火力中受损，如今终于快要支撑不住。
Her broom's been hit. It's failing.

红弩箭：现在可不行，老伙计，你至少得把我带回河边去，我可不想栽在这林子里。
Lilya: No, no, no. Not now, buddy! At least get me clear of the woods!

晚了。暴力驾驶的后果就是无故障时间急剧缩短。她急速下坠。
It's too late. She's already pushed the broom beyond its limits. She's falling fast.

红弩箭：好吧，这下是真的糟了。
Lilya: This is bad. Really bad.

红弩箭：稳住！
Lilya: Steady!

12TH-02 永恒的秋天 / The Eternal Autumn

顿河下游的平缓草甸上，土围子和原木围出了一块营地。不比一座堡垒更大，但足以让一支军队歇下脚。
Downstream of the Don, on a stretch of flat meadow, a camp rises from mud-packed earth and stacked logs. It's no grand fortress, but it's enough to shelter an army at rest.

芝诺骑兵军军长伊万·伊万诺维奇·布列科夫正在观看一群新兵按照芝诺操典练习队列。
Zeno cavalry commander Ivan Ivanovich Burakov stands, tall and broad, watching the recruits drill their formations.

军长伊万：……
Commander Ivan: ...

斯捷尔诺娃：军长。
Sternova: Commander.

一声问候之后，芝诺骑兵军参谋长莎宾娜·斯捷尔诺娃迎面走来。
With her usual brief greeting, Zeno cavalry chief of staff Sabina Sternova approaches.

军长伊万：有什么事吗，莎宾娜？
Commander Ivan: Yes, Sabina?

斯捷尔诺娃：我看你从指挥室里出来了，有什么要指示的吗？
Sternova: You've left the war room. Any commands?

军长伊万：只是出来透透气，帐篷里太闷热了。
Commander Ivan: Just catching a breath. That stuffy air will be the death of me.

军长伊万：另外，最近又有很多新兵入伍，我多出来走一走，能帮助他们记住自己的军长长什么样。
Commander Ivan: Besides, a little more time among the pups won't hurt. Keep their spines straight and their commanding officer's face in their minds.

斯捷尔诺娃：的确如此，但我相信他们已经认识你了。很多人都是在你亲自去村子里动员的时候，才决定加入骑兵军的。
Sternova: I think they know your face already. After all, many only joined the cavalry after you gave that speech in the village.

军长伊万：那也不错。有些新人是红柳树村来的，他们有带来什么新消息吗？
Commander Ivan: Ah, Tamarovka. Tell me, Sabina, did the pups bring any news?

斯捷尔诺娃：你想问的是佳琳娜夫人？——她一切都好，说希望有机会再见你一次。
Sternova: From Ms. Galina? She's fine. She says she wants to see you again at your convenience.

军长伊万：最近骑兵军不会有大动作，应该能抽出一点时间去看看她。
Commander Ivan: There are no great rides ahead for now. I'll find the time to visit her.

军长伊万：只是，“金色饥荒”一直持续的话，她继续留在顿河也不安全了。
Commander Ivan: *sigh* If this Golden Famine continues to gnaw at us, the Don will be no home for her.

军长伊万：冬天迟迟不肯到来，依靠土地生长的作物又没法自然生长……要想个办法劝她离开。
Commander Ivan: No winter, no crops ... The steppe has turned her most brutal. I will find a way to persuade her to leave.

斯捷尔诺娃：我们早就向基金会报告了顿河的饥荒，可答应派来解决气候异常的调查员至今没见到踪影。
Sternova: We reported the famine to the Foundation long ago, but there's still no sign of their investigators.

军长伊万：这里不是战争的焦点地区，人手不足的时候，基金会是不会在乎顿河的。
Commander Ivan: This is far from the heart of the war, and with the Foundation so short on manpower, we're just dust on their boots.

营地入口处传来杂沓的马蹄声，这是营内常见的“意外发生”预兆。
Messy hoofbeats burst from the camp entrance—the familiar sound of bad news.

斯捷尔诺娃：——怎么了？
Sternova: What's wrong?

红弩箭：——让一让，别顾着你们的队列了，新兵蛋子们。
Lilya: Out of the way, rookies. Wounded incoming.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：是啊，你们没听到这家伙的鬼哭狼嚎吗？太可怜了，我都要替他流眼泪了。
Zeno Cavalryman I: Yeah, don't you hear his whimpering? I could almost cry.

匆忙进入营地的马队后方，缀着一名被绑在马背上的哀嚎着的伤员。
At the rear, tied to a horse's back, sits a wailing injured boy.

谢尔盖：你——你可闭嘴吧，萨沙。我中弹了——中弹了！你明白吗？
Sergey: Sh-Shut up, Sasha! I got shot, for God's sake, shot!

谢尔盖：疼啊，太疼了——我要废了……
Sergey: Argh, it hurts. I'm never going to walk again.

营地里的士兵纷纷为归营的侦察队让开通路。红弩箭率先在开阔处下马，接着是除了谢尔盖之外的其他队员。
The soldiers quickly clear the way for the reconnaissance team. Lilya dismounts first, followed by the rest of the team, except Sergey.

芝诺骑兵Ⅱ：谢尔盖交给我吧，中尉。你去找军长。
Zeno Cavalryman II: Leave Sergey to me, Lieutenant. You should report to the commander.

红弩箭：没问题，你最好想个办法让他住嘴，否则他迟早要对营地里的每个人都讲一遍受伤的英勇壮举。
Lilya: On it. And find a way to shut him up before the whole camp's forced to listen to the wails of his great military feat.

她刚刚转过身，就看见了正在向事发现场走来的骑兵军指挥官。
She turns to see the commander striding forward.

军长伊万：我就在这里，出什么事了，中尉？
Commander Ivan: No need to hunt me down, Lieutenant. What news?

红弩箭：出了些小意外，在下一批飞行扫帚的零件送到前我飞不了了。
Lilya: Bad is what. Broomstick's broken. Won't be flying until I get the parts to fix it.

红弩箭：但这还不是最糟的，军长，我想我们碰上了一些真正的大麻烦。
Lilya: But it gets worse. We have a situation, sir. And I think it's a big one.

军长伊万：和我到指挥室说。莎宾娜，你也一起来。
Commander Ivan: To the war room. You too, Sabina.

军长伊万：……芝诺装备的AZP-37高射炮，还有神秘术引导的近炸防空炮弹，出现在匪军手中。
Commander Ivan: So, the bandits have Zeno AZP-37s and arcane-guided VT fuse anti-aircraft guns.

军长伊万：这一切你都很有把握吗，中尉？
Commander Ivan: You swear it, Lieutenant?

红弩箭：我不会看错。我还在受训的时候，教官就是用这种炮来让我们练习规避——当然，装的是训练弹。
Lilya: Yes. We practiced how to dodge anti-aircraft shots with these kinds of guns when I was a trainee. Loaded with training ammo, of course.

斯捷尔诺娃：骑兵军近期没有丢失武器的记录，更不用说我们根本没有装备这个型号的高射炮。
Sternova: There have been no reports of missing weapons, and we're not carrying any AZPs.

将军中物资流向牢记于心的参谋长率先排除了部分可能性。
The chief of staff, keeping the entire supply chain in mind, quickly rules out several possibilities.

军长伊万：也就是说可以假定AZP-37是从外部进入顿河流域的。进一步说，有很大可能匪军还藏有更多类似的重武器。
Commander Ivan: Then those weapons came from an outer source, and like as not, they have more of them.

斯捷尔诺娃：从外部的话……空运是绝无可能的，而从外部进入骑兵军管辖区的主要陆地与航运通道都处在监视之下。
Sternova: An outer source ... Impossible through air, and all land and water routes are under our surveillance.

斯捷尔诺娃：要说匪军熟悉环境，知道某些隐藏的小路，那骑兵军里的本地士兵也一样会知道。
Sternova: And there's no reason the locals wouldn't know about any hidden bypaths they might have used.

斯捷尔诺娃：目前看不出匪军有什么办法将大量武器和人员运送到顿河流域。
Sternova: I can't think of any way of transporting mass weaponry and personnel without drawing attention.

军长伊万：比起渠道，更重要的是供应者——除芝诺本身之外，有谁掌握芝诺装备？
Commander Ivan: Then we look to the hand that fed them. Who would hold Zeno weaponry besides Zeno itself?

斯捷尔诺娃：也许是重塑之手在其他战场缴获了我方的武器，然后把它们提供给了顿河的匪军。
Sternova: Manus Vindictae? They might've captured them on another battlefield and given them to the bandits here.

红弩箭：把一切都推给重塑之手确实是个省事的思路，不过我看这种可能性并不是很大。
Lilya: Yeah, the Manus. That would save us some brain juice. But I don't think that's likely.

红弩箭：匪军里的人类多到能让基金会心花怒放。相比合作，重塑之手应该更想把他们一起消灭。
Lilya: Do you know how many humans there are among the bandits? Any Manus would blast them all to bits before they gave them so much as a pistol.

红弩箭：另外，匪军在遭受损失之后就立刻逃跑，他们没有表现出受重塑之手控制的那种疯狂的进攻性。
Lilya: Plus, these guys ran as soon as they suffered a loss. There's no way they're under Manus Vindictae's control.

红弩箭：我们还是谈谈另外一种可能性吧——有没有可能是伊戈尔的叛军？
Lilya: There is a possibility we're ignoring here: Igor's rebels.

骑兵军将领们的表情凝固了一秒，就连烛光也突然静滞。可抛出话题的中尉却仿佛与空气中的情绪完全隔绝。
For a second, the faces of the Cavalry Corps's leaders freeze. Even the candlelight seems to stop flickering. Only Lilya seems immune to it.

红弩箭：他也有能力从非常规渠道投送人员和武器，对吧，军长？我记得你以前在伊戈尔手下干过。
Lilya: You served under Igor, didn't you, Commander? He's more than capable of transporting personnel and supplies in unconventional ways, right?

斯捷尔诺娃：中尉，我需要纠正一点——
Sternova: I have to correct you, Lieutenant.

军长伊万：没错，在伊戈尔手下的时候，我了解过他的神秘术。他的确有办法突破封锁投送武器和人员。
Commander Ivan: You're right. While under Igor, I saw his arcane skill in use. He could slip men and guns through stone as if it were air.

红弩箭：好消息是，伊戈尔在南极仪式之后和重塑之手闹掰了。无论是哪一种可能，我们只要面对两个麻烦中的一个。
Lilya: Well, good news is, Igor cut ties with Manus Vindictae after the ritual in Antarctica. So whether it's him or them, we only need to deal with one.

这种程度的好消息还无法驱散军长眼窝中沉积着的一片铁灰色。
News like this cannot lift the iron-gray shadows sitting beneath the commander's eyes.

军长伊万：就算假定是伊戈尔，不明朗之处还有很多。他和他所谓的狮鹫军到距离前线上千公里的别列格勒附近做什么？
Commander Ivan: If it is Igor, the questions only grow. Why bring this Gryphon Legion of his to Bereggrad, so far from the front?

军长伊万：就算这里有什么他想要的东西，他又为什么和匪军合作？——据我对他的了解，他可看不起土匪。
Commander Ivan: Even if he seeks something here, why ride with bandits? He never stomached their filth before.

军长伊万：他想要补给？可“金色饥荒”已经让顿河地区颗粒无收，还是说他就是这场饥荒的始作俑者？
Commander Ivan: Is it supplies he wants? But the Golden Famine grips the entire basin. Or is this all by his hand?

男人的追问快要逐渐演化为焦躁的絮语，他赶紧制止自己继续说下去。
His questions quickly trail off into agitated muttering. He stops himself before more can leave his lips.

军长伊万：我会把这件事告知指挥部，情报部门应该能分析出更多可靠的信息。
Commander Ivan: I'll send word to headquarters. Intelligence should reach a more solid conclusion.

军长伊万：莎宾娜，把巡逻队的人数和任务频率都提高一倍，重点关照较为隐蔽的林地地区。
Commander Ivan: Sabina, double the patrols. I want eyes on the woods at all times.

斯捷尔诺娃：遵命，军长。
Sternova: Yes, sir.

军长伊万：红弩箭中尉，骑术不是你的专长，所以，在飞行扫帚修好之前，我要求你留在营地。
Commander Ivan: Lieutenant Lilya, since horsemanship is not your expertise, you will remain at camp until your broomstick is mended. That's an order.

飞行女巫想说些什么来反驳对她骑术的否定，但还是把话咽了回去。
Lilya almost defends her riding skills but quickly swallows her words.

红弩箭：——好吧，我明白了。
Lilya: Alright, understood.

在这个钟点，很容易就能找到营地里的野战厨房——烤无酵饼的香气会引导饥饿的人穿越营帐构成的迷宫。
It's easy to find the field kitchen at this hour. The aroma of hot unleavened bread guides their rumbling stomachs through the maze of tents.

红弩箭：倒是正好赶上了饭点。
Lilya: Right in time for dinner.

她在一只硕大的汤锅前瞄到了与其他士兵站在一起的谢尔盖，他正端着碗，一边往口中塞食物一边不停说话。
She glances at Sergey, who's standing among the other soldiers around a huge soup pot. He holds his bowl, talking between heavy mouthfuls.

谢尔盖：……说时迟那时快，朋友，我仿佛是看到子弹朝我飞过来。真的，一定是我身上的护身符起作用了。
Sergey: ... In that moment, I saw the bullet coming at me! I'm telling you, my amulet worked!

谢尔盖：我赶忙一个侧身，虽然是躲过了致命伤，但子弹还是往我腿肚子里打去了。你们绝对想不到那是什么滋味……
Sergey: Gave me just enough time to dodge the hit to the chest. Still hit the leg, though. You have no idea how much it hurts.

红弩箭：我看你恢复得挺快啊，谢尔盖。
Lilya: Too bad it didn't hit your mouth.

谢尔盖：中尉，你来了——
Sergey: H-Hey, Lieutenant.

谢尔盖手中的碗一抖，不自觉地并腿立正，些许白菜汤洒在他的手指缝里。
His legs snap to attention, some cabbage soup spilling from the bowl in his quivering hand onto his fingertips.

红弩箭：刚把腿肚子里的子弹取出来，你就能自己走来捞汤喝了？
Lilya: Oh yeah, must really hurt. Still managed to drag yourself to the mess hall for some soup though, didn't you?

谢尔盖：那……那是当然，我可是钢筋铁骨。唉，说到这汤啊——
Sergey: W-Well, of course! It'll take more than a bullet to take me down. Speaking of soup—

他举起手中的碗，容器内是泡着一张饼的卷心菜汤。
He raises the bowl in his hand. Inside, a few measly scraps of cabbage float around a single soaked scrap of bread.

谢尔盖：你看看我们吃的是什么东西啊？当兵的不能就靠这些东西过活呀。
Sergey: Look at this stuff! We're soldiers, not rabbits!

红弩箭：别抱怨了，你自己不是藏了一些肉干吗？——拿出来吃了吧。
Lilya: Quit your whining. I know you've got some dried meat. Eat it.

红弩箭也从供餐处拿走一块饼，又从汤锅中舀起一碗汤。纤薄的菜叶像是一片浸湿的纱布一般沉在碗底。
Lilya grabs a piece of bread from the table and spoons herself a bowl of soup. The thin cabbage leaves sink to the bottom of the bowl like damp gauze.

和所有人的吃法一样，红弩箭也用菜汤来泡软干硬的无酵饼。
Like everyone else, she dips the dry unleavened bread into her soup to soften it.

谢尔盖掏出一些肉干交给红弩箭，自己又从身后拿出一瓶藏好的饮料。瓶中的液体清亮透明，看似无害。
Sergey hands her some dried meat, then pulls a bottle from behind his back. The liquid inside is clear—seemingly harmless.

谢尔盖：给，你也喝点。
Sergey: Here, have some, Lieutenant.

红弩箭：这还不错。
Lilya: Not bad.

谢尔盖：……所以，到底是怎么回事，土匪手里怎么会有那样厉害的玩意儿，能把你都打下来？
Sergey: So, what was it? How come the bandits have something powerful enough to shoot you down?

红弩箭：现在谁也说不准匪军是怎么搞到这些玩意儿的，也不知道他们想拿这些武器干什么。
Lilya: Don't know how, don't know why. Nobody does.

谢尔盖：这还不好猜吗？！他们当然是要去打劫村子……这可糟了，村子里留守的那点人可遭不住这种火力。
Sergey: Well, it isn't hard to guess. They're obviously going to rob the villages! Wait. This is bad. All the young and fit have gone to war. They won't be able to defend themselves.

青年哥萨克脸上的阴云来了又去，他的心很快被另一个念头占据。
For a moment, a dark cloud falls upon his face. But soon, it's lightened by another idea.

谢尔盖：我听说咱们队下午没有安排，你要不要和我一起去河边网点鱼？
Sergey: Hey, no orders this afternoon, right? Want to go fishing with me? I'm going to the river.

红弩箭：在这种时候捞鱼？你不怕会被人一枪打死吗？
Lilya: Now? You forget that bullet so quick?

谢尔盖：我知道安全的地方，再说，我随身带着护身符，子弹打不死我的。
Sergey: I know a safe place where we can fish, and I've got the amulet! There's no bullet that can kill me. Trust me.

谢尔盖：就算是在打仗，没有东西吃也不行。虽然麦子不长了，但河里一定还有不少鱼。
Sergey: You're not going to tell me you're full after that sorry excuse for a soup, are you? There may not be any crops, but I bet there are still plenty of fish in the river.

红弩箭以审视的目光查看谢尔盖据说中弹了的小腿。
Lilya checks Sergey's allegedly shot leg.

红弩箭：我记得你腿肚子不是被打坏了吗，这就能去捞鱼了？
Lilya: Weren't you just wailing about your leg a few hours ago?

谢尔盖：这、这没什么妨碍的！
Sergey: It-It's no big deal!

谢尔盖几口扒拉完最后的食物，放下碗跑远了。
He finishes the last of his food, drops the bowl, and jogs away.

红弩箭：呵，我看顶多就是被擦破了一点皮。
Lilya: "Shot in the leg." Pft. More like scratched.

干热的风袭来，被压到不满半人高的针茅草形成层叠的、沙沙作响的浪涌。
The arid wind blows the needlegrass into a sea of rustling waves.

安德烈森：咴～
Andreas: Neigh—

这里是马儿的乐园，但却会让疲于奔命的逃亡者叫苦不迭。
A horse's playground. But for a fugitive on a long run from the authorities, it's hell.

梅蕾尔：卡戎，离开大路之后，我们已经走了多远？
Merel: *sigh* Charon, how far have we gone since we left the road?

在辽阔的草原上游走，通常会陷入数小时不见人烟的困境。光靠无垠的草浪无法判断自己究竟身处何方。
On the open grassland, one might travel for hours without seeing another soul. Among the endless waves of grass, it's easy to lose your way.

卡戎：按照平时步行的速度，我们应该是往东南走了十五公里，但也许现在我们的速度要比之前更慢。
Charon: Fifteen kilometers southeast, perhaps less. Our speed is slower than usual.

卡戎：你累了吗，要不要休息一下？
Charon: Are you weary? Would you like to rest?

梅蕾尔：唉，再往前走走吧，这里怎么看都不像是能休息的地方……你觉得车夫给我们的地图可靠吗？
Merel: Um, maybe later. This doesn't seem like the best place for a break. Do you think this map is reliable? The one the cart driver gave us?

卡戎：你说的是哪一个车夫？
Charon: The cart driver?

梅蕾尔：……
Merel: ...

梅蕾尔：我还是再帮你回忆一下之前发生的事吧，这已经是第不知道多少次了，卡戎。
Merel: Alright, I'll refresh your memory one more time, or should I say, for the millionth time.

梅蕾尔：就从离开波兰之后说起，我们稀里糊涂地搭上了一辆满是捷克斯洛伐克人的火车，和他们一起往东走。
Merel: It all started after we left Poland. Somehow, we got ourselves on a train heading east—the one full of Czechoslovakians.

卡戎：是因为稀里糊涂吗？好像是他们告诉你，再往东走就不会见到黑衣的军队，然后你就吵着要上车了。
Charon: Memories of you insisting they let us aboard the train because "you can avoid the soldiers in black in the East" come to mind.

梅蕾尔：噢……这你倒记得了。总之他们让我们上车，可还没走多远，火车就被另一伙不知道是什么的人拦下来了。
Merel: Of course you'd remember that of all things. Anyway, so we got on the train, but before we could get too far, it was stopped by some group.

梅蕾尔：再之后，到处都是枪响。我们去载马的车厢把安德烈森救走，趁乱往南逃了。
Merel: A fight must've broken out, because there were gunshots everywhere. It was utter bedlam, so we grabbed Andreas from the stock car and slipped away south.

安德烈森：咴咴……
Andreas: Neigh ...

战马对那场惊心动魄的营救行动仍然心存感激。
The warhorse seems grateful for the daring rescue.

梅蕾尔：之后就是我说的那个车夫，他丢了一匹马。
Merel: That's when we met the cart driver I mentioned. He'd lost a horse.

梅蕾尔：我们和他商量了一个办法——安德烈森借他拉一天的车，而他要告诉我们往哪里走更安全。
Merel: So we made a deal: we'd lend him Andreas for the day, and he'd take us somewhere safe.

卡戎：那么，这确实是一个安全的地方，四周都很安宁。
Charon: Then he has fulfilled his promise. This is indeed a peaceful and safe place.

梅蕾尔：但我要的安全不是这种啊！——再找不到有人的地方，我们，不对，只有我会饿死在路上的。
Merel: Hardly! We're in the middle of bloody nowhere! If we can't find people soon, we'll—no, I'll—starve to death!

不用进食的亡者低下头，仿佛是在为自己考虑不周而失落。安德烈森也别过脑袋——它倒是能靠嚼草根过活。
Charon lowers his head, troubled by his failure to consider the needs of the living. Andreas also turns his head aside. He can live off the grassland alone.

梅蕾尔：别这样啊，我又不是在怪你们……算了，除了往前走也没有什么更好的办法。
Merel: Oh, n-not to blame you two. *sigh* Forget it. Guess there's nothing for it but to keep moving forwards.

她再次举起极尽潦草的手绘地图，用尽了全部的想象力，才从混乱的线条中辨认出一条河的形状。
She lifts the messy, hand-drawn map again, squinting to make out the shape of a river among its chaotic lines.

梅蕾尔：他说我们可以到渡河口村找他的侄子，就在顿河边……可到底哪条河才是顿河？
Merel: He said we could find his niece in Perevoznaya by the Don River. But which one is the Don?

梅蕾尔：假定我们的确没有走错路，再假定车夫的地图比例没有太过夸张，呃……安德烈森？
Merel: *sigh* If we're even going in the right direction, that is, or if this map is actually accurate. Um, Andreas?

安德烈森：咴咴？
Andreas: Neigh?

梅蕾尔：让我在你背上站一会儿，好吗？
Merel: Could I stand on your back for a minute?

黑马屈膝下伏，少女四肢并用爬上马背。
Andreas lowers himself, allowing the girl to clamber onto his back.

随后，人和马一同站起，梅蕾尔双腿颤抖着立在马背上。
Then, they both rise at the same time, Merel's feet trembling.

卡戎：你在做什么，梅蕾尔？你会摔下来的。
Charon: What are you doing, Merel? You could fall.

梅蕾尔：我、我没事，我——我要摔下来的时候，你、你可要接住我。
Merel: I-I'm fine. Just be ready to *grunt* catch me if I fall, alright?

梅蕾尔哆哆嗦嗦地举起从途经的一座废墟中捡来的望远镜，向她认为的东方看去。
Merel shakily detaches the telescope she picked up in some ruins from her belt and looks toward what she believes to be the east.

梅蕾尔：是在哪儿……这边什么也没有，全都是草，树林……
Merel: Where could it be? All I see is grass and trees.

梅蕾尔：另一边呢？……另一边——嗯？
Merel: Alright, other side, other side. *gasp*

梅蕾尔：卡、卡戎，我好像看到屋顶了！就在前面，你——
Merel: Ch-Charon! Charon, I see rooftops! Right ahead! You—

梅蕾尔：救命！
Merel: Wah! Help!

少女激动得手舞足蹈，如预料之中的那般失去了平衡。
She hops in excitement and, as expected, loses her balance.

12TH-03 交汇口 / Intersection

渡河口青年：你说你从马上摔下来了？——哈，没关系，这种事就连威风的阿塔曼都一定经历过。
Young Villager: You fell off your horse? Haha, I wouldn't worry. I bet even the mighty Ataman has fallen once or twice.

身穿制服的青年来到一棵高大而无果的梨树下，将一碗蒸熟的麦饭端给眼巴巴看着他的逃难少女。
The young man in uniform comes to the tall, fruitless pear tree Merel is seated under and offers her a bowl of steamed rice mixed with wheat. She gazes at him longingly.

渡河口青年：给，谢谢你们帮我叔叔拉了一天车，不过我们家没有更多东西可以吃了。
Young Villager: Here you are. Thanks again for helping my uncle with his cart. I know it's not much, but this is all we have right now.

梅蕾尔：这……
Merel: I ...

她伸出一只手，又尴尬地收了回去。
She reaches out a hand, then pulls it back awkwardly.

梅蕾尔：对不起，我不知道这里的情况这么糟。在我来的路上，还听人说这里的收成很好，粮食很多……
Merel: I'm sorry. I thought I heard you had a strong harvest this year.

渡河口青年：前几年情况还不错。虽然很多人出去打仗了，但地里的粮食没有亏待我们。
Young Villager: The past few years were good. It's true. People had to leave to fight, but the land still blessed us.

渡河口青年：不过今年冬天可真是怪了，刚播种没多久，这小麦就疯长成了这个模样。只看见田里金灿灿的一片，但就是没收成。
Young Villager: But this year has been strange. Certainly the winter. Soon after planting, the wheat grew wild. The fields are gold, yes, but there's no grain.

他嘴上抱怨着歉收的粮食，但还是把碗塞进梅蕾尔手里。
Even as he speaks of the failed crops, he still hands the bowl to Merel.

渡河口青年：你把这碗饭吃了吧，不用管我。我要到骑兵军去当兵，那里的饭管够。
Young Villager: Eat. You look starving. I've enlisted with the cavalry. There will be plenty enough food for me there.

梅蕾尔：骑兵军？
Merel: The cavalry?

渡河口青年：芝诺骑兵军。
Young Villager: The Zeno Cavalry.

梅蕾尔：——？！
Merel: ...?!

饥肠辘辘的逃兵把一声“芝诺”的惊呼憋进了肚子，埋下头开始吃麦饭。
Merel forces her cry of "Zeno" down, lowers her head, and begins to eat.

青年转向一直躲在树后阴影中的影子。
The young man turns toward the shadow that has been hiding behind the tree.

渡河口青年：你真的不用吃东西吗？
Young Villager: Are you sure you wouldn't like any food?

卡戎：我不用，感谢你愿意分享仅剩不多的食物，我能为你做些什么，来交换这份好意？
Charon: I need no sustenance. Thank you for sharing the little food you have left. How may this kindness be repaid?

渡河口青年：不必，我马上就和村里的新兵一起走了，我家也没有活可以干。
Young Villager: Ah, no need. I'll be leaving soon, and there's no work to do right now.

渡河口青年：你的马倒是漂亮得很，我希望也有一匹这么好的马……别误会，不是问你们要这匹马的意思。
Young Villager: You have a beautiful horse. Wish I could have one as lovely as him. Oh, don't get me wrong. I'm not asking for him.

芝诺征兵官：——阿列克谢。
Zeno Conscription Officer: Alexei.

充满长官威严的声音在不远处叫住了新兵。
A commanding voice stops the new recruit mid-sentence.

芝诺征兵官：你还在这里闲逛什么？我们马上要出发了，你又和什么人在说话？
Zeno Conscription Officer: What are you dawdling for? The team is leaving. Who are you talking to?

渡河口青年：只是两个难民，长官。
Young Villager: Just two refugees, sir.

征兵官凑近来观察，他的目光在身披白布的怪异流亡者身上停留了许久。
The conscription officer steps forward, his eyes lingering on the strange man covered in white cloth.

芝诺征兵官：难民？从哪儿来的？
Zeno Conscription Officer: Refugees? From where?

梅蕾尔：我是从……波兰过来的，本来想在那里找个……朋友，但是那里也还在打仗，朋友也找不到……
Merel: F-From Poland. I was looking for a friend there, but because of the war, I couldn't find ... um ...

她猛烈地眨着眼，为蹩脚的谎言而心虚。
She stammers, blinking wildly over her clumsy lie.

所幸，心不在焉的征兵官没有看出她的窘迫。
Fortunately, the officer is too distracted to notice her embarrassment.

芝诺征兵官：你们都是神秘学家？——如果有一技之长的话，可以加入芝诺骑兵军，包管你们有吃有住。
Zeno Conscription Officer: Arcanists, aren't you? We could use your talents in the Zeno Cavalry. Room, board, and meals provided.

卡戎：不用在乎我，先生，我只是一个没有目的的游荡者，也不想加入任何一支军队。
Charon: Apologies, sir. I am only a wanderer. There is no desire to join any party within me.

梅蕾尔：我、我没什么擅长的，军官先生。我连枪都没用过。
Merel: A-And I-I don't have any talents at all, officer. Sir, I can't even hold a gun.

第二个试图把自己从乱世中摘出去的谎言。征兵官的注意力依旧不在她的身上。
Another lie erupts from her—another bid to escape desperate times. But the conscription officer takes no interest.

芝诺征兵官：那你们最好快点离开。现在草原上到处都是土匪，真不知道你们怎么会往这里跑。
Zeno Conscription Officer: Then you'd better leave soon. This place is crawling with bandits.

梅蕾尔：土匪？
Merel: Bandits?

芝诺征兵官：是啊，你们路上都没遇到过吗？呵，算你们命大，当然，也有骑兵军清剿得当的功劳。
Zeno Conscription Officer: Brigands, raiders, ruffians. You didn't bump into any on your way here? Lucky dogs. Though you can thank the Cavalry Corps for that.

芝诺征兵官：不过最近的情况又要变糟了，匪军不知道从哪里搞来了新武器，也许又要和他们打一场大仗。
Zeno Conscription Officer: But even with our efforts, the situation's been getting worse. Somehow, they've got new weapons. We might be facing a serious battle.

梅蕾尔：怎么到了这里还在……打仗……
Merel: Even all this way away, there's still fighting?

芝诺征兵官：天下没有太平的地方。
芝诺需要新鲜的血液，这样我们才能打败敌人，迎来和平。
Zeno Conscription Officer: The flames of conflict burn everywhere. This is why I'm asking you to join us. Zeno needs new blood if we're to ever know peace.

芝诺征兵官：要是改了主意，想为骑兵军服务，就沿着顿河向下游走，过了城就能看见我们的营地。
Zeno Conscription Officer: If you change your mind, come to our camp. It's downstream of the Don, past the city.

征兵官背过身去，此时，又有十几个新入伍的哥萨克聚集在他身后，三五成群地与熟悉的人站在一起。
The conscription officer turns around. Just then, a dozen newly enlisted Cossacks gather behind him, standing in the little groups of those they know.

他们互相显摆着新制服，攀比着谁家的马照顾得更好，谁家的马刀来历更传奇。
They show off their new uniforms, competing over who takes better care of his horse and whose shashka has the most legendary history.

芝诺征兵官：好了，别像小鸡仔一样围成一团，地上有米给你们啄吗？全体都有，成行军纵队——
Zeno Conscription Officer: Quit milling around like chickens and form rank—

芝诺骑兵：——长官！
Zeno Cavalryman: Sir!

村外，一名全副武装的骑兵狂奔而来，一头扎进了惊慌失措的新兵队列中。
A fully armed cavalryman gallops in from outside the village, plunging himself between the panicking ranks of recruits.

他半截身子浸在发黑的血污中，胯下的战马因长途奔跑而不断喷打鼻息。
Half of his body is smeared dark with blood, the horse beneath him snorting heavily.

芝诺骑兵：匪军——一支匪军的骑兵队正在来渡河口村的路上，估计有一个排。我们怎么办？
Zeno Cavalryman: Bandit cavalry incoming. The size of a platoon! What do we do?

芝诺征兵官：你还能骑马吗？
Zeno Conscription Officer: Can you still ride?

芝诺骑兵：撑得住。
Zeno Cavalryman: Yes, sir!

芝诺征兵官：那你快马赶回塞契通报，我和其他人留在村内拦住匪军。
Zeno Conscription Officer: Then hurry to the sich and report this. The rest of you form a blockade. Do not allow the bandits to enter the village.

芝诺骑兵：是！
Zeno Cavalryman: Sir, yes, sir!

征兵官环视一圈，入伍不足半小时的年轻人们神色慌张，将他这个“长官”视作唯一的救世主。
The conscription officer scans the area. The unsettled young cavalrymen, enlisted less than half an hour ago, look to him as if he is their only savior.

芝诺征兵官：新兵，不要逃跑，这只会让你们把后背暴露给敌人！
——拿起你们的枪，掩护你们的家人撤离！
Zeno Conscription Officer: Rookies, there is no escape! Turn your back to the enemy, and they will take the opportunity! Take up your weapons! Protect your families!

惊慌失措的新兵们得到指令，不再像年幼的草原兔那样挤成一团，纷纷生疏地扛起了武器。
The boys shake off their scared looks, leaving their huddled groups and shouldering their weapons, albeit a little clumsily.

梅蕾尔：什么……匪军？！
Merel: What? Bandits?

大脑一片空白，梅蕾尔感觉到卡戎把缰绳递到自己手上。
As Merel's mind goes blank, she feels Charon press the reins into her hands.

卡戎：让安德烈森带你离开这里，梅蕾尔。
Charon: Let Andreas take you. Leave here, Merel.

梅蕾尔：可是你怎么办？
Merel: What? What about you?

卡戎：你说过，遇见危险就会自己逃跑。请不要浪费时间。
Charon: "I'll just run off when danger comes." That is what you said. Do not waste any more time.

梅蕾尔：但是我都不知道应该往哪里走——
Merel: I don't even know where to—

卡戎：往下游去，梅蕾尔，就像军官说的，一路沿着河跑，快。
Charon: Downstream of the Don River, like the officer said. Now go.

梅蕾尔：我、我快掉下去了，安德烈森！
Merel: Andreas! I-I'm slipping!!

安德烈森：咴——！
Andreas: Neigh—!

少女四肢并用，紧紧扒在尽全力奔跑的黑马背上，甚至无法抽出一只手拿出武器还击。
She clings to the horse with all her might as he charges at full speed. She can't even spare a hand to draw her weapon and fight back.

？？？：别让她跑了！——开枪！
???: Don't let her get away! Fire!

一连串劈啪作响的子弹声在她耳旁炸开。
A series of crackling gunshots blasts past her on all sides.

梅蕾尔：不——不要啊！安德烈森，我抓得住！快跑！
Merel: Ah! Run, Andreas, run! I'll hold on. Go!

安德烈森：咴！
Andreas: Neigh!

？？？：她那马过不去顿河！散开，我们围住她。
???: She can't cross the Don! Spread out and surround her!

梅蕾尔：什么？什么河？
Merel: What? The-The Don?

她鼓起勇气，睁开眼，才发现一条宽阔的河流横亘在逃亡的路上。
She gathers her courage and opens her eyes, only to find a broad river blocking her escape.

梅蕾尔：完、完蛋了！
Merel: Oh. Oh no!

她的脑子一片空白，安德烈森也不得不在汹涌的河水前放慢了脚步。
Her mind goes blank again. Andreas can only slow down before the rushing water.

？？？：她慢下来了，你们别开枪，小心伤到马。
???: She's slowing down. Don't shoot. You might hit that beauty she's riding.

？？？：我把人打下来，这匹马就归我。
???: I'll take her out, and I'll get the horse.

梅蕾尔：——啊！
Merel: Aaargh!

她的手臂仿佛被一只巨锤狠狠锤击，马背上的少女失去了平衡，从一侧摔了下去。
It's like a hammer has struck her arm. She loses her balance and falls to one side.

黑暗而冰冷的河水在一瞬间将她吞没，随后，手臂上的枪伤爆发出撕心裂肺的疼痛感。
Dark, freezing water swallows her in an instant, followed by the piercing pain of a bullet.

梅蕾尔：不……不要——唔——唔咕咕咕咕……
Merel: No. Don't ... *gulp*

她昏迷过去。
The shimmering light through the water above turns dark.

斯捷尔诺娃：——军长。
Sternova: Commander.

一声通报之后，参谋长进入营帐。
The chief of staff enters the tent.

军长伊万：说。
Commander Ivan: Speak.

军长的声音有些干哑，但斯捷尔诺娃还是一口气吐出她准备好的汇报内容。
The commander's voice is hoarse, yet Sternova delivers her report without pause.

斯捷尔诺娃：渡河口村已经失陷了，我们不知道战斗之后的情况，但一定不会乐观。难民说在身后看见了房屋燃烧的浓烟。
Sternova: Perevoznaya is lost. We don't know the details of the situation, but it's surely devastating. The refugees said they saw a huge smoke cloud coming from the village.

斯捷尔诺娃：至少有另外三个定居点遭到匪军的袭击，据幸存者说，敌人拥有许多他们没有见过的武器。
Sternova: At least three settlements have been attacked. The survivors say the weapons employed were unconventional.

军长伊万：……
Commander Ivan: ...

斯捷尔诺娃：遇袭的村庄都在上游，别列格勒城东北。我认为应当快速将骑兵军主力部署到以下位置，好抢占有利地形。
Sternova: The villages struck are all upstream from here, northeast of Bereggrad. I suggest we quickly position the main force here, here, and here to seize advantageous terrain.

参谋长在桌面的军用地图上指出几个早已构思好的地点，却发现骑兵军指挥官的目光无法在地图上集中。
The chief of staff points out the positions on the military map spread across the table, only to find the commander's focus is elsewhere.

那沉重的空气还是不可阻挡地将斯捷尔诺娃包裹，打断了她进一步的战术构想。
The heavy air closes in around Sternova. She falters.

斯捷尔诺娃：军长？
Sternova: Sir?

军长伊万：芝诺指挥部给我下过命令了，莎宾娜。
Commander Ivan: Headquarters has spoken.

斯捷尔诺娃：那他们怎么说？——指挥部不至于干涉骑兵军怎么执行具体战术吧？
Sternova: What did they say? They wouldn't interfere with the Cavalry Corps's tactics, would they?

军长伊万：骑兵军要在两周内从顿河撤离，下个月，我们就会在匈牙利与重塑之手交战。
Commander Ivan: We withdraw from the Don in two weeks. We will engage Manus Vindictae in Hungary next month.

军人的本能使她无法第一时间理解这则命令。
Her military instincts prevent her from making sense of this order.

斯捷尔诺娃：我……没听懂，军长。指挥部知道现在的情况吗？有一支匪军在外烧杀抢掠，骑兵军却要在两周内离开？
Sternova: I ... I don't understand, sir. Bandits are killing and robbing civilians in higher numbers than ever, and we've just been told to leave? Are you certain headquarters is fully aware of the situation?

军长伊万：他们知道得比我们更多。情报部门的结论是，我们有很大概率遇上了伊戈尔本人的军队。
Commander Ivan: They are more aware than any of us. Intelligence gave their conclusion. We've stumbled upon Igor's army.

斯捷尔诺娃：那他们应该派援军来，和骑兵军一起消灭叛军，而不是让我们逃跑。
Sternova: Then they should send reinforcements, end the rebels once and for all, not ask us to run away with our tails between our legs!

军长伊万：现在全世界的重塑之手军队都在往基金会总部进军，前线的压力非常大，我们不会得到任何援军。
Commander Ivan: There are no reinforcements. Manus Vindictae's army marches on the Foundation headquarters as we speak. The front is under immense pressure.

军长伊万：何况骑兵军原本的任务，就是在顿河地区招募到足够多的新兵之后，去缓解总部防线的压力。
Commander Ivan: Don't forget that our mission here was to recruit new blood to bolster headquarters defenses.

军长伊万：至于伊戈尔——他在南极行动之后就脱离了重塑之手，双方似乎是完成了什么交易，但具体细节未知。
Commander Ivan: As for Igor—he cut ties with Manus Vindictae after Antarctica. They say some kind of bargain was struck, though the terms remain unknown.

军长伊万：自那之后，叛军就没有与基金会和芝诺发生过冲突，而联合委员会的高层希望保持这种互相中立的状态。
Commander Ivan: Since then, the rebels have crossed no blades with either the Foundation or Zeno. The Joint Committee wants to keep it that way.

斯捷尔诺娃：也就是说，如果我们面对的真的是伊戈尔，反而要避免和他起冲突？
Sternova: So, they want us to leave so we won't fight Igor?

军长伊万：没错。
Commander Ivan: Correct.

斯捷尔诺娃：鬼扯！基金会——尤其是“鹰派”的人——拿叛军的事来贬低芝诺，另一边又想和伊戈尔拉近关系？
Sternova: To hell! All this time, the Foundation, especially those Hawks, has been belittling Zeno for Igor's betrayal, yet here they are, still trying to stay in his good graces?!

军长伊万：对政治家来说，这两件事并不矛盾。
Commander Ivan: Politicians, Sabina. For them, the two don't clash.

斯捷尔诺娃：我烦透这一切了，这些——这些该死的政客，什么狗屁基金会、什么鸟派别、伊里内伊，还有——
Sternova: Politicians, ha! I'm sick to death of the conniving bastards! To hell with the Foundation, to hell with those ridiculous bird parties, to hell with Irinei, and to hell with—

军长伊万：——莎宾娜。
Commander Ivan: Sabina.

名字的发音中带上了警告的意味，但这并没有阻止斯捷尔诺娃说出接下来的话。
The hint of warning in his tone fails to stop her.

斯捷尔诺娃：——还有红弩箭，名义上是提供空中支援，但我看得出派她来是带着怎样的目的。
Sternova: —Their lapdog, Lilya! "Air support"? Don't make me laugh. I know why they sent her!

斯捷尔诺娃：有芝诺和基金会的双重编制，有基金会的大人物给她做担保，档案里还写着“经调查后可确保忠诚可靠”。
Sternova: She's both Zeno and Foundation. Her file says "loyalty guaranteed after investigation."

斯捷尔诺娃：所以她被派来监视你——监视我们所有人——的一举一动，生怕顿河变成又一个“圣保罗”。
Sternova: She's a surveillant! A Foundation babysitter monitoring you, me, everyone, so the Don doesn't become the next São Paulo!

斯捷尔诺娃：我们不应该受到这样的侮辱，芝诺也不应该向所谓的“鹰派”委员低头。
Sternova: It's an insult! A humiliation! Zeno should never have to yield to those so-called Hawks!

军长伊万：——斯捷尔诺娃上校，难道政治也让你头脑发热了吗？！
Commander Ivan: Colonel Sabina Sternova! Have you lost your senses?

温和的警告无效，军长出口的话已转变为训斥。
His gentle warning proving ineffective, the commander turns to harsh reprimand.

斯捷尔诺娃：……
Sternova: ...

军长伊万：你对红弩箭的指控是有证据支持，还是只是因为她有基金会的身份？
Commander Ivan: Do you accuse Lieutenant Lilya based on proof? Or only because of her ties to the Foundation?

斯捷尔诺娃：我……
Sternova: I ...

军长的嘴唇紧紧抿在一起，艰难蠕动着，仿佛是在咀嚼一块铁片。
The commander purses his lips, his jaw grinding as if he were chewing on a piece of steel.

他俯身，从一堆文件中抽出一张已经揉皱了的信纸，递过桌面。斯捷尔诺娃疑惑地皱着眉，接了过去。
He bends down, draws out a crumpled letter, and passes it across the table. Sternova takes it, her brows knitting together.

斯捷尔诺娃：“伊万：伊里内伊的人做到了，芝诺的结局无可避免。我附信来只是想以私人身份给予你一些提醒。”
Sternova: "Ivan, Irinei's people have done it. Zeno's fate is inevitable. I write this letter only as a reminder from one friend to another."

斯捷尔诺娃：“联合委员会正在加紧对芝诺军队的控制，每位外派的将领身边，都必须要有一位基金会信得过的联络人。”
Sternova: "The Joint Committee is tightening its control over Zeno's military operations. Every commander stationed outside of HQ must be accompanied by a liaison entrusted by the Foundation."

斯捷尔诺娃：“你曾是伊戈尔最信赖的下属，原本光凭这一条，‘鹰派’就要在庭审上把你折磨得够呛。”
Sternova: "You were once Igor's most trusted subordinate. For that reason alone, the Hawks were planning to torture you during the trial."

斯捷尔诺娃：“我能做的，就是在委员会面前担保你的忠诚，并且派给你一个最不适合担当联络员的飞行女巫。”
Sternova: "All I could do was assure the Committee of your loyalty and assign the least capable liaison to you—the flying witch."

斯捷尔诺娃：“你一定听过她的名字和事迹。她对政治毫无兴趣，不会乱打报告，甚至在某些行事风格上还与你相似。”
Sternova: "I'm sure you've heard this title before. She has no interest in politics, never writes reports unless forced to, and, in many ways, shares your temperament."

斯捷尔诺娃：“前提是你不要真的干出什么蠢事，你要严格执行每一条命令——芝诺的命令，现在就是基金会的命令。”
Sternova: "That said, ensure you strictly follow every order, both from Zeno and the Foundation. We must be smart."

斯捷尔诺娃：“你担负的责任比你想的还要多，不要让我们所有人都难堪。——索姆。”
Sternova: "The burden on you is much heavier than you realize. Do not embarrass us. Somme."

信纸被放下。室内一时间没了声音。
The letter is set down. Silence falls.

几次心跳后，一阵含混不清的呐喊穿过军用帆布透入室内——那是营地里的哥萨克们正在与一匹烈马搏斗。
After a few heartbeats, muffled shouts carry through the canvas. The Cossacks are struggling with a fierce horse.

斯捷尔诺娃：我会……安排撤出顿河的准备工作，如果这是你的决定。
Sternova: I ... I'll begin preparations for the withdrawal, if that is your order.

疲惫不堪的军长长叹一口气。
The commander lets out a long, weary sigh.

军长伊万：命令的详细要求是，所有骑兵军士兵在别列格勒城内集结，依托城市固守，在撤离前的两周内保护城市安全。
Commander Ivan: *sigh* Orders are to assemble all cavalrymen in Bereggrad. We hold the city for two weeks. Then, we withdraw.

斯捷尔诺娃：既然我们要走了，保护别列格勒又是为了什么？
Sternova: We're withdrawing anyway. Why risk the two weeks?

军长伊万：为了司辰。
Commander Ivan: For the safety of the Timekeeper.

斯捷尔诺娃：司辰？
Sternova: The Timekeeper?

Z：我们已经和骑兵军取得联系。红弩箭中尉的通讯设备在战斗中被损坏，但是她本人安全回到了驻地。
Z: We've contacted the Cavalry Corps in the Don River basin. Lieutenant Lilya's communication device was damaged during the battle, but she has returned to her post safely.

维尔汀：那太好了。
Vertin: That's a relief.

Z：但根据她的汇报，伊戈尔的叛军出现在东线应该是确有其事。
Z: However, according to her report, it's all but confirmed that Igor's rebels have shown up at the Eastern Front.

Z：维尔汀，关于前往别列格勒的计划，是否有待商榷？那里很可能将爆发一场新的战争。
Z: Vertin, is it possible to delay your plans to travel to Bereggrad? A conflict is highly likely to break out there.

没有必要在少数值得信赖的人面前隐藏情报。
There's no need to hide intel from the trusted few.

维尔汀：刻雷乌斯私下给了我一份有关兀尔德的情报，就在别列格勒城中。我不清楚这有多可靠。
Vertin: Creius privately conveyed to me a message about Urd. It said there's some information to be gleaned about her in Bereggrad. I'm not sure how dependable it is.

维尔汀：但事关兀尔德的行踪，我想我必须去一趟。
Vertin: But since it concerns Urd's whereabouts, I have no choice but to go.

Z：很高兴你愿意向我透露情报来源，可是……刻雷乌斯？
Z: I appreciate you sharing the source of your information with me, but, Creius?

Z女士罕见地露出了惊讶的神情。
Madam Z betrays a rare look of surprise.

Z：南极行动前，他只是基金会军事部的传令官，执行着基金会与芝诺行动部队间的沟通与调度工作。
Z: Before the Antarctic Operation, he was just a liaison of the Foundation's military department, responsible for communication and coordination between the Foundation and the Zeno Task Force.

Z：虽然在本次“暴雨”时代中得到了重用，可……
Z: He got promoted after we entered this era, but ...

Z：在基金会内部，兀尔德的一切信息都被严格控制，只能在小部分必要人员间传阅。
Z: All information held by the Foundation concerning Urd is strictly controlled, only accessible to the authorized few.

Z：以刻雷乌斯的职位来说，他并不在此列。
Z: And he's not one of them.

Z：更可能的是，“鹰派”希望利用你去取得他们无法合规获得的情报，刻雷乌斯则充当他们避险的中介。
Z: More likely than not, this information came directly from the Hawks. They're using you to obtain information they can't legally acquire themselves, and Creius is their intermediary.

维尔汀：从第八次“暴雨”以来，寻找兀尔德一直就是我的主要任务。
Vertin: Locating Urd has been my primary mission since the eighth "Storm."

维尔汀：如果这一切对基金会的行动是有利的呢？
Vertin: A mission that may prove useful to the Foundation, don't you think?

Z：如果这份情报真的能让你找到兀尔德的下落，那么按常理来说，是的，它对所有人都是一个好消息。
Z: If this information really does help you find Urd, then yes, it would be good news for everyone, no matter their affiliation.

Z：但你或许会因此欠下一份“人情”。在未来的某个时刻，“鹰派”会以此胁迫你站在他们那边。
Z: But in the Hawks' eyes, you'd owe them one. They might hold this over you if and when the time comes for you to choose a side.

Z：加之司辰小队的权责扩大也是在“鹰派”主导下实现的，那么，外人难免会以此判断你作为司辰的立场。
Z: What's more, the expansion of Team Timekeeper was spearheaded by the Hawks. It's only natural that people are starting to doubt the Timekeeper's neutrality.

Z女士的嗓音变得柔和而循循善诱，她真切地希望眼前人不会被困于政治的漩涡。
Madam Z's voice is gentle but persuasive. She sincerely hopes the young lady before her will not be drawn into the whirlpool of politics.

Z：我知道你没有任何政治倾向，可是，“鹰派”正在用各种手段塑造你在与他们合作的印象。
Z: I know you have no political inclinations, but the Hawks are creating an image that you're working with them.

Z：我说这些不是想阻拦你的行动，维尔汀，只是想提醒你基金会内部正在发生的事。
Z: I'm not saying this to stop you, Vertin. I simply want to keep you abreast of what's happening inside the Foundation.

维尔汀：……谢谢，Z女士，我已经做好了面对这些的准备。
Vertin: Thank you, Madam Z. I'm ready for whatever lies ahead.

维尔汀：我申请前往别列格勒。
Vertin: Please accept my official application to travel to Bereggrad.

只有亲身踏入洪流，才能看清水底的秘密。
Only by stepping into the flood can one uncover the secrets hidden beneath the water.

Z：我明白了。
Z: I see.

Z：索姆将军接受了联合委员会的劝诫，命令骑兵军优先保护城市。在一段时间内，别列格勒应该是安全的。
Z: After the Joint Committee's admonition, Admiral Somme ordered the Cavalry Corps to prioritize the safety of the city. Bereggrad should be safe for a time.

维尔汀：联合委员会现在对伊戈尔是什么态度？
Vertin: What's the Committee's attitude towards Igor now?

Z：伊戈尔的确是我们的敌人，但从西线的战报来看，他目前没有与重塑之手联合行动。
Z: Igor is the enemy. However, reports from the Western Front state he's no longer working with the Manus.

Z：伊戈尔的动机现在正在重新评判中，但联合委员会希望减少树敌——我们与芝诺间的关系，自真正的战争开始后就变得有些岌岌可危。
Z: We're currently re-evaluating Igor's motivations. That said, the Committee does hope to avoid making enemies. Our relationship with Zeno has become somewhat fragile since the real war began.

Z：我会批准你的这次外勤。
Z: Permission granted, Timekeeper.

Z：去收拾行囊吧，我会让莎朗把必要的文书送给十四行诗。
Z: Pack your bags. I'll have Sharon deliver the paperwork to Sonetto.

维尔汀：谢谢，我会尽量在战争爆发之前回来。
Vertin: Thank you, Madam Z. I'll do my best to return before the war breaks out.

转身走出几步后，身后传来一声轻轻的叹息。
As she turns, a soft sigh comes from behind her.

Z：你向来有自己的想法，维尔汀。我希望你能保持着这样的自我，它在这个时代尤其珍贵。
Z: *sigh* You always follow your own judgment, Vertin. A precious quality in this era. I hope it never changes.

12TH-04 寂静所笼罩的 / Beneath the Silence

谢尔盖：嘿，我捞着东西了！快过来帮把手，萨沙！
Sergey: Hey! I got something! Sasha, come give me a hand!

在距离营地不远的河边，出来为连队饮马的谢尔盖仍在坚持不懈地捞鱼——草原上酝酿的危险还没有吓退他。
Not far from the camp, Sergey has been watering the horses while he fishes, undeterred by the danger brewing across the steppe.

去年没能偷到手的渔网，在离乡时还是出现在了谢尔盖的行囊里，老索莫夫亲手装进去的。
The fishnet he failed to steal last year ended up in his pack before he left home. Old Somov put it there himself.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：我抓住了——该死的，这网真沉。
Zeno Cavalryman I: Got it! Dear Lord, this is heavy!

谢尔盖：这证明我们捞到真正的大东西了，快，使点劲啊，萨沙！
Sergey: Must be a big one. Come on, Sasha, put your back into it.

两个在河畔长大的青年用尽全身的力气，才刚刚足够将激流中的渔网缓缓拖向岸边。
The two young men, children of this very river, use all their strength to drag the fishnet to the riverbank.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：谢尔盖，你见过力气这么大的鱼吗？
Zeno Cavalryman I: Have you ever caught a fish this big before?

谢尔盖：从来没有，地里的麦子不长了，鱼倒是在疯长。
Sergey: Never! The fish done all the growing this year instead of the crops?

谢尔盖：就差一点，别废话了，你抓好网的另一头，听我的——一，二，三！
Sergey: Just a bit further. Grab tight. On my mark. One! Two! Three!

捕鱼者向后栽倒，而渔网里的重物也终于被拖上了岸。
They stumble back as they finally haul the net ashore.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：快去看看，这到底是什么东西——我打赌，我爷爷这辈子都没见过这种鱼。
Zeno Cavalryman I: Go check it out. I dare say even my grandpa has never seen fish so big.

谢尔盖首先跑到网边，手法熟练地解开纠缠的网绳。
Sergey runs to the net and untangles the cords like an expert.

？？？：咳……
???: *cough*

怎么听这都不像是鱼类能发出来的声音。
That's not a sound a fish would make.

谢尔盖：啊？这是，这——
Sergey: Huh? Thi-This is—

？？？：咳——咳！
???: *cough*

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：到底是什么鱼啊，谢尔盖？
Zeno Cavalryman I: What kind of fish is it, Sergey?

伙伴还在远处，正揣着巨大的好奇心往谢尔盖身边赶来。
Sasha hurries over to join him.

谢尔盖：我的老天爷，萨沙，这、这是一个人？！
Sergey: I'll be damned! Sasha! It's a person?

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：一个人？你疯了吧！
Zeno Cavalryman I: A person? Have you lost your mind?

？？？：咳、咳咳！救……救命……
???: *cough* Help. Help me.

谢尔盖：快来，该死的，这真的是一个人！她还活着，快把她抬到营地里去！
Sergey: Damn it! Hurry up, will you? It's a living person! We have to take her to camp!

梅蕾尔：嗯……？
Merel: Hmm?

她听见马匹的鸣叫，不过不是一匹，而是数十匹马在同时出声，而且听起来离她十分遥远。
The sound of dozens of horses neighing at once echoes from somewhere far away.

梅蕾尔：……安德烈森……卡戎？——这是，咳咳，这是哪里？
Merel: Andreas? Charon? Where *cough* where am I?

温暖干燥的气流吹向她的面颊，她听见柳木条燃烧的噼啪声。
Warm, dry air sweeps across her cheeks. She hears the crackle of burning willow sticks.

谢尔盖：醒了？站起来试试。
Sergey: You're awake? Try getting to your feet.

梅蕾尔：呕……我的头好晕，站不起来。
Merel: Ergh. My head's spinning. I can hardly ...

谢尔盖：忍住，别倒下，尽量走两步，这对溺水的人很有用，相信我。
Sergey: Whoa, whoa, easy now. Just try and take a few steps. It'll help, trust me.

梅蕾尔完全不知道自己是怎么站起来的，她只记得自己摇摇晃晃、不明不白地站直了身子。
Merel doesn't know how she gets to her feet. All she remembers is swaying as she somehow pulled herself upright.

梅蕾尔：我……这是……这是哪里？
Merel: I ... What is this place?

谢尔盖：芝诺骑兵军营地。放心，你很安全。
Sergey: Relax. You're in the Zeno Cavalry Corps camp. It's safe here.

梅蕾尔：芝……芝诺？不是吧……
Merel: Z-Zeno? Oh, you've got to be kidding.

这个名字就像一个熟悉的杀手，似乎要追杀她到世界的尽头。
That name is like a hell-bent killer pursuing her to the ends of the earth.

谢尔盖没有意识到落难少女语气中不自然的惊恐。对他来说，她多半只是吓坏了。
Sergey doesn't notice the unusual panic that grips her. To him, she's simply a frightened lost girl.

梅蕾尔四下张望，看见一位着装明显不同的士兵向她走来。
Merel looks around and sees a soldier in a different uniform walking toward her.

红弩箭：你把什么人带来了，谢尔盖？
Lilya: Sergey, I heard you found a girl.

梅蕾尔：这……这不是……
Merel: No. It can't be ...

谢尔盖：从河里捞上来的，中尉，她刚醒。
Sergey: We fished her out of the river, Lieutenant. She just woke up.

红弩箭：喔？你怎么知道不是叛军的探子？——她看起来可不像本地人啊。
Lilya: And you just brought her straight into camp? She's obviously not a local. What if she's a rebel spy, huh?

谢尔盖：是不像本地人，但这样子也不像匪军的人吧。
Sergey: Sure, she's not a local, but she doesn't seem like a bandit either.

红弩箭走近梅蕾尔，盯着她看了好一阵。
Lilya steps closer and stares at her for a long while.

红弩箭：……也有道理。你叫什么名字？
Lilya: Hm. Fair enough. What's your name?

梅蕾尔：我——
Merel: I—

一个刚编好的假名字被她吓得咽了回去。在红弩箭中尉的质问下，少女失去了撒谎的勇气。
She falters before she can say the false name she created. Under Lieutenant Lilya's piercing gaze, the girl loses the courage to lie.

梅蕾尔：梅……梅蕾尔。
Merel: M-Merel.

红弩箭：梅蕾尔？好吧，听起来确实不是本地人。你是怎么掉水里的？
Lilya: Merel? Not from around here, then. How'd you end up in the water?

梅蕾尔：我是逃难到这儿来的，呃……然后，就是……在河边碰到了也许是土匪之类的人。
Merel: I, uh, I came seeking refuge near the river, and then, I ... I was chased by some people—bandits or something.

梅蕾尔：我开始跑，但是不小心从马背上跌下来，摔进了河里。
Merel: I tried to escape, but I fell off my horse and into the river.

红弩箭无可奈何地摇头，为少女的不幸而遗憾。她转向谢尔盖。
Hearing her tale of misfortune, Lilya shakes her head helplessly and turns to Sergey.

红弩箭：等她恢复好之后就送她到安全的地方去。军长下令了，明天一早拔营进城，中途在红柳树村驻扎一日。
Lilya: Send her somewhere safe after she recovers. We'll decamp tomorrow morning, station in Tamarovka for a day, and then head to the city. Commander's orders.

谢尔盖：真的？那就是我家呀，我要住自己的房子去，看看姑父和姑母。
Sergey: Really? That's my home! I can visit my aunt and uncle! I can sleep in my own bed for a night!

红弩箭：你得向军长请假才行——对了，梅蕾尔，我去给你拿些吃的，基金会送来的肉罐头还剩了些，你刚从水里出来，可不能再喝白菜汤了。
Lilya: You'll have to apply for leave to do that. You eaten anything, Merel? We still got some canned meat from the Foundation.

梅蕾尔：肉罐头……
Merel: Canned meat ...

“基金会”一词带来的压迫感被“肉罐头”的诱惑所取代。饥肠辘辘的少女咽下一口唾沫。
The temptation of canned meat outweighs all fear of the Foundation. She swallows her saliva.

中尉离开后，谢尔盖照常开始抱怨起来。
After the lieutenant leaves, Sergey returns to his usual complaining.

谢尔盖：可惜啊，今天没捞着什么鱼，光把你捞上来了。
Sergey: Too bad I only caught you today, huh?

梅蕾尔：那……对、对不起？
Merel: Um, s-sorry?

谢尔盖：别担心，以后还有机会捞鱼，总不至于再捞上个人来。对了，到了红柳树村，你也可以直接住进我姑父的家。
Sergey: Don't worry. It's not every day you fish a person out of the river, hahaha. Oh, by the way, you can stay at my uncle's when we arrive in Tamarovka if you like.

谢尔盖：不是什么好房子，但总比住在帐篷里舒服。
Sergey: It's no Winter Palace, but it's better than a tent, that's for sure.

梅蕾尔：你和你姑父一起生活？
Merel: You live with your uncle?

谢尔盖：是啊，我老爹四年前死在前线了，妈妈在前年冬天也病死了，好在姑姑一家人好，收留了我。
Sergey: Yeah. Father died at the front four years ago, and my mother was sick—lost her two years later. My aunt and uncle took me in.

谢尔盖：当然，我们得替他们家干农活，但这对我来说不算什么问题。
Sergey: I do have to do farm work to earn my keep, but that's no big deal.

谢尔盖：你是从哪儿来的？——你说你是逃难的，你的家人现在在哪里？
Sergey: How about you? Where are you from? You said you're a refugee. Where's your family now?

梅蕾尔：我……我……
Merel: I ... I ...

少女双目失神地盯着眼前的空地。
The girl stares at the empty ground before her.

梅蕾尔：我没有家人。
Merel: I don't have a family.

一向不正经的谢尔盖也收起了笑意，他不禁回想起母亲在咳嗽声中死去的那个冬天。
Even the ever-slippery Sergey loses his smile. He can't help but think of that winter when his mother lay dying.

梅蕾尔：一个，嗯……孤儿学校收留了我，之后我就在学校里长大……
Merel: An, um, orphanage took me in. I grew up there.

梅蕾尔：骑兵军里有很多本地人吗，像你一样？
Merel: Are there many locals in the cavalry? Like you?

谢尔盖：没错，像我一样当兵的大部分都是本地人。芝诺刚到这里来的时候只有千来号人，还算不上什么骑兵军呢。
Sergey: Yeah, most of us actually. Back when Zeno first got here, there were only a thousand people. The Cavalry Corps didn't even exist.

谢尔盖：后来顿河开始闹饥荒，地里连土豆都长不出来了。但骑兵军给吃给住，也不乱来。
Sergey: When the famine struck the steppe, and even potatoes wouldn't grow, the cavalry gave us food and shelter.

谢尔盖：我觉得来给他们当兵也不错，至少能给家里多留些粮食。
Sergey: So I thought, maybe it wouldn't be too bad to join them. At least then I could save some food for my family.

梅蕾尔：可……这是入伍，你要上战场的。
Merel: But you've enlisted in an army. You'll have to fight.

谢尔盖：这不还没开始正经打仗嘛，眼下大家都还活得好好的，这不就成了？
Sergey: But I haven't had to yet. And everyone's alive and fitter than ever. Isn't that enough?

红弩箭：你们已经是朋友了？
Lilya: Friends already, huh?

红弩箭从物资库慢悠悠地走回来，把一个肉罐头精准地扔进了梅蕾尔怀里。
She precisely tosses a can of meat into Merel's arms.

谢尔盖：没有我的份吗，中尉？
Sergey: Nothing for me, Lieutenant?

红弩箭：嘴馋了不早说？自己去领！
Lilya: Too slow. Got to get it yourself now.

梅蕾尔藏在芝诺士兵们轻松的闲聊中，低头盯着罐头上基金会的标志看了许久。
Merel, silent among their chatter, stares at the Foundation symbol on the can for a long while.

最终，她用食指拉开了罐头拉环，低头啜饮了一口飘着油花的肉汁。
Finally, she slips her index finger under the ring and pulls the can open. She lowers her head and sips the oily gravy.

？？？：曾经，我以为你会带领我们夺取永恒之物。我以为你像我一样，拥有这种崇高的、值得人追随的野心。
???: There was a time I thought you would lead us to the eternal. I thought you were like me—a man with ambition, a leader worth following.

？？？：可你现在变成了什么？——我从没想过，你是一个临阵退缩的懦夫。
???: But look what you've become. A coward.

？？？：我的立场从来没有变过，我要登上的是受人供奉的祭坛。在这一点上，我远超过你，伊戈尔。
???: You buckled while I stood tall. I have far excelled you, Igor, and the world will worship me for it.

他拿出手枪，瞄准眼前拦路的高大身影，然后扣下扳机，却只听见撞针击空时发出的脆弱“咔哒”声。
He whips out his pistol, aims at the tall figure blocking his way, and pulls the trigger, only to hear the faint click of the firing pin.

伊戈尔：……没有凡人能跨越永恒，格鲁托夫。
Igor: No mortal can transcend eternity, Krutov.

反倒是对手从容不迫地拔出了马刀。
His opponent calmly draws his shashka.

伊戈尔：你的傲慢超越了你应有的限度，使你变得愚蠢而残忍。这令我失望。
Igor: Your arrogance has gone beyond your means, turning you cruel and foolish. How disappointing.

格鲁托夫：你杀不死我，伊戈尔，你——
Krutov: You can't kill me, Igor. You—

格鲁托夫：——！
Krutov: ...!!

喧哗。枪声。互相推搡时的咒骂。马蹄掀起几乎有些烫人的尘埃。
Shouts, gunfire, curses, as men shove past one another and hooves kick up an almost scalding dust.

押送士兵：——把人都带过来，神秘学家和人类都分开。芝诺的俘虏单独带到一边，快动起来，一群懒鬼！
Escort Soldier: Bring everyone here! Separate the arcanists from the humans! Zeno's captives in their own line! Move it, slackers!

格鲁托夫：……
Krutov: ...

他从一贯焦躁的梦境中脱离，周身仍然弥漫着残余的熏香，令人憎恶的天仙子气味挥之不去。
He wakes from his restless dreams. Incense still lingers in the air around him, the hateful scent of henbane clinging to his nostrils.

格鲁托夫：没用的东西……我就知道那些脑子烧坏的术士完全不可靠。
Krutov: Useless. I knew that witless ritualist was not to be trusted.

仪式术士：格鲁托夫将军。
Ritualist: General Krutov.

似乎是早已预料到营帐中的人已清醒，一位着装与四周环境格格不入的术士侧身进入。
As if having foreseen that the man in the tent would awake, an oddly dressed ritualist slips inside.

仪式术士：熏香还未完全散去，你就已经清醒了。依我之见，你应该继续梦境，直到你能战胜梦魇。
Ritualist: You have awoken, yet the incense has yet to fade. I suggest you return to your dreams until you're capable of overcoming your nightmare.

格鲁托夫：这些谜语你爱说多少就说多少，但我已经受够这种把戏了——你进来做什么？
Krutov: Enough of your riddles and trickery. Why are you here?

仪式术士：俘虏。第一批俘虏已经送到了营地。
Ritualist: Captives. The first batch has arrived.

格鲁托夫：那就按照我们说好的去做，你把神秘学家带走，其余人都留下来交给我处置。有什么问题吗？
Krutov: Then you do as we agreed: Take the arcanists and leave the rest to me. What part of that do you not understand?

仪式术士：被俘的人中有一个比较奇特的个体，一名意识唤醒者。我们之前没有讨论过如何处理这种东西。
Ritualist: There is a peculiar individual among the captives—an Awakened. We didn't discuss how to deal with them.

格鲁托夫：意识唤醒者通常有些不同寻常的用处。关于它，你还知道些什么？
Krutov: An Awakened. Those can be particularly useful. What do you know of it?

仪式术士：拜祂赐予的知识，我得以知晓一些有关它的情报。没想到会在这里见到它。
Ritualist: Thanks to the knowledge bestowed by Her, I was able to glean some insight. Though, I'm surprised to have encountered it here.

仪式术士：一些可悲而愚钝的人采用神话中的名字为它命名，仿佛靠这种方法，就能让他们有罪的灵魂安息……
Ritualist: It seems the human fools named it after a mythological deity, as if by doing so, it would somehow render it capable of resting their sinful souls in peace.

格鲁托夫：有意思，带我去看看。
Krutov: Interesting. Take me to it.

营地边缘传来间歇性的沙袋落地声，每一次间隔中都夹杂着一阵密集的枪响。
Between the thudding of sandbags hitting the ground, bursts of gunfire echo through the camp.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

已为这个时代的悲剧献出生命的亡者，凭借着本能，感知周遭正在发生的一切。
Having already given his life to the tragedy of this age, Charon has already sensed what is happening around him.

他想要离开这处困境，却始终动弹不得。不久前，一位术士在他脚下留下了一连串能禁锢行动的符号。
He wants to leave but cannot move. Not long ago, a ritualist scratched a series of symbols beneath his feet, binding him to the spot.

格鲁托夫：卡戎，是吗？
Krutov: Charon, is it?

他很晚才意识到迫近的脚步声。顺着声音的来向，他缓缓转过身。
He senses the approaching footsteps only when they are already close, then turns toward the voice.

卡戎：……为什么要杀死那些投降的人？
Charon: Why did you kill those who surrendered?

格鲁托夫：我没有那么多粮食来喂他们，事实上，整个顿河也没有足够的粮食供现在的所有人过冬。
Krutov: Well, too many mouths to feed. There isn't enough food across the entire Don to keep everyone alive through the winter.

卡戎：你可以把他们放走，他们只是平民，不会对你的军队造成伤害。
Charon: You could have set them free. They were only civilians. They would cause you no trouble.

格鲁托夫：草原上只有凶狠而野蛮的哥萨克，没有平民。这些人会去投靠我的敌人，我不想好心做了坏事。
Krutov: Civilian implies civilization—civility, wouldn't you say? The Cossacks are barbarians. Setting them free would only bolster my enemies. I will not take the risk.

卡戎：……
Charon: ...

亡者垂首沉默，看起来他要说的、能说的已经说完。
Charon lowers his head in silence. It seems there are no words left in him.

格鲁托夫：真有意思……你和那个术士说得一模一样。告诉我，你真的能看见人们的死亡吗？
Krutov: Intriguing. Just as the ritualist said. Tell me, are you able to foresee a man's death?

卡戎：我知道阴影已经笼罩了草原，将有无数人死于饥饿与仇恨驱使的杀戮。所以，我来到了这里。
Charon: The shadow of death lingers over these grasslands. Countless will die in a killing driven by starvation and hatred. That is what brought me here.

格鲁托夫扭过头，看向营地边缘，微微隆起的小丘上，枯黄的牧草温顺地低垂着。
Krutov looks off to the edge of the camp, where the yellow pasture grass bows gently on small rises.

又有一阵密集的枪声，同样地伴随着某些东西摔向地面的声音。
Gunfire crackles again, along with the sound of something crashing to the ground.

格鲁托夫：就连我也能告诉你，草原即将被鲜血灌溉。明年的土地将会更加丰沃，而我是主宰这一切的主人。
Krutov: A shadow, you say? I see a man walking the grasslands, the dead nourishing the soil. He stands amid a bountiful harvest. I am that man.

格鲁托夫：我需要的不是这个，而是一个更精准的死亡预言，关于某一个人，或者……关于我自己。
Krutov: Your "shadow of death" means nothing. What I need is a precise prophecy, one for a single man, for me.

卡戎：我无法做到这样的事，也不愿预言任何人的死亡。
Charon: I cannot do such a thing. Nor is there any desire to.

格鲁托夫：我是在给你机会，意识唤醒者。留在我身边，为我的军队服务，我就不会把你交到那个术士手上。
Krutov: I am offering you a chance, Awakened. Serve me and my army, and I will spare you the ritualist's hand.

卡戎：术士？
Charon: Ritualist?

格鲁托夫用下巴指了指卡戎脚踩着的禁锢术式。
Krutov gestures toward the binding ritual beneath Charon with his chin.

格鲁托夫：这就是那个术士的杰作。她告诉我，你曾经用神秘术消除了这些术士施加在一个人类身上的精神咒术。
Krutov: This is her work. She tells me you dispelled another incantation cast by her kind on a human soldier.

格鲁托夫：现在，他们非常希望把你一点点拆成碎片，搞清楚你的神秘术究竟是如何运作的。
Krutov: She's desperate to tear you apart and see how you did it. Some special arcane skill, she claims.

格鲁托夫：相信我，那些疯子不会让你好受的。
Krutov: Trust me. What she will do to you is one thing you do not want to foresee.

卡戎：……重塑之手。
Charon: Manus Vindictae.

格鲁托夫：看来你也不是真的一无所知。现在，你知道该怎么做决定了吗？
Krutov: Ah, so you can see some specifics. Well? What is your decision?

卡戎：不……我既不是你的敌人，也不是你的盟友。除了为死者送葬，我无法为你们做到任何事。
Charon: No. Neither your enemy nor your ally. There is nothing I can do for you but bury the dead.

格鲁托夫凝视着卡戎，眼色锐利，仿佛是想切开对方遮蔽面容的血污白布。
Krutov fixes a sharp gaze on Charon, as if he could tear through the cloth covering his face with sight alone.

格鲁托夫：呵——理念不合，是吗？
Krutov: Difference of opinion, hmph?

格鲁托夫：人们总是这样，做出对所有人都不好的决定，所有人——所有人都在做错误的事！
Krutov: Why am I surprised? You're just like the rest of them. One bad decision after another!

比起卡戎，他简直是在咒骂一个并不存在于此处的对象。
His cursing seems to be directed at some invisible onlooker rather than at Charon.

格鲁托夫：而我会纠正所有的错误，只有我才会做到。
Krutov: And I am left to right their wrongs. It seems only I can.

格鲁托夫：我给过你机会了，怪东西。
Krutov: I gave you your chance, freak.

12TH-05 陌生的目光 / Strange Gazes

数千匹战马走过红柳树村前的道路，它们驮着全副武装的骑兵，用沉重的马蹄将土路踏得坚硬无比。
Thousands of warhorses carrying fully armed cavalrymen travel to Tamarovka, their heavy hooves pounding the dirt road into hard-packed earth.

骑兵军侦察连队首先抵达了村庄。村民们在屋门前张望，以一种警惕的姿态看着骑兵军士兵。
The Cavalry Corps's reconnaissance team reaches the village first. The villagers are on alert, eyeing the soldiers from their doorways.

谢尔盖：你听说了吗，梅蕾尔？等会儿会有个基金会的老爷到村里来。我们村还是第一次见这种人。
Sergey: You heard, Merel? A Foundation big shot's coming to the village. That's a first!

梅蕾尔：老爷？什么老爷？
Merel: Big shot? Who?

梅蕾尔不自觉地想拉起面罩，陡然意识到她已经在逃难的路上弄丢了原来的衣服。
Merel unconsciously reaches for her mask, suddenly realizing that she lost it during her escape.

谢尔盖：听说是个大官，军长亲自接待……算了，这不关我们的事。
Sergey: Not sure, but the commander needs to welcome them personally. *sigh* Forget it. None of our business.

谢尔盖：娜塔——什么？
Sergey: Natash—huh?

当他们走近一栋房屋时，谢尔盖似乎看见了熟人，想靠过去打声招呼。站在房门口的女人却飞快地关上了门。
As they pass a nearby house, Sergey seems to spot an old acquaintance in a doorway. He leans forward to greet her, but she shuts the door in his face.

梅蕾尔再也无法忽视从四面八方袭来的敌意，这种被盯着看的感觉让她想要缩成一团。
The hostility radiating from the onlookers in every direction makes Merel want to curl into a ball.

梅蕾尔：……谢尔盖，这真是你原来的村子吗？为什么村子里的人看我们的眼神这么奇怪。
Merel: Um, Sergey, isn't this your hometown? Why are they staring at you like that?

谢尔盖：我可不记得我之前有过这么多仇家，顶多……顶多也就一两个。这是在搞什么？
Sergey: I don't know. It's not like I've made that many enemies. Just one or two at most.

谢尔盖：搞不明白，还是去见我姑父吧——看见那座铁皮瓦的房子了吗？那就是我家。
Sergey: Anyway, let's go meet my uncle. See that house with the iron sheeting? That's our home.

梅蕾尔顺着谢尔盖指示的方向看去，在那座蓝色铁皮屋顶房子的院落前，见到了一位拄着拐杖的老人。
Merel follows his finger to a house with a blue iron-sheet roof. A man holding a cane stands in the yard.

谢尔盖兴奋地摘下帽子，举起来不断挥舞。
Sergey takes off his hat and excitedly waves it in the air.

谢尔盖：姑父！
Sergey: Uncle Petro!

老人止不住地用拐杖在地上敲着，拼命挤着眼睛，似乎在说“臭小子别开口了”。
The old man only strikes the ground with his cane. His heavy blink seems to say, "Don't start, boy."

谢尔盖：奇怪……
Sergey: What's going on?

梅蕾尔：也许有什么隐情……要不我们还是靠过去问一下吧。
Merel: Maybe something happened? Should we go ask him?

谢尔盖从没想到自己会一脸沮丧地来到家门口。姑父一把将养子拉到一边，梅蕾尔也下意识地跟了上去。
Sergey never expected his return home to be so dispirited. His uncle pulls him aside. Merel follows behind.

谢尔盖：这到底是在干什么呀？
Sergey: What's wrong, Uncle Petro?

姑父：还问我呢，倒是我要问你小子——你们的军长到底打不打那帮匪军？
Sergey's Uncle: You tell me! Did your commander say you'd fight those bandits or not?

谢尔盖：当然是要去打的。
Sergey: Of course!

姑父：什么时候打？
Sergey's Uncle: When?

谢尔盖：这、这倒是没告诉我……行动时间可是军事机密！
Sergey: That-That I don't know. It's a military secret!

姑父：有人说你们要进城去当乌龟，那我们这些住在乡下的，骑兵军还管不管了？
Sergey's Uncle: Word is you're going to the city—the lot of you! So where does that leave the rest of us, hm? The villagers need protecting too!

青年人没有想好怎么回答，只好尴尬地沉默着。姑父叹一口气，用一只干瘦有力的手死死捉住谢尔盖的胳膊。
The young man can't think of an answer. He can only stand in awkward silence. The uncle sighs and grips his nephew's shoulder hard with a slim yet powerful hand.

姑父：我懂了，我们一起逃难去吧。家里的东西已经收拾好了，今天我们就走，投奔你姑母在彼得罗夫卡的表姐去。
Sergey's Uncle: Alright, Seryozha, I understand. Everything's packed and ready to go. Come, we're leaving to your cousin's in Petrovka.

谢尔盖：姑父，你能不能把话说清楚一点！我怎么能当逃兵呢？
Sergey: Uncle Petro! Could you just tell me what's going on? I'm not deserting Zeno!

谢尔盖甩开姑父的手。一阵尴尬的愠怒染红了老人的脖子，他别过脸，斜眼看向一旁的梅蕾尔。
Sergey shakes off his uncle's hand. The old man's neck flushes red with embarrassment and anger. He turns and glances at Merel.

谢尔盖：她是我朋友，你别在意她，说吧。
Sergey: It's fine. She's a friend.

姑父：我们都在说，骑兵军不会管我们死活了，就算要管也管不了了。上游逃难过来的人说，匪军有好几万呢。
Sergey's Uncle: The cavalry is leaving us here to die. And the refugees from upstream—they said there are tens of thousands of bandits up there.

姑父：他们哪儿来这么多人啊？——这我倒不知道了，反正比你们骑兵军的人还多不少吧。你们拿什么打呢？
Sergey's Uncle: I don't know where they all came from, but your cavalry's nothing compared to that, right? You'll never fight them all off.

姑父：我悄悄告诉你，在你们来之前的几天夜里，村里剩下的小巫师、小女巫都投匪军去了！
Sergey's Uncle: And keep this quiet, but the kolduny left and joined the bandits!

谢尔盖：什么？！
Sergey: What?

姑父：别喊这么大声！他们走之前都说，谁要和骑兵军站一边，等他们杀回来了，就烧谁家的屋子。
Sergey's Uncle: Tch-tch-tch! They said they'd punish anyone who stands with the cavalry when they return.

他忧心忡忡地看着从村口经过的骑兵军。
He watches the Cavalry Corps soldiers passing by the village entrance.

姑父：要是你们打不过，全村都要被他们烧个一干二净了。所以，你到底和不和我逃难去？
Sergey's Uncle: If you can't fight them off, they'll burn the village to ashes. So, are you coming with us? Yes or no?

维尔汀：我看到红弩箭了。
Vertin: I see Lilya.

一支小规模的援军在草原上缓缓而行，运送枪弹与火炮的车队则缀在队伍之后，车轴隆隆作响。
A small group of reinforcements makes its slow advance across the grassland. A transport team carrying guns and artillery rumbles close behind.

十四行诗：她身边的人……应该就是芝诺骑兵军的军长了。
Sonetto: Hmm. That must be the commander of the Zeno cavalry beside her.

在此等候的骑兵军士官骑着马来到援军队列前，引导他们前往指定地点。
The Cavalry Corps officers awaiting them ride out to the head of the team to guide them to their destination.

老朋友先军长一步迎上司辰。
Before the commander can reach them, an old friend steps forward to greet the Timekeeper.

红弩箭：——头儿！基金会怎么偏偏在这个时候放你过来了？现在可一点也不太平。
Lilya: Captain! Why did the Foundation send you here? Isn't exactly the safest place in the world right now.

维尔汀：是我主动申请的，我需要在别列格勒搜寻一些情报……
Vertin: I applied for it. There's something I need to find in Bereggrad.

维尔汀：别这么看着我，红弩箭。Z女士批准了我这次外勤申请。
Vertin: Don't give me that look, Lilya. Madam Z approved it.

红弩箭：好吧，既然是Z女士同意过的。
Lilya: Alright, what Z says goes.

十四行诗：很高兴得知你安然无恙，红弩箭，在收到你的消息时我们都很紧张。
Sonetto: I'm glad to see you safe and sound, Ms. Lilya. Your message had us worried.

红弩箭：基金会应该更新一下通讯设备了，特殊时期，通讯器也该做成防弹的才对。
Lilya: Hah. The Foundation seriously needs to update their communication devices. At least, make them bulletproof.

军长靠近正在攀谈的队伍。
The commander approaches as they chat.

军长伊万：司辰。
Commander Ivan: Timekeeper.

维尔汀：你好，军长。我希望尽快了解别列格勒及周边的情况。
Vertin: Commander Ivan, it's a pleasure to meet you. If you could, a brief walk-through of the situation in Bereggrad and the surrounding areas would be most helpful.

军长伊万：我会向你们说明的。在此之前，我想问问这一支部队是哪儿来的？通讯中没有提到过他们。
Commander Ivan: Of course. But tell me, where did that company behind you spring from? I received no word in our communications.

军长看向援军中的一支百人左右的小队伍，他们由一位骑士所率领。
The commander's eyes settle on a small detachment within the reinforcements, about a hundred soldiers strong, led by a red-haired knight.

领队的红发骑士也发现了军长正在注意自己，便主动下马，靠上前来。
The knight notices him, too. She dismounts and steps forward.

玛尔纱：布列科夫少将，我是基金会“Ⅻ”特别行动小队的队医，我身后的是从前线返乡的士兵，还有一支野战医疗团队。
Marsha: Vice Admiral Burakov, I am the medic of the Foundation's special unit "XII." Behind me are the soldiers returning from the front lines and our field medical team.

玛尔纱：他们愿意加入骑兵军，参加对抗匪军的战斗。
Marsha: Every one of them is willing to enlist in the cavalry and join the fight against the bandits.

军长伊万：……这再好不过。
Commander Ivan: Good to know.

军长伊万：去找莎宾娜·斯捷尔诺娃上校，她会安排好你带来的这些人。
Commander Ivan: Go to Colonel Sabina Sternova. She will see your men settled.

玛尔纱：我明白了。
Marsha: Yes, Commander.

骑士带领这支特别的队伍离去。
The knight leads the special unit away.

军长伊万：请随我来吧，司辰。
Commander Ivan: Follow me, if you will, Timekeeper.

军长伊万：……目前，顿河零散的匪军有合流之势，他们得到了来源不明的芝诺武装，集中在相对靠近上游的位置。
Commander Ivan: Intelligence has spoken: the scattered bandit forces are converging upstream of the Don. They carry Zeno weaponry, though their identity is yet unknown.

军长伊万：有很大概率是伊戈尔主导了这一切，目前为止，按照指挥部的命令，我们没有与对方主力发生过大规模冲突。
Commander Ivan: Most likely, this is Igor's doing, though we've kept clear of them thus far, as headquarters ordered.

军长伊万：部分上游村庄已经遭到匪军洗劫。少数市民已经向下游逃难了，但是大多数还留守在城中不愿离开。
Commander Ivan: Villages have been plundered. Many have fled downstream, yet most cling to their homes.

军长从地图上抬起眼，露出了若有所思的神情。
The commander lifts his eyes from the map, still deep in thought.

军长伊万：根据芝诺的命令，骑兵军会在明早启程进城防守，直到你完成在别列格勒城内的任务。
Commander Ivan: Zeno has ordered the cavalry station in Bereggrad until your mission is complete. We ride at dawn.

维尔汀：骑兵军里有很多这个时代的本地人，他们对伊戈尔的认知是怎样的？
Vertin: Many of your cavalrymen are locals from the era. What do they think of Igor?

军长伊万：按照规定，他们没被告知圣保罗的事。伊戈尔在他们眼中是一个普通的军阀领袖。
Commander Ivan: What happened in São Paulo is classified. To them, he's a warlord like any other.

军长伊万：虽然我们还控制着一条进出城市的道路，但你要在这种情况下进城吗，司辰？叛军随时可能对城市发动攻击。
Commander Ivan: We do have a controlled route to the city, but Timekeeper, are you certain you wish to enter? The rebels could strike at any moment.

维尔汀：是的。至少城内还没有发生战斗，我需要尽快完成调查任务。
Vertin: Yes. I'll complete my mission quickly, hopefully before any conflict arises.

军长伊万：为了能更好地配合你的行动，我能了解任务的具体细节吗？
Commander Ivan: I see. Then tell me the details of your mission so that I may lend my hand.

维尔汀：我需要在城内找到一个与“暴雨”有关的重要线索，它与一个叫做“琥珀屋”的地方有关。
Vertin: There's a place in the city called the Amber Room. It's said to hold an important clue about the "Storm."

维尔汀：这就是我知道的全部。你对这个词有印象吗，军长？
Vertin: Does it sound familiar at all, Commander?

军长伊万：我想你说的不是放在圣彼得堡的那座国家宝藏，不然你也不会到一千公里外的别列格勒来了。
Commander Ivan: Not the Amber Room in St. Petersburg, I presume. We're a long way off from there.

军长伊万：我在别列格勒从未听人提起过它，看来我没法为你提供别的援助。
Commander Ivan: Then no, can't say it does. It seems I cannot aid you much in this.

军长顿了顿，问出了自己更加关心的问题。
The commander pauses, then asks the question that's been gnawing at him since the Timekeeper's arrival.

军长伊万：司辰，除了调查“暴雨”线索外，你身上是否还肩负调查“金色饥荒”的任务？
Commander Ivan: Timekeeper, may I ask: besides your "Storm" investigation, are you also here to deal with the Golden Famine?

军长伊万：我们尝试过自己解决，但芝诺的军人不具备调查神秘学事件的经验，很难找到症结所在。
Commander Ivan: We tried ourselves, but Zeno soldiers have little experience in arcane matters. We couldn't unearth the root.

维尔汀：抱歉，我没有接到相关的指示，但我会尽量留意可能的线索。
Vertin: I'm sorry. I didn't receive any information on that matter. But I'll keep an eye out for you.

军长伊万：……我明白了。
Commander Ivan: I see.

军长伊万：骑兵军会全力协助你。可是目前我们拥有的兵力，加上援军，也很难保证别列格勒的安全。
Commander Ivan: The cavalry will aid you in any way we can. But with our strength as it is, I cannot guarantee the safety of Bereggrad.

维尔汀：虽然我不确定这会有多大帮助，但是我在不久前刚得知了新一批即将到来的增援。
Vertin: I'm not sure how much it will help, but I heard reinforcements are on the way.

维尔汀：一支新组建的飞行巫师中队马上就会抵达红柳树村，她们还多带来了一把新的飞行扫帚。
Vertin: The newly formed Flying Witch Company will arrive soon, along with a new broomstick for Lilya.

一旁昏昏欲睡的红弩箭来了兴趣。
Lilya suddenly perks up.

红弩箭：芝诺重新组建了飞行巫师中队？
Lilya: Zeno reformed the Flying Witches?

维尔汀：不，这是属于基金会的飞行中队。
Vertin: No, this unit belongs to the Foundation.

维尔汀：另外，红弩箭，伊里内伊委员委托我问你，你愿意在这次行动中临时担任飞行中队的队长吗？
Vertin: Lilya, Committee member Irinei asks if you'll serve as its temporary captain. What do you say?

在她面前的是一座孤独的空房子。
Sternova gestures to a lonely, empty house.

斯捷尔诺娃：以前住在这间屋子里的人有两年没有回来了。我问过村长，他同意把这里借给你住几天。
Sternova: We haven't seen the owner of this place for two years. The elder said you can stay here for a few days.

玛尔纱：这里……还挺宽敞的。
Marsha: This is spacious.

只要能忽视它摇摇欲坠的结构，这还算是一间不错的临时住所。
If you ignore its decrepit state, it is a fairly decent place for a short stay.

斯捷尔诺娃：嗯，就是院子里的马厩已经倒了，一直没有修好。不介意的话，你的马可以交给骑兵军统一照料。
Sternova: Um, yeah. The stable in the yard still needs some fixing up, so the cavalry will have to take care of your horse, if you don't mind.

玛尔纱：那再好不过，麻烦你们了。
Marsha: That would be kind of you. Thank you very much.

斯捷尔诺娃：没事，骑兵军有的是马，多一匹马也不算什么事。
Sternova: It's no big deal. What's one more horse to feed?

斯捷尔诺娃把房屋的钥匙交给玛尔纱之后，牵着她的马离开了。
Sternova hands the key to Marsha and leads her horse away.

玛尔纱转过身，正准备将钥匙插入锁孔，便被一阵窸窣声吸引了注意力。
Just as Marsha is about to slip the key inside the lock, a rustling sound catches her attention.

玛尔纱：有老鼠？
Marsha: Is that a rat?

——可这大得不像是老鼠能发出来的声音。
Not the sound a rat would make.

一个小小的黑色阴影消失在院落一旁曾经茂盛过的榆树下。
A small black shadow vanishes behind the once-leafy elm in the corner of the yard.

玛尔纱：嗯？是村里的小孩吗？
Marsha: Hm? Or a child from the village?

玛尔纱：算了……先进房屋休息吧。
Marsha: Never mind. I need to rest.

同样的动静再次传来，玛尔纱再次朝可疑的地点投去目光。
She hears it again. She looks over to the same spot.

玛尔纱：到底是谁躲在那儿？
Marsha: Who's there?

在榆树干后，她的目光与一颗探出来的脑袋短暂相遇。
From behind the elm, a head peeks out, briefly meeting her eyes.

？？？：……！
???: ...!

这一次，人影不再依靠掩体遮蔽身形，而是消失在一道神秘术的辉光中。
This time, the shadow doesn't hide itself behind the tree but disappears in the glow of an arcane skill.

玛尔纱：消失了？
Marsha: Vanished? Just like that?

玛尔纱警惕起来——她很难再把躲藏者视作无害对象。骑士拿出武器，向着神秘术辉光消散的方向而去。
This could be a threat. Marsha draws her weapon and moves toward the fading arcane light.

一抹团状的黑色影子又一次在视线中一闪而过。
A shadow flashes past once more.

玛尔纱：这是什么东西？刚刚看见的明明是一个人影才对。
Marsha: What? That was definitely a person.

玛尔纱：这么躲躲藏藏的实在是太可疑了，而且还是在骑兵军驻扎的村子里……难道是间谍？
Marsha: A person sneaking in the shadows around the cavalry's station. Suspicious to be sure. A spy, perhaps?

“沙沙——”
*a strange sound*

声音再次暴露出方位。
Its direction is exposed again.

在追逐之前，玛尔纱凝神审视——
Turning, Marsha stares intently.

玛尔纱：……我没看错吧，那对蟹螯……是招潮蟹？在顿河草原上？
Marsha: Are my eyes playing tricks on me? Is that a fiddler crab? On the Don steppe?

骑士迈开脚步，以惊人的速度向可疑的招潮蟹靠近，沉重的盔甲也完全没有影响她的速度。
The knight runs toward the dubious fiddler crab at astonishing speed. Her heavy armor doesn't seem to slow her down in the slightest.

而对方几乎是慌不择路地横着向村外逃窜。
In its desperation, her opponent flees sideways toward the outskirts of the village.

二人之间的距离越来越近。
But there is no escape. The knight is closing in on the crab.

玛尔纱：——抓到你了！
Marsha: Got you!

被逼到墙角的海栖魔精咔嚓作响地在空中挥舞巨螯。
Forced into a corner, the fiddler crab snaps its oversized claws in the air.

招潮蟹？：嘶嘶……嘶嘶嘶——！
Fiddler Crab?: Sssss!

玛尔纱：放弃吧，你的变形术也太拙劣了，招潮蟹怎么可能会在草原上出现？
Marsha: Enough, shapeshifter! This is absurd! How would a fiddler crab make it out here to the plain?

玛尔纱：而且作为一只招潮蟹，你的体型也太大了。
Marsha: And might I remind you that you're too big to be a crab?

招潮蟹？：嘶……
Fiddler Crab?: Sss ...

辉光再次闪烁着，环绕着招潮蟹周身的光线开始扭曲变形。
The same glow returns, the light surrounding the fiddler crab bending and distorting.

施术者终于放弃了无用的神秘术。
It reveals the figure of a girl.

梅蕾尔：……
Merel: ...

新晋的“Ⅻ”小队队医与逃亡中的“Ⅻ”小队队员四目相对。
The newly appointed medic of the "XII" Squad locks eyes with her team's deserter.

梅蕾尔：又……又见面了——
Merel: H-Hey, nice to see you again. Heh.

玛尔纱：梅，蕾，尔？
Marsha: Merel?

玛尔纱：你怎么……
Marsha: H-How did you ...

玛尔纱向前一步。被抓捕的逃兵立刻下蹲，双手护住头顶。
Marsha steps forward. Caught at last, Merel squats down, covering her head with both hands.

梅蕾尔：别……别打我！我什么都说！
Merel: D-Don't hurt me! I'll tell you everything.

玛尔纱：……你是说，打算就这么混在骑兵军里直到战争结束？
