Merel: Oh, oh, God. Marsha, you're hurt. And all these kids ... Hurry, she needs medical help!

12TH-17 骑兵们 / The Cavalry

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：他们逃跑了——和我一起追上去，谢尔盖！
Zeno Cavalryman I: The enemy's turned tail! Let's ride them down, Sergey!

马背上的骑兵视野开阔，他向东北方的上游位置望去，见到零星逃窜的黑衣士兵。
From horseback, the rider has a clear view. Upstream to the northeast, a few black figures are fleeing.

谢尔盖：什、什么？他们真跑了？
Sergey: Th-They're running? Are you sure?

谢尔盖一边扒拉杂草，一边踮起脚，伸长了脖子朝战友指示的方向张望。
Sergey pushes through the grass and stands on his tiptoes, straining to see where his comrade is pointing.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：那当然，我们往前一冲，这些人就和扒在肉上的苍蝇一样逃走了。他们留下了不少东西，我看见有重机枪呢！
Zeno Cavalryman I: Course I am! The moment those cowards saw us coming, they scattered like scared little rabbits! Left their heavy guns and supplies right where they stood!

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：——诶？你怎么站在地上？你的马去哪儿了？
Zeno Cavalryman I: Wait, where the hell's your horse gone?

只有两条腿能依赖的青年哥萨克急得脖子通红。
Sergey flushes red.

谢尔盖：我只记得，有一道黑影照我脑门上“呼啦”一下飞过来，然后我闭上眼，拿刀往前头一挥。
Sergey: I-I'm not sure. All I know is something flew right at my forehead, and before I could think, I'd swung my shashka at it.

谢尔盖：我、我不知道砍到什么东西，只觉得手上被一道力气使劲一扯，就从马上摔下去了。
Sergey: I don't even know what I hit. Next thing I knew, I was on the ground.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：这可是你第一次参加真正的冲锋啊，谢尔盖。
Zeno Cavalryman I: That's one way to end your first charge, Sergey.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：前两次出击没有轮到我们连，你还吱哇乱叫呢，现在就自认倒霉吧——我们先走一步，等不了你了。
Zeno Cavalryman I: And to think you were whining about not getting to charge in first. Well, looks like you'll be waiting a while longer, haha.

谢尔盖：等等，你带我一起去吧，萨沙。这场胜仗也得有我的一份吧！
Sergey: Hey, wait. Take me up on your horse. I'm not missing out on our victory.

谢尔盖好不容易穿越草地，刚刚能够到朋友的战马旁。
He presses his way through the tall grass, finally reaching his friend's horse.

山羊胡骑兵：给我站住！
"Goat": Stop right there, all of you!

谢尔盖：——！
Sergey: ...!

迎面又撞出来一匹高头大马，拦住了企图前去追逃的骑兵的去路。马背上的老哥萨克挺直了腰，他说话时，下巴上的胡须也随之剧烈抖动。
A rider on a tall horse cuts off the chase. The old Cossack sits straight, his goatee trembling as he speaks.

山羊胡骑兵：萨沙，谢尔盖，还有所有打前锋的连队，全都给我回来，禁止追击！
"Goat": Sasha, Sergey, all of you, stop your pursuit!

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：他们没跑多远，长官，都是些步兵，我们能追上他们的。
Zeno Cavalryman I: But they're on foot. We can still catch them if we go now.

山羊胡骑兵：命令就是命令，不给我滚回去，我把你们一个个都带给军长处置！
"Goat": This order comes from the commander himself, so do as I say, or I'll haul your disobedient asses straight to his feet!

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：行——行吧，听你的！可这到底又是闹哪出呢，尤里？
Zeno Cavalryman I: Fine, fine! But, why? You've fought all kinds of battles, Yuri. What do you think?

山羊胡骑兵：后方主力已经和我们脱节了，如果敌人在前面埋伏，我们一个人都回不来。
"Goat": The main force probably hasn't caught up with us. We would be exposed to a counterattack if we move too far ahead.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：他们留下的东西我们也不要吗？
Zeno Cavalryman I: But what about the stuff they left behind? Are we just going to ignore it?

山羊胡骑兵：又不会有乌鸦飞来把它们偷走。
"Goat": For now. It is not like the ravens will swoop down and snatch them up.

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：那我们在这儿等着，之后再去拿。
Zeno Cavalryman I: Then, shouldn't we just grab their weapons first and then wait?

山羊胡骑兵：不，已经打了一整天了，我们要回营休息，人和马都得喘口气，吃点东西。
"Goat": We have been fighting for hours. Head back to camp. Catch a breath and a bite to eat while you can, for you and your horse.

山羊胡骑兵：之后会有其他团来轮替我们。侦察部队确认前方安全后，他们会去把敌人丢下的东西捞回来。
"Goat": They will rotate another unit in later, after the scouts confirm whether the front is secure. Let them have the bother of retrieving the enemy's supplies.

谢尔盖：可是那些东西是我们——
Sergey: What? But we found them fir—

山羊胡骑兵：你是为了战利品打仗？——你是芝诺的骑兵，还是强盗？！
"Goat": And you think that means they belong to you, huh? Are you a Cossack or a bandit?

谢尔盖被吓得一愣。
Sergey freezes.

谢尔盖：我才不是强盗……
Sergey: I-I'm no bandit.

山羊胡骑兵：那就听好，骑兵军会统一分配战利品，别再惦记这回事。现在所有人都和我一起回营地。
"Goat": Then stop thinking like one. Leave the supplies for now. We must return to camp.

谢尔盖：我听你的，但我也得找到我的马，我不能没有马呀！
Sergey: But my horse is gone. I need to find him first.

山羊胡骑兵：别大喊大叫的，我刚才都看见你的马了，它自己往营地的方向跑了。
"Goat": Stop your whining now, sonny. I spied your horse wandering off toward camp.

谢尔盖：它自己跑回去了？
Sergey: What? He ran back without me?

马和人都歇下了。它们依偎着站在一起，像一队疲惫的士兵。
The men and horses rest. They sit and lean against one another, looking weary.

山羊胡骑兵：来，洗一洗伤口，喝点水。
"Goat": Here, drink this, or use it to clean your wounds.

老哥萨克身上挂着几个军用水壶，穿梭在或坐或躺着的骑兵间，最后来到了一片草坡上。
The old Cossack moves among the riders with several canteens in hand. He makes his way to a grassy slope.

谢尔盖：欸——你踩着我了，尤里叔叔。
Sergey: Hey, watch your step, Uncle Yuri. You nearly stepped on my foot.

谢尔盖在地上翻了个身，老哥萨克将水壶递到年轻的哥萨克面前。
Sergey rolls over on the ground. The old man offers him a canteen.

山羊胡骑兵：你的水，小子。水壶洗了三次，用苇草擦干净的，一点儿泥巴味都没有！
"Goat": Here's yours, sonny. Cleaned it three times myself. Drink up and be grateful.

谢尔盖本能地伸手去接，却忽然吃痛。
Sergey reaches for it and winces.

谢尔盖：——好疼！嘶……刚从马上摔下来还感觉什么事都没有呢……
Sergey: Agh! *gasp* I didn't feel anything after I fell off my horse, but now ...

老骑兵嘴上的山羊胡抖了抖。他坐在谢尔盖身边的草地上。
The old cavalryman's goatee twitches. He takes a seat on the grass beside Sergey.

山羊胡骑兵：第一次打仗的感觉怎么样？
"Goat": Your first taste of battle. How does it settle with you?

老骑兵的语气温和，与之前在战场上呵斥年轻人时大为不同。
His voice is gentle now, not as sharp or scolding as it was on the battlefield.

谢尔盖：……和想象中不太一样。
Sergey: Well, it's not what I imagined.

谢尔盖战斗刚结束时的兴奋劲儿也消失无踪。
Having seen war for the first time, Sergey's naive excitement has faded.

谢尔盖：在马背上我连枪都端不稳，更别提瞄准了。手指一扣，一匣子弹全抖了出去，一根毛都没打着。
Sergey: Everything's different when it's real. Couldn't hold my gun steady. Just fired at everything that moved until my ammo was spent. I'm not even sure I hit anything.

山羊胡骑兵：你的马刀呢？
"Goat": And your shashka, Sergey?

谢尔盖：这和切熏肉一点儿也不一样。好几次我想把刀收回来，他们的骨头都紧紧攥住了我的刀，刀把在我手里直打滑。
Sergey: Yeah, I got a few with it. I thought it would be simple, like cutting a knife through bacon. But I can still feel it—how the blade shook when I struck their ribs, the sound as I pulled it out of their chests.

周围逐渐响起了鼾声，于是谢尔盖把声音放得更轻了些。
Amid the snores of his countrymen, Sergey keeps his voice low.

谢尔盖：尤里叔叔，我觉得我会下地狱。
Sergey: I think I'm going to hell after I die, Uncle Yuri.

老哥萨克把还剩一点儿水的水壶往谢尔盖怀里一扔。
The old Cossack tosses the nearly empty canteen into Sergey's lap.

谢尔盖：哎哟！
Sergey: Oy!

谢尔盖：你这是干嘛呢？！不能生火，我这头发、衣服一晚上都干不了。
Sergey: What did you do that for? I'm drenched.

山羊胡骑兵：让你别瞎想。你是个小男巫，本来就进不了那些传教士嘴里的天堂。
"Goat": Heh! To rinse your thoughts. You're a koldun, remember? You were not allowed into their so-called "heaven" in the first place.

山羊胡骑兵：或者说，你觉得天堂是个什么地方？
"Goat": What would "heaven" look like to you, anyway?

谢尔盖：房梁挂着吃不完的冷熏鲟鱼，姑母每天都会做热乎的鸡肉蘑菇馅饼。
Sergey: Hmm. It'd be a place where smoked sturgeon hangs in rows from the beams, and the air's thick with the smell of my auntie's chicken-and-mushroom pies.

谢尔盖：住在村口的阿司塔霍娃夫人在夜里哼着歌，我和兄弟们假装回家路过，实际上是特意绕的路，只为远远看她一眼。
Sergey: Every night, the beautiful Madam Astakhova would sing. My friends and I used to sneak down to the village square just to catch a glimpse of her.

谢尔盖：马儿在丰沃的草甸上漫步，一条不会泛滥也不会干涸的河穿过草场中央……
Sergey: And our horses would roam free on a lush green steppe, and a river would run through its heart—a river that never floods and never runs dry.

谢尔盖：噢！
Sergey: Oh, isn't that ...?

话说到这儿，饶是谢尔盖这样年轻的灵魂也意识到了“天堂”所在。
He suddenly recognizes what "heaven" he's describing.

山羊胡骑兵：顿河，你的家，我的家。我们永恒的根基和最终的归宿。
"Goat": Yes, the Don steppe. Our eternal homeland. Where we were born, and where we will always belong.

山羊胡骑兵：孩子，把你的刀磨亮，给你的枪上膛——你是“天堂”最忠诚的卫士。除了我们，没有任何人有保护这里的能力和资格。
"Goat": So sharpen your shashka and ready your rifle, faithful guardian of heaven. Only we will, only we can, protect it.

他用力拍了拍谢尔盖的肩膀，把他从沉思中拉了回来。
A firm clap on the shoulder brings him back from his thoughts.

山羊胡骑兵：去，再练练瞄准。回来的时候记得给大家的水壶都灌满。
"Goat": Go for a walk. Practice your aim. And be sure to refill everyone's canteens on your way back.

谢尔盖：好、好……
Sergey: O-Okay.

谢尔盖懵懵懂懂地应了一声，小跑着捡起水壶走向河边。
Mumbling, Sergey takes the canteen and jogs toward the river.

谢尔盖：……要怎样才能像尤里叔叔那样精准呢？
Sergey: Hmm, how can I become a sharpshooter like Uncle Yuri?

谢尔盖举起枪，歪头瞄准。
Sergey lifts his rifle and tilts his head to aim.

下一秒，他就沮丧地放下了枪。
A moment later, he lowers it, frustrated.

谢尔盖：不对，不太对。如果在马背上这么举枪，马会把我甩下来的。
Sergey: Something's wrong with my stance. If I hold the gun like this, the horse will throw me off again.

谢尔盖：斯捷尔诺娃上校又是怎么做的呢？我听说她蝉联了三次芝诺自由骑射大赛的冠军。
Sergey: How does the colonel do it? She won the Zeno Horseback Shooting Contest three times in a row.

谢尔盖又举起了枪，这次他闭上了一只眼，想象自己是草场上最受人瞩目的大明星。
He tries again and closes one eye, picturing himself a star on the steppe.

谢尔盖：把背挺直，谢尔盖！放松你的屁股，在马鞍上坐稳……
Sergey: Sit up straight, Sergey. Relax your buttocks. Stay steady.

谢尔盖：对，就是这样！这样看东西也更清楚……
Sergey: Yeah, that's it! I think I've got it now!

视野里出现了几只蚂蚁。
A few ants crawl across his sights.

谢尔盖：嗯……？
Sergey: Hmm?

谢尔盖揉了揉眼睛。
He rubs his eyes.

这一次，蚂蚁大小的黑点变成了黑衣军人。
They're not ants. They're people.

谢尔盖：**[斯拉夫粗口]！是格鲁托夫的人！
Sergey: Damn! It's Krutov's men!

谢尔盖：敌袭！敌袭！呜——！
Sergey: Enemies! Enemies atta—ugh!

谢尔盖发现自己像是被下了什么咒，舌头变得肿大，堵在了嗓子眼。
Sergey's tongue sticks fast in his mouth.

仪式术士：看看我们发现了什么……一名小巫师。
Ritualist: Hmph. Look what we've found. A koldun.

仪式术士：芝诺真是狂妄。有着如此优秀血脉的神秘学家，竟然只能当饮马小倌？孩子，你拿得动枪吗？
Ritualist: Those arrogant Zeno fools. How could they assign a gifted arcanist like you to such trivial chores? And so young. Can you even use that thing properly?

谢尔盖：呜……呜！！
Sergey: Urh. Urgh!

谢尔盖用行动回答了术士的讥讽。
Sergey answers the ritualist's taunt with action.

没有多余的瞄准动作，他高举步枪，将枪口对准夜空——
Without aiming, he swings his rifle toward the night's sky—

——砰！
*bang*

一阵骚乱从不远处的矮坡后传来。骑兵们屈起拇指含在唇边，让马哨如枪声一般唤醒夜空。
The resting cavalrymen jump to their feet, their whistles cutting through the darkness as they press their thumbs and forefingers to their lips.

仪式术士：该死……！
Ritualist: Curse you!

仪式术士：复苏之母的孩子们！为了祂的愿望与我们闪耀着无尽空白的未来——
Ritualist: Children of the Great Mother of Resurrection, show your devotion to Her grand vision and the imminent brilliant Blank Era!

随着太阳徐徐升起的，还有一束束硝烟。
Gunsmoke filters the light as dawn breaks.

每隔五俄里——这是骑兵军战时电台的最长中继距离——枪声与战马的嘶鸣一同响起，随后冲天的火光便融进了黎明。
At every five versts, the maximum relay distance for cavalry field radios, the steppe is torn by gunfire and the cries of men and horses.

格鲁托夫：骑兵军从较为薄弱的左岸进军，想要断掉我的后路——呵，伊万，还是这样天真，惹人发笑。
Krutov: Thought you'd outflank me from the left bank and cut off my supply line? Ha! Ivan Ivanovich, I almost thought better of you.

格鲁托夫：就算在这个时代，骑兵也是过时的玩意。
Krutov: Even in this era, cavalry have outlived their use.

在他身旁不远处，重塑之手的术士口中念念有词，专心致志地清点昨夜的猎获。
Not far off, a Manus ritualist counts the night's catch, murmuring steadily to herself.

仪式术士：十一、十二……一共十三名神秘学家。遗憾的是，潜入城市的部队已经失去了联络，权且当他们已经死去吧。
Ritualist: Eleven, twelve, thirteen arcanists in total. But the unit we sent into the city has gone silent. Already dead, likely.

术士对昨夜的“收获”十分满意。她点了点头，随后勾了勾手。
The ritualist seems pleased. She nods and curls a finger.

谢尔盖：唔——！
Sergey: Urgh!

仿佛有一条看不见的锁链套上了他的脖子，谢尔盖和其他十二个被俘的神秘学家被无形之力牵扯着向前。
An invisible chain seems to clamp around his neck. Sergey and twelve other captive arcanists are wrenched forward.

渐渐地，谢尔盖感觉一阵极寒从脚踝缠上了他。
A deep cold starts to creep up Sergey's legs.

谢尔盖：嗯？
Sergey: Huh?

他低下头，发觉脚下踩着的泥土竟被无来由的寒意冻得僵硬，粘住了他的鞋子，让他动弹不得。
He looks down. The earth has frozen hard from a chill conjured from thin air. It has glued his boots in place.

仪式术士：……你这是什么意思，将军？
Ritualist: What's the meaning of this, Krutov?

格鲁托夫转了转手腕，面露不悦。
Krutov straightens his cuff, looking annoyed.

格鲁托夫：你没经过我的允许，就擅自派遣重塑之手的士兵潜入城市。这不是我想看到的合作态度。
Krutov: You sent Manus soldiers into Bereggrad without my consent. This is far from the cooperation I was expecting.

仪式术士：我们要明确一点，重塑之手的军队不受你的指挥。
Ritualist: To be absolutely clear, General, Manus Vindictae's soldiers are not under your command.

仪式术士：你执意要调走主力进攻伊戈尔，这已经严重扰乱了我们在顿河的任务。这也不是我们希望看见的合作态度。
Ritualist: You insisted on diverting your main force to attack Igor, seriously disrupting our efforts in the region. Do you call that cooperation?

仪式术士：现在，那帮飞行巫师正在一个接一个地破坏术阵的节点，大规模战争也导致神秘学家大量外逃……
Ritualist: Those atrocious Flying Witches are flitting around destroying our rites as we speak. And I won't even speak of the arcanists we could've recruited if it weren't for the battles you sparked.

格鲁托夫：伊戈尔就躲在骑兵军的塞契里，等我的主力开到，他的生命和他的军队很快就会走到尽头。
Krutov: Hmph, soon, my army will reach the Cavalry Corps's sich. Igor will be forced out of his hole, his pathetic life will end, and his so-called "Legion" will crumble.

格鲁托夫：至于骑兵军则更是不值一提。顿河很快就会完全掌控在我的手中，到那时你们想在顿河做什么都随便。
Krutov: As for the rest of them, they're beneath concern. The Don will soon be under my control; after that, you can do whatever you want here.

格鲁托夫：当然，你们可以选择加快战争的进程。只要你为我打开那条“通道”，把我的人送到塞契……
Krutov: Of course, our victory could be brought about even sooner with that "gateway." Just open it and teleport my men directly into the sich.

仪式术士：呵，您必须经过面具的试炼，才有资格利用那条“通道”，否则我也无法为你开启。
Ritualist: Hmph. It cannot be done until you pass the mask trial and earn the right to enter it.

格鲁托夫：不要再用面具的事来搪塞我。你们不愿意全力援助，就不要指望我会完全配合你们的行动。
Krutov: Ah. These masks—a convenient excuse to undermine me. If you refuse to scratch my back, don't expect me to scratch yours.

格鲁托夫：不借助你的小伎俩，我的军队也有其他进军路线可以选择。
Krutov: My army will achieve victory, with or without your cheap tricks.

仪式术士：悉听尊便，将军。
现在，我可以带这些神秘学家回归复苏之母的怀抱了吗？
Ritualist: Pray, do as you please, General. Now, would you allow me to return these arcanists to Her embrace?

格鲁托夫轻哼一声，挥了挥手。缠住俘虏的冻土开始融化。
Krutov sniffs and waves a hand. The frozen ground holding the prisoners begins to thaw.

格鲁托夫：那些受了重伤没法当劳工的人类也一并处理了。
Krutov: Deal with the injured humans while you're at it. They're no use to me.

仪式术士：当然。
Ritualist: My pleasure.

术士从袖中拿出一个嗅盐瓶子。
The ritualist pulls a bottle of smelling salts from her sleeve.

仪式术士：骤风即至！
Ritualist: Blow till thou brust thy wind!

瓶中的苦味粉末被狂风吹散，送入其他俘虏的鼻腔。
Bitter powder scatters on the wind, swirling and twisting among the captives.

山羊胡骑兵：……
"Goat": ...

血液在呼吸之间沸腾，眼球、心脏、大脑都随着一种独特的旋律跃动了起来。
Blood boils in their veins, their eyes, hearts, and minds tuning in to a strange rhythm.

谢尔盖从未感觉思维如此清晰，一种莫名的兴奋抓住了他的脖子，让他回头看向被俘的长官——
Sergey's thoughts have never been so clear. A wild excitement grabs him by the neck, willing him to turn toward his captured commander.

谢尔盖：呜……！
Sergey: Argh!

惨叫被术士的神秘术堵在了牙关。谢尔盖挣扎着，眼中血管爆开，将他染成了一头浴血的兽。
The ritualist's arcane skill strangles the scream in Sergey's throat. His face contorts, his eyes bulging red as if possessed by some beast.

血色视野中，他的战友、家人，乃至“天堂”一一坠落。
In the red haze, his friends, his family, even his "heaven" all fall away.

12TH-18 灰色马 / The Pale Horse

飞行中队缓缓降下高度，盘旋在草原上空。
The flight unit makes a slow descent as they circle above the plains.

红弩箭：嗯……
Lilya: Hmm.

这支队伍的临时队长正在沉思着。
Their temporary captain remains lost in silent thought.

阿尔法2号：伊戈尔给了我们一个空的节点，中尉，我们是不是被耍了？
Alpha Two: There was nothing at the coordinates Igor sent us. Do you think he lied to us, Lieutenant?

阿尔法2号：阿……阿嚏！
Alpha Two: Achoo!

空中的飞鸟比地上的生灵更快感觉到天气变化，渐起的寒风让其中的不少人都打起了哆嗦。
Those in the air sense the changes in weather before the creatures of the earth do. A sharp wind sends a shiver through their ranks.

红弩箭：天气开始变冷了，说明其他被我们破坏掉的那些节点是对的。他没必要拿这最后的节点耍我们。
Lilya: The weather's gotten colder every time we destroyed a rite. I don't see why he'd only trick us with the last site.

阿尔法2号：那又是怎么回事，术阵不能长着腿跑了吧？
Alpha Two: Then what's going on? You can't move rites around, can you?

红弩箭：我也想不明白——还撑得住吗？先落下去加件衣服吧。
Lilya: Beats me. How's everyone holding up? If it's too cold, we can fly low until we get on some extra layers.

她们就等着队长的这句话，白色制服的飞行员们迫不及待地继续降低高度——
They'd been waiting for those words. The white-clad Witches immediately lower their altitude.

阿尔法2号：咳……
Alpha Two: *cough*

她茫然地张开嘴，颈椎骨片、肌肉组织被血冲了出来。
Her mouth falls open, her eyes wide as blood gushes from the hole blasted in her neck.

飞行器失去控制，在空中打着转，将它再无声息的主人抛下了。
Her aircraft spirals out of control, flinging its lifeless pilot from its back.

红弩箭：阿尔法2号！！
Lilya: Alpha Two!!

红弩箭压低扫把向地面俯冲，在飞行巫师坠落地面前接住了她。
Lilya plunges into a near-vertical dive, catching the falling Witch before she hits the ground.

红弩箭压低扫把向地面俯冲，在飞行巫师坠落地面前接住了她。

红弩箭：哈……
Lilya: Rrrgh!

红弩箭：1号、3号，立刻脱离编队，近地飞行，把那放冷枪的杂种揪出来！
Lilya: Alpha One and Three, break formation and stay low! Flush out the shooter.

红弩箭：4号、5号、6号，都别愣着，忘了你们的训练吗？拉高——飞到那帮耗子的射程死角！
Lilya: Get a grip, the rest of you! Alpha Four, Five, and 6, pull up and stay out of range of those rats on the ground!

阿尔法4号：队长！
Alpha Four: Lieutenant!

阿尔法4号在低空盘旋，尾焰倏地点燃了河畔枯黄的苇草，让藏匿其中的黑色军队暴露无遗。
Alpha Four circles low, igniting the dry riverside reeds and revealing the black-clad forces hidden among them.

阿尔法4号：重塑之手的人已经围过来了！
Alpha Four: The Manus are gaining on us!

红弩箭蹲下身，替她的队员阖上了眼。
Lilya crouches and gently closes her wingmate's eyes.

再扶着红色38站起来时，苇草燃烧的火焰点燃了她的双眼。
She grabs Red 38 and stands, the fire of the burning reeds blazing in her eyes.

红弩箭：那就让他们亲眼看着自己是怎么被撕成碎片的！
Lilya: Good. They can watch as I tear them apart piece by piece!

红弩箭反手擦掉了脸上的血。
She wipes the blood from her cheek.

鲜红、温热，来自一位数分钟前还挠着头发愣的飞行员，一条数分钟前还鲜活着的生命。
Warm and red, from a pilot who had just moments ago been scratching her head in bewilderment. A whole life lost, just like that.

飞行巫师们像秋天的枫叶般盘旋着，落到了红弩箭身边。
The Flying Witches descend, landing nearby.

阿尔法4号：……队长。
Alpha Four: Lieutenant.

红弩箭因疲惫而呆滞的双目闪烁了一下。
A faint light returns to her dull, weary eyes.

红弩箭：你和5号先带她回城里。等一切都结束了，我们会送她回家。
Lilya: Take her to Bereggrad along with Alpha Five. We'll bring her home once the battle's over.

红弩箭：其他人……任务继续，我们必须找到最后一个节点，彻底破坏重塑之手的术式。
Lilya: The rest of us will keep looking for the last rite. Mission's clear: the Manus must be stopped.

红弩箭：天空不是万全的庇护所，时刻注意来自地面的埋伏。我不希望阿尔法2号的悲剧再重演。
Lilya: I want everyone watching for threats from the ground at all times. We can't let this happen again.

红弩箭目送白鸽们再次列队起飞。
She watches as the team forms up and rises again.

红弩箭：……
Lilya: ...

红弩箭：**的[斯拉夫粗口]……
Lilya: Goddammit!

直到那些白色的影子冲进云层，她才长长叹了一口气，猛地蹲了下来，把脸埋进了手里。
Only when they disappear into the clouds does she let out a deep sigh, her back sinking as she buries her face in her hands.

红弩箭：喂，头儿。
Lilya: Hey, Captain.

维尔汀：一切都还好吗，红弩箭？
Vertin: Are you alright, Lilya?

维尔汀：过去的一小时里，我和十四行诗一直在试图和你取得联络。
Vertin: Sonetto and I have been trying to contact you for the past hour.

红弩箭：呼……抱歉，头儿。刚刚我被重塑之手的家伙缠住了。
Lilya: *phew* Sorry, Manus rats kept me busy.

红弩箭：……
Lilya: ...

红弩箭：别列格勒城东南42英里坐标点，飞行中队遭到了重塑之手的伏击，阿尔法2号未能返航。
Lilya: About 42 miles southeast of Bereggrad, my squadron was ambushed by the Manus. Alpha Two didn't make it.

维尔汀：……节哀。
Vertin: My condolences.

悲伤与焦虑的情绪也在此处蔓延。帐外传来夜风般的呜咽，将帐中的沉重又加深了几分。
A heavy grief and anxiety hangs between them, the silence only deepened by the moaning wind outside.

维尔汀：我们也有坏消息。
Vertin: We've got some bad news of our own.

维尔汀：从午夜起，塞契指挥部陆续失去了和前线骑兵部队的联络。
Vertin: Around midnight, the command post lost contact with the frontline cavalry.

维尔汀：同时我们也没有再收到任何来自城里的消息。
Vertin: We haven't heard anything from Bereggrad either.

军长伊万：顿河沿岸燃起了烽火，可能还有幸存者。但需要飞行中队的各位从空中确认情况。
Commander Ivan: Scouts reported flares upriver. There may yet be survivors. A flight unit's eyes would tell us for certain.

红弩箭：我明白了。那城里怎么办？
Lilya: I'm on it. What about the city?

旁听着一切的叛军将领从沙盘边站了起来。
Igor stands up from the sand table.

伊戈尔：配合民兵守城的是我的人，我必须亲自去确认情况。
Igor: My soldiers are responsible for the city's defense. I will go there myself to assess the situation.

斯捷尔诺娃：你答应过要留在塞契，伊戈尔。
Sternova: You promised to stay in the sich, Igor.

伊戈尔：是，可现在前线与城镇同时失联，飞行部队在城郊遇袭，敌军却依然神出鬼没、动向不明。
Igor: A promise I intended to keep. But as you can see, we're struggling on multiple fronts, and our enemy remains hidden.

伊戈尔：在座的各位都知道这意味着什么——临时联军的全线溃败已近在眼前。
Igor: We all know this coalition's collapse is imminent. We must act.

斯捷尔诺娃：……
Sternova: ...

军长没有犹豫多久，率先采取了行动。
After a beat, the commander speaks.

军长伊万：……我去给你选一匹快马。
Commander Ivan: I'll lend you a horse.

伊戈尔：这很有帮助，但我需要的不只是一匹马。
Igor: Appreciated, but I will need more than that.

军长伊万：你还想要什么。
Commander Ivan: What is it?

伊戈尔：这个。
Igor: This.

伊戈尔抬起手，露出神秘术抑制咒文。
Igor reveals the arcanum-suppressing runes on his arm.

军长伊万：呵……总是让人在绝路中做选择，这就是你的策略？
Commander Ivan: Hmph, always offering a devil's bargain. Another clause in that twisted code of yours?

通讯器的噪声停了下来，营帐在一片骇人的沉默中下沉。
The static from the communicator fades, leaving the tent in a dreadful silence.

军长伊万：你又想摆弄你的萤火虫了？
Commander Ivan: Not thinking of playing with your fireflies again, are you?

军长伊万：别列格勒和“那里”不一样，轰炸无法解决这里的问题。有将近十万居民选择留在家里，和别列格勒共进退。
Commander Ivan: Bereggrad is unlike "that battlefield." Tens of thousands have stayed in the city. Raining fire from above will do us no good.

伊戈尔：呵……
Igor: Heh. No!

他低头看向手中的萤火虫罐，里面的光点正上下翻飞着闪烁。
He looks down at the jar in his hand. The fireflies inside flicker and flutter.

伊戈尔：我会在合适的时机与地点打开突破口。相信我，我唯一的目标只有打赢这场战斗。
Igor: I will take action only at the right time and place. Our goals remain the same: to win this battle for everyone.

军长伊万：……
Commander Ivan: ...

军长伊万：斯捷尔诺娃，去替我把马牵来。
Commander Ivan: My horse, Sternova.

斯捷尔诺娃：军长……
Sternova: Commander ...

她没有继续说下去，而是转身离开。
She silences herself, furrows her brow, and leaves.

斯捷尔诺娃走后，军长苦笑一声，用食指关节敲了敲桌面。伊戈尔将手臂摆在伊万指示的地方。
The commander turns to Igor with a wry smile and taps the table with his knuckle. Igor places his arm on the spot.

伊万拔出匕首，以尖端刺破伊戈尔镌有咒文的皮肤。刀尖的神秘术辉光忽明忽灭，如同风中影影绰绰的烛光。
With a drawn dagger, Ivan pricks the rune-inscribed skin. The blade glows with arcane energy, flickering like a candle in a draft.

军长伊万：那匹马是我的老战友，我养了很多年。
Commander Ivan: That horse has carried me for years.

不断渗出的血珠逐渐汇成殷红的溪流，顺着紧绷的肌肉向下流淌。操作匕首的人并未因此有丝毫怜悯。
Blood wells up, flowing over taut muscle. But the hand holding the knife feels no pity.

军长伊万：温顺，但是很勇敢，而且无比忠诚。只要骑手给它下达了指令，它会毫不犹豫地冲向最危险的地方。
Commander Ivan: Steady. Brave. A loyal companion. Give the command, and he will charge into hell.

冰冷的金属已在血中浸得滚烫，帐外已经隐约能听见战马的嘶鸣。
The cold steel warms with blood as the gentle neighing of warhorses reaches their ears.

军长伊万：可它喝不惯草原外边儿的水……记得带它回家。
Commander Ivan: But he's not used to the water beyond the steppe. Make sure you bring him home.

12TH-19 牺牲简报 / Casualty Report

所有人都认得这张苍老的脸，记得是谁带来了炮火，却也知道是谁在保护他们。
They all know this aged face. He is the one who brought the gunfire and the one who now guards them.

守城民兵没有难为伊戈尔，甚至为他指出了留守城内的狮鹫军新的驻扎地。
The militia allows Igor to pass, even guiding him to where the Gryphons are now quartered.

伊戈尔：你还记得在芝诺学到的东西，我感觉很欣慰，托勒密。
Igor: I'm glad to see you still remember Zeno's teachings, Ptolemy.

伊戈尔：面临轰炸威胁时，要让非防空部队的人进入地下……
Igor: When facing a bombardment, we move all vulnerable units under—

让他失了声的除了这彻底的静默外，还有几具被白布收殓着的尸体。
Silence. A row of bodies under white sheets.

他们的眼睛上都放着两颗压住眼皮的方糖。托勒密坐在后面的椅子上，整个人沉在阴霾中。
On each pair of eyes rest two sugar cubes pressing their lids shut. Ptolemy sits behind them, shrouded in a dark shadow.

托勒密：父亲……您来了……
Ptolemy: Father ...

伊戈尔：他们战死在哪儿？
Igor: How did they die?

托勒密双手颤抖，垂着头，试图将表情藏在阴影里。
His son stares at the ground, unwilling to show his face. Only his trembling hands betray his emotion.

狮鹫军士兵：简报已经整理出来了，请您过目……
Gryphon Soldier: Here's a written report. For your review, Admiral.

伊戈尔没有去接那几张染着血的纸。
Igor does not take the bloodied papers.

伊戈尔：让他说。
Igor: I will hear it from him.

伊戈尔：把头抬起来看着我，托勒密。告诉我你作为这次行动的城防指挥官，都做了些什么。
Igor: Raise your head, Ptolemy. Tell me your course of action as the commander of the city operation.

伊戈尔的语气平静，却让在场所有人都不寒而栗。
He speaks calmly, but it sends a chill through the room.

托勒密：是、是……
Ptolemy: Y-Yes.

托勒密：昨日午后四时，我们和民兵团、骑士团一起剿灭了数支潜入城内的重塑之手步兵班。
Ptolemy: Around sixteen hundred hours yesterday, we coordinated with the militia and Cavalry Corps to eliminate several Manus infantry squads that had infiltrated the city.

伊戈尔：这点在昨天的最后一次通讯中已经传达过了。
Igor: You already reported that during our last communication.

伊戈尔：我想知道的是，在通讯被切断后发生了什么。
Igor: And after the signal was jammed?

托勒密：我……
Ptolemy: I ...

托勒密：为了排查通讯故障的原因，我派出了一支……包括了五名神秘学步兵和两名通信兵的临时战术小队，由雅罗斯拉夫·列夫丘克担任队长。
Ptolemy: I dispatched an ad hoc squad to investigate the source of the signal interference. Five arcanist infantry troopers and two technicians. Yaroslav Levchuk was the squad leader.

伊戈尔：除了排障外，你还下达了什么指令？
Igor: What else did you order them to do?

被父亲亲手撕开遮羞布，托勒密感觉自己的脸因羞愧而发烫，头脑的热度却因恐惧降至冰点。
His father has torn away the veil. While shame burns Ptolemy's face, fear freezes his words.

托勒密：我让他们……潜入了林地。
Ptolemy: I-I ordered them to sneak into the forest.

托勒密：我让他们不计代价找到对方指挥官的动向，找到……格鲁托夫。
Ptolemy: To find traces of Krutov at any cost.

托勒密：……
Ptolemy: ...

托勒密：其中六人的尸身由敌军送了回来，保留了完整的尸身。
Ptolemy: And then, six corpses were delivered to the entrance of our base.

伊戈尔：你的大脑被无用的仇恨塞满了，托勒密。再这样下去，我很难将狮鹫军未来的指挥重任托付于你。
Igor: You allowed yourself to be blinded with hatred, Ptolemy. How can I entrust you with the Gryphon Legion if you can't maintain a steady hand?

托勒密：……是，父亲，是我的判断有误。我愿意接受所有惩罚。
Ptolemy: I know, Father. I made a grave mistake. I will accept whatever punishment you see fit.

他顿了顿，残留在眼眶中的疼痛让他罕见地在父亲面前露出了不甘心的神色。
He pauses, the ache in his left eye socket betraying a resentment rarely shown in front of his father.

托勒密：可格鲁托夫——他就躲在那些漆黑的林子里！躲在装甲车后面！
Ptolemy: But Krutov ... I saw him! He was right there, hiding in the woods!

托勒密：我离他很近了，近到我能看到他嘴角浮现着的、令人厌烦的傲慢弧度！看到他在帐篷里用古典乐掩盖着战场轰鸣的做作姿态！
Ptolemy: I was so close I could see that arrogant sneer of his, hear the incessant classical music playing from his tent!

托勒密：您知道他对我……对我们做了什么！！
Ptolemy: You know what he did to me, to us!

托勒密：每当听到他的名字，我都能感觉到那如同乌鸦啄食般的痛……
Ptolemy: Every time I hear that wretched name, my eye aches with unbearable pain.

陌生的天花板，强烈的阵痛，以及失去一半的视野。
A strange ceiling. A sharp, throbbing pain. Half the world has gone dark.

托勒密：……？！！
Ptolemy: ...?!

托勒密：队医！队医没给我打吗啡吗？！
Ptolemy: Agh, ah, medic! Medic! I need morphine!

莫莉德尔：已经用过药了，托勒密。
Moldir: They just gave you some, Ptolemy.

托勒密：莫莉德尔……发生了什么？我们的车队被诡雷给……？
Ptolemy: Moldir, what happened? Did our convoy hit a booby trap?

莫莉德尔：不是诡雷。
Moldir: No, not a booby trap.

莫莉德尔：敌人伪装成平民，藏在必经之路旁的田地里。他们浑身捆满了炼金辉光管，冲向了你乘坐的运兵车。
Moldir: Enemies disguised as civilians were lurking by the farms you passed through. No one expected them to be hiding explosive Blazefuse cylinders beneath their clothes.

托勒密：……我想起来了。我的眼睛什么时候能痊愈？
Ptolemy: Right, right. I remember. My eye ... When will it be healed?

莫莉德尔：……
Moldir: ...

莫莉德尔：左眼视网膜被高温辉光重度灼伤，我会负责你的康复训练。在此之前，你先安心养伤。
Moldir: The retina in your left eye took a severe burn in the explosion. I'll see to it that you recover as much as possible. For now, just rest.

他知道这代表着什么，他未来将不得不换到另一侧持枪。
He understands what this means. He'll have to learn to fire from his other shoulder.

托勒密：格鲁托夫上尉呢？他和我在同一台车上。
Ptolemy: Is Captain Krutov alright? We were in the same car.

莫莉德尔：多亏了你把他及时推下了车，上尉只是受了点脑震荡。
Moldir: He only suffered a mild concussion, thanks to you. I doubt he would have survived if you hadn't pushed him off in time.

莫莉德尔：……你先休息，我去叫队医来给你加药。
Moldir: You should sleep, brother. I'll ask the medic to increase your dosage.

托勒密用力地拽住了她的胳膊。
Ptolemy grips her arm tightly.

托勒密：告诉我，我们胜利了吗？
Ptolemy: Did we win?

莫莉德尔：当然。父亲的战略获得了成功，我们成功摧毁了敌军后方的指挥部，在第四战场上大获全胜。
Moldir: Of course. Father's strategy was effective as always. We destroyed the enemy command post. We took sector four decisively.

托勒密：……那就好。
Ptolemy: Good.

托勒密：你也去休息吧，莫莉。不用叫军医了，我不需要吗啡了。
Ptolemy: You need to rest too, Molly. And don't send for the medic. I don't need morphine anymore.

托勒密：我们从南极离开时，有人试图从你行囊里偷走的文件，我全看过了。
Ptolemy: As we left Antarctica, I saw the documents those traitors tried to steal from your bag.

托勒密：那次刺杀是格鲁托夫的自导自演。他骗过了我们所有人的眼睛，目的是促使基金会通过高危神秘学武器使用许可的审查。
Ptolemy: I learned what Krutov did—staging an assassination on himself, making it look like an enemy ambush—just to pressure the Foundation into approving the use of high-risk arcane weapons!

托勒密：在他的计划中，我是牺牲名单的头号对象——如果不是我“多此一举”地把他推下车，让刺杀者犹豫了片刻的话。
Ptolemy: Killing me was part of his plan all along! I only survived because the assassin hesitated when I tried to save him!

托勒密：父亲，您为什么要瞒着我？
Ptolemy: Father, why did you keep this from me?

伊戈尔：真相只会让你被愤怒冲昏头脑，就像你现在犯下的错误一样。
Igor: Anger would only cloud your judgment, as proved with your actions.

伊戈尔：你会有亲手剜出他的眼睛的机会的，我向你保证。
Igor: You will have your revenge, an eye for an eye. I promise you.

伊戈尔：但现在，你必须记住他们的牺牲和你必须背负的责任。
Igor: But now, you must bear responsibility for your mistakes and honor the sacrifice of your brothers.

伊戈尔：这些人放弃了过往的荣耀，放弃了身份，放弃了存在的证明。他们舍弃了一切，选择了将未来交到我的手上。
Igor: They gave up past glory, identity, and every proof of their existence for us, entrusting the future into my hands.

伊戈尔：离开圣保罗后，我已经说得很清楚了。
Igor: Do you not remember what I told you after leaving São Paulo?

伊戈尔：“不会有更多无意义的牺牲，不会有新的背离。”作为我的代言人之一，你必须比任何人都铭记这一点。
Igor: No more meaningless sacrifices. We don't leave anyone behind. You speak with my voice; you should remember this more than anyone.

托勒密：……
Ptolemy: ...

托勒密：我会的，父亲。
Ptolemy: I will, Father.

托勒密摸了摸眼罩后灼痛的眼睛。他默默地点了点头，试图让自己恢复冷静。
Ptolemy touches the bandage over his burning eye socket and nods, willing himself to remain steady.

伊戈尔：那些噪声是什么？我以为格鲁托夫的袭击已经彻底切断了通讯。
Igor: What's that noise? I thought communications were severed after Krutov's assault.

托勒密：在您抵达的半小时前，我们设法重新架设了信号天线，但只接收到了一段带有敌方信号特征的频率。
Ptolemy: We managed to reestablish a signal. It's been up nearly half an hour, but the only thing it's picked up is some bizarre enemy frequency.

托勒密：情报专员认为那极有可能是某种干扰手段。因此对它设置了屏蔽，然后就变成了这种……噪音。
Ptolemy: The operators think it's some form of interference intended to jam our signals, so they've muted it.

伊戈尔：你是说……来自格鲁托夫军的电台？来自——重塑之手的信号？
Igor: You mean this noise is a signal from Krutov's army, from Manus Vindictae?

托勒密：呃……理论上而言，的确如此。
Ptolemy: Well, in theory, yes.

伊戈尔：接通它，立刻。
Igor: Bring it up and unmute it! Now!

托勒密：是！
Ptolemy: Yes, sir!

他迅速地解除了所有屏蔽干扰的频段，将音量旋钮转至最大。
He cuts all the jamming signals at once and turns the volume to its maximum.

“敌方电台”接通了。背景中，枪林弹雨的声音隐约可闻。
The "enemy radio station" crackles to life. Faint gunfire sounds in the background.

？？？：鹰隼06呼叫鹰巢，鹰隼06呼叫鹰巢。第……四十五次呼叫，收到请回答！
???: Falcon 6 calling the nest. Falcon 6 calling the nest. This is the 45th call. Please respond!

？？？：……接通了？！听得到吗？！有人吗？
???: Huh? What? Is it connected? Command, do you copy?

伊戈尔：是的，我能听到你的声音。
Igor: We read you loud and clear.

伊戈尔：我是狮鹫军总指挥伊戈尔，请汇报。
Igor: This is your commander. Report your status.

12TH-20 最后的防线 / The Last Defense

列夫丘克：太好了，是将军！
Levchuk: Good to hear your voice, Admiral!

托勒密：列夫丘克？！你——你还活着？
Ptolemy: Is that Levchuk? You're still alive?

列夫丘克：没有时间寒暄了，敌方集团军正在向河南岸靠拢，装甲已经开进了红柳树村——
Levchuk: This is urgent. Enemy forces are marching toward the southern bank. Their armored convoy has already reached Tamarovka!

列夫丘克：至少两个装甲师和一个陆军师的兵力，此外还有三个辅助炮兵团。
Levchuk: There are at least two armored divisions and one infantry division, plus three artillery regiments!

伊戈尔：了解，我已收到你的汇报。
Igor: Roger. Good work.

电台的那一侧，对方显然松了一口气，并瘫软在地上。
The man on the other end collapses to the floor with relief.

背景中的枪声隐约变得更清晰——伊戈尔希望那是一种错觉。
The gunfire in the background sharpens. Igor hopes it's just his mind playing tricks on him.

伊戈尔：报告你的位置，上士。我会立刻派人营救你。
Igor: Report your position, Staff Sergeant. A squad will be sent to your rescue immediately.

电台另一侧的人沉默许久，然后笑了一下。
A long silence follows, then a soft laugh.

背景的枪弹声显而易见地变得更近，更令人……恐惧。子弹仿佛掠过了耳边。
The gunfire grows closer, unmistakably so. Bullets seem to be tearing right past the receiver.

伊戈尔：现在情况如何，你是否预留了撤退的道路？
Igor: Have you secured your retreat?

列夫丘克：……
Levchuk: ...

列夫丘克：报告长官，雅罗斯拉夫·列夫丘克顺利完成了任务。
Levchuk: Commander, I—Staff Sergeant Yaroslav Levchuk—have successfully completed my task.

托勒密急不可耐地挤到了送话器跟前。
Ptolemy pushes his way to the speaker.

托勒密：什么意思？你**[狮鹫军粗口]的不准放弃，不准死！我现在就去带你回来！
Ptolemy: What are you saying? Goddammit! Don't you die on me! I'm coming to bring you back right now!

列夫丘克：托勒密，你这臭小子。别再给将军添麻烦了。
Levchuk: Stop causing trouble for the admiral, you hear, Ptolemy?

炮弹声逐渐盖过了上士的声音。
Artillery begins to drown out the staff sergeant's voice.

列夫丘克：我从不后悔成为您麾下的士兵，将军。
Levchuk: It has been a true honor serving under you, sir. I have no regrets.

“嘟——嘟——嘟。”
*beep ... beep ... beep ...*

电台信号在枪声中消失了。
As the gunfire swells, the signal is cut off.

沉重的喘息声也随之消失了。
Along with the heavy breathing of their comrade.

伊戈尔：整备部队，托勒密。除防空炮手外所有人，撤出别列格勒。
Igor: Reorganize the troops, Ptolemy. All units save the anti-air squads are to evacuate from Bereggrad.

托勒密：撤出别列格勒？要退回安全屋吗？
Ptolemy: Evacuate Bereggrad? To where? The safehouse?

伊戈尔：不，向骑兵军塞契集结。
Igor: No, to the Cavalry Corps's sich.

伊戈尔：格鲁托夫从我们这里带走的东西，我们要让他一一吐出来。
Igor: We will make Krutov return everything he stole from us.

狮鹫军带来了最坏的消息。
The Gryphons bring the worst news.

军长咽下了悲痛，让写满牺牲数字的简报消失在炭火中。
The commander swallows his grief and feeds the casualty list to the coals.

塞契沉浸在一片肃穆中时，他已经做出了判断。
In the solemn silence of the sich, he has already made his decision.

军长伊万：红柳树村会是格鲁托夫攻城的关键。
Commander Ivan: Tamarovka is the keystone of Krutov's plan.

军长伊万：一旦失守，城市将直接暴露给一支火力凶猛的神秘学装甲部队。装甲师最依赖的是供给线……需要有人去掐断这条命脉。
Commander Ivan: If it falls, Bereggrad will face a formidable arcanist force with armored vehicles. If only we had cut off their supply lines ...

伊戈尔：我有办法带人从内部奇袭红柳树村。
Igor: The Legion can launch a raid from inside Tamarovka. They won't see it coming.

斯捷尔诺娃：纵使狮鹫军有村内捣毁敌人部队的能力……
Sternova: Even if your Gryphons could strike the enemy undetected ...

参谋长第三次从沙盘的这头踱步到另一头。
The chief of staff paces the length of the sand table for the third time.

斯捷尔诺娃：但谁去阻挡格鲁托夫源源不断的补给线？
Sternova: They won't hold long if Krutov keeps getting supplies and reinforcements. We have to cut them off, but how?

托勒密：我看塞契里还有很多牵马的骑兵，他们能不能——
Ptolemy: I saw plenty of soldiers standing out by their horses. Couldn't they—

斯捷尔诺娃：都是孩子！
Sternova: They're only kids!

斯捷尔诺娃双手砸在了桌上，冲击让用来推演的棋子纷纷移了位。
Sternova slams her hands on the table, scattering the markers.

斯捷尔诺娃：十八岁以上的骑兵第一波出征就派出去了。
Sternova: All the grown men rode out in the first sortie.

斯捷尔诺娃：剩下的都是些为了一口饱饭，谎报年纪混进来的小孩，连握缰的茧都没磨出来，嫩得和刚出壳的潜鸭没两样。
Sternova: Most of them lied about their age, just trying to get a good meal. Their hands haven't even been toughened by the reins yet. They're boys! Not soldiers.

军长伊万：莎宾娜。
Commander Ivan: Sabina.

军长拍了拍她的背，推着她走到了营帐之外。
The commander pats her back and ushers her out of the tent.

少年们披挂着空荡的军服，步枪背带深勒进单薄的肩胛，马刀鞘尾拖拽在未长硬的腿骨旁。
The boys stand in their oversized uniforms, rifle straps digging into their thin shoulders, shashka scabbards dragging against their soft legs.

他们静立如一片削瘦的黑杨林，稚嫩的喉结在绷紧的领口下滚动，却只为塞契带来了沉默。
They stand quietly, their throats working under tight collars.

这种沉默压制住了她的怒火。
Their silence suppresses her anger.

斯捷尔诺娃：你们知道自己在做什么吗？
Sternova: Do you understand what you're facing?

斯捷尔诺娃：跨上战马，离开家乡，然后死在战场上……之后再也回不了家。
Sternova: In all likelihood, you'll die on the battlefield. You'll never see home again.

少年骑兵Ⅰ：您别小看我了！我可是哥萨克，和我的哥哥、姐姐、爸爸、妈妈一样！
Teen Cavalryman I: Don't take me for a kid, ma'am! I'm a Cossack, like my brother, sister, and my parents before me!

少年骑兵Ⅱ：是啊！我身体里流着骑兵的血，这是英雄的血！
Teen Cavalryman II: Ura! The blood of the Cossacks—of heroes—runs through me!

斯捷尔诺娃：……
Sternova: ...

少年骑兵Ⅰ：我们是哥萨克，哥萨克从来不怕上战场。
Teen Cavalryman I: We may be young, but our blood is strong. No Cossack fears the battlefield!

少年骑兵Ⅰ：就算断手断脚也没什么可怕的。家乡的命运得我们来决定！这是必要的牺牲！
Teen Cavalryman I: If it means losing a hand, a leg, or even our lives, we'll do anything, make any sacrifice, to protect our homeland!

伊戈尔：……
Igor: ...

似曾相识的话语撞击在情感的底线上。
Those familiar words strike her deep.

军长伊万：你看见了，伊戈尔。
Commander Ivan: See, Igor?

军长伊万：我会带领这支队伍撵走那些戴面具的疯子。
Commander Ivan: These soldiers will drive those masked lunatics from the steppe.

军长伊万：我要把这片土地还给这些孩子们，把未来交到他们手上——这个时代的顿河，并不由我们来定义。
Commander Ivan: Her future rests with the young. We old-timers have no right to shape this era.

军长红着眼睛，看向这些消瘦的影子。
The commander, eyes red, looks over these thin shadows.

军长伊万：我们会取得胜利。告诉我这一点。
Commander Ivan: Tell me, great riders of the steppe, will victory be ours today?

少年骑兵Ⅰ：我们会取得胜利！
Teen Cavalryman I: Victory will be ours!

少年骑兵Ⅱ：我们会把那些疯子赶出我们的家！
Teen Cavalryman II: We'll drive these madmen from our home!

未变声的呼喊如汛期的顿河浪潮般层层叠叠，凿穿了塞契的每一寸垛口。
Unbroken voices rise like the flow of the Don in spring, crashing into every corner of the sich.

军长回过头，对上叛军首领深沉的目光。
The commander looks back, meeting the heavy gaze of the rebel leader.

军长伊万：伊戈尔，这是我们最后的机会了。
Commander Ivan: Igor, this is our last chance.

他的手在颤抖，周围所有人都看得一清二楚。
His hands are noticeably quivering.

但无人指摘他的战栗。
But no one blames him for it.

12TH-21 将军与他的部下们 / The Admiral and His Men

重型装甲从河道交汇之处的浅滩开进了红柳树村。
Heavy armor rolls into Tamarovka through the river shallows.

履带碾碎了村口石砌的路面，桥边的百年红柳也被装甲行过的热浪持续灼烤，风再吹过时，灰烬纷纷从炭化的枝条上剥离。
Treads grind the village's stone road to dust. The heat from the machines scorches the old willows by the bridge, the following rush of wind peeling the ash from them.

谢尔盖：……
Sergey: ...

谢尔盖和其他神秘学家俘虏正被重塑之手的术士押着向村中走。
Sergey and the other captive arcanists are being marched to the village by the Manus ritualist.

意图反抗的人都和冻土下的腐殖质融为了一体，沉默和温驯现在成了这支俘虏队伍的代名词。
Those who fought now feed the frozen earth. Silence and obedience reign.

俘虏：你又在瞎看什么？
Captive: Hey. What are you looking around for?

借着火炮车队从身边隆隆驶过的机会，年长的俘虏低声斥责起了谢尔盖。
As the guns rumble past, an older captive hisses at Sergey.

尽管术士就紧跟在队列最后，鞭子随时会再一次落在身上，路过姑父家附近时，谢尔盖还是忍不住抻长了脖子。
Despite the ritualist's brandishing of her whip close behind, Sergey strains to look as they pass near his uncle's house.

谢尔盖：我……我是这村里的人。
Sergey: I ... I'm from this village.

俘虏：噢，节哀。
Captive: Oh. I'm sorry.

谢尔盖：嘿……！
Sergey: Hey!

谢尔盖：别急着唱衰，出征前军长让咱们回了趟家，很多人都得到消息往城里去了。他们现在肯定没事。
Sergey: Don't say things like that! I'm sure most of the villagers fled to the city before all this happened.

“——啪！”
*crack*

铭文鞭的钢棱砸进了谢尔盖的脊背，皮肉在重击下绽开。血顺着鞭体凹槽倒流，在古老的铭文上覆了层温热的釉。
She lashes at Sergey's back, tearing flesh. Blood runs down the grooves of the whip, coating the inscriptions in a shimmering scarlet glaze.

仪式术士：别交头接耳。
Ritualist: Keep quiet!

疼痛让谢尔盖吞下了自己的舌头。
The pain renders him silent.

铭文烙下的血痕如奇迹般切断了他与灵性间的通道，让神秘学家捉摸不定的大脑落在了地上，疼痛也因此变得更为明晰。
The blood-stained runes sever his link to pneuma, sending his arcane mind crashing to the ground and intensifying the pain.

年长的神秘学家俘虏搀扶着谢尔盖，将身体压得极低，让他们成为沉默队伍中又一个安静的真空带。
The older arcanist supports him. They bend low together, another silent pocket in the procession.

格鲁托夫从一辆装甲车里走出，皱眉看向这支俘虏队伍。
Krutov steps out from an armored car, a heavy frown on his face.

格鲁托夫：河岸边有些淤泥需要处理，不然会阻碍后续军队抵达村庄的速度。这帮神秘学家里有没有拿得出手的？
Krutov: I need hands to clear the sludge from the riverbank, or it'll slow our advance. Put some of these captured arcanists to work, understand?

仪式术士：恐怕他们帮不上忙，将军。遵您的指令，我暂时没有让他们接受复苏之母的试炼。
Ritualist: It would be my pleasure, General, but I'm afraid they'll be of little use. Per your previous command, I have yet to put them through Her Benevolence's trial.

指腹缓移过金属鞭上的棱槽。在凹陷处形成釉质层的半凝血在纹路上重新漫开。她缓慢而虔诚地抚摸着铭文，像在确认某种受难仪式的接口。
She glides her thumb over the whip's ridges, the coagulating blood smearing over the grain. She touches the inscriptions slowly, reverently, as if to confirm the channeling of some sacred affliction.

仪式术士：为避免节外生枝，我祈求祂降下福祉，让他们不再与灵性谐振。
Ritualist: And to avoid complications, I've prayed for Her blessing to ensure their pneuma remains completely dormant.

格鲁托夫：那你要把他们带去哪里？
Krutov: Then, where on earth are you taking them?

仪式术士：哦……摆弄一些神秘学道具，山楂枯枝、红石竹花、冬青叶，或许再来一些魔鬼手指孢子……
Ritualist: Oh, just a small trip to the wilderness to harvest some hawthorn twigs, red carnations, holly leaves, and, if possible, a few devil's finger mushrooms.

仪式术士：如果只是硬化河道的话，我也可以代劳。
Ritualist: If you need to hasten the march, I could provide you a shortcut by freezing part of the river.

格鲁托夫：你还会这样的神秘术？
Krutov: You know such a skill?

仪式术士：不值一提的小把戏而已。但代价是这片土地三年内长不出一粒麦子。
Ritualist: It's no great feat, really, but it comes at a small price. The soil we stand on will be utterly infertile for three years.

仪式术士：如何？您想要榨干这里的最后一滴血吗？
Ritualist: So? Do you wish to drain the life from this place?

格鲁托夫：无所谓。不过是个活不过冬天的村子。
Krutov: Hmph, as if I'd give a damn about some pitiful village.

格鲁托夫扬了扬下巴，示意术士行动。
Krutov lifts his chin to signal the ritualist to act.

格鲁托夫：被我们灭口的骑兵军还不是全部，等剩下的人反应过来了，一定会集结兵力向车队发起反攻，我们必须在那之前抢占先机。
Krutov: We've already eliminated most of the Zeno cavalry, but their remnants will likely attempt to regroup and make another attack. We must take the battle to them before they get the chance.

格鲁托夫：绞紧河床，把它雕成伊戈尔的坟墓。
Krutov: Let the river freeze, and we will carve it as Igor's tomb!

术士笑着应了声“是”。
She smiles a "yes."

在她将要举起鞭子驱赶俘虏时，空气啸叫着被撕开数道裂口。
As the whip is cracked, the air tears with a shriek.

灰白鸽群在上空划破积云，尾迹拖出一道道猎猎旌旗，风声向大地宣告一曲镇魂歌。
A flight of pointed hats splits the clouds above, their trails streaming like banners.

红弩箭：我看见格鲁托夫了！
Lilya: It's Krutov. I spotted the bastard!

红弩箭下压飞行器，整支飞行队伍在她的带领下应声收拢，如利箭般刺破寂静。
Lilya dips her broomstick, and the formation tightens into a sharp arrow behind her.

红弩箭：打击坐标：桥头枯树三点钟方向。目标视觉确认，全员解除保险栓！
Lilya: To me, Alpha team! Target confirmed at three o'clock from the dead tree at the bridge! Weapons hot!

飞行巫师们纷纷拉下护目镜，鸽群如白色流星般加速掠过战场。
The Flying Witches lower their goggles and dive like white shooting stars over the battlefield.

红弩箭：把他们的车给我炸上天！
Lilya: Let's blow them to hell!

渡鸦-3型火龙燃素燃烧弹从天而降，砸向重塑之手的车队。
Raven-3 Pyrodrake Phlogiston Incendiaries rain down on the Manus forces.

重塑士兵：这是什么——
Manus Soldier: What?

短暂的倒计时结束后，火焰从龙血弹中喷薄而出，精准地从观察口爬进装甲车内。
After a brief pause, flames pour from the firedragons, crawling into the armored cars through their observation ports.

重塑士兵：呃……啊……啊啊！
Manus Soldier: Aah! Ahhhh!

火焰骤然咬住钢铁骨架，漆黑的车体转瞬间被火舌包裹。
The black cage is engulfed in seconds.

火光照亮了拖车俘虏们伤痕累累的脊梁，片刻的愣神后，他们就像被烫伤的狼群一样撞进荒原。
The glow illuminates the bloodied faces of the captives. After a stunned moment, they break for the open land like wolves fleeing a burning forest.

重塑军官：俘虏跑了！
Manus Officer: Captives are getting away.

军官对着俘虏逃向生还与自由的背影连开数枪。
An officer fires at their backs, the whip gashes illuminated by the flames as they make their desperate bid for freedom.

有人扑倒在地，再无声息。也有人踉跄几步后，又坚定地奔向村外。
Some fall, while others stumble on to the outskirts of the village.

格鲁托夫：别把子弹浪费在牲畜身上。
Krutov: Don't waste your bullets.

格鲁托夫抬手制止了戴面具的军官，抬头看向借着云层掩护越行越远的白色流星群。
Krutov raises a hand, stopping the masked officer. He looks up at the white specks fading into the clouds.

格鲁托夫：飞行巫师就一个中队。通知空中部队，把这些苍蝇打下来。
Krutov: There are only a few of these flying pests. Call the air units to take them down.

重塑军官：你其他的作战单位呢？
Manus Officer: Where's the rest of your army?

格鲁托夫抬手指向远处若隐若现的城市轮廓。
Krutov points toward the hazy outline of the city in the distance.

格鲁托夫：按照原计划，向别列格勒进军。
Krutov: They're marching on Bereggrad as we speak.

重塑军官：既然要拿下红柳树村，为什么不集中所有力量？
Manus Officer: If you wanna capture Tamarovka, why not concentrate your forces?

格鲁托夫：我们已经剿灭了半数的骑兵军，等到城市沦陷，芝诺胆小鬼的士气就该崩溃了，他们不会再敢包庇伊戈尔。
Krutov: Over half the Zeno cavalrymen are gone. When my men storm the city, they will crumble at my feet, and Igor will be mine.

重塑军官：呵，但愿一切都会像你说的这样顺利……我该去找我的人了。
Manus Officer: Heh, let's hope everything goes as smoothly as you say. I'll be taking my leave now.

军官转过身，一步踩进了一块松软的虚无里，点点萤火从液化的地面飞出。
The officer turns, his foot sinking into soft, false earth. Fireflies rise from the liquid ground.

重塑军官：这是……？
Manus Officer: What's this?

仪式术士：是死亡女巫的术阵痕迹！快从那里走开！
Ritualist: A Baba Yaga ritual! Step away from it!

格鲁托夫：……！
Krutov: ...!

格鲁托夫：……是你。
Krutov: You ...

伊戈尔：格鲁托夫，好久不见。
Igor: It's been a long time, Krutov.

格鲁托夫：独自前来拜访，这就是你的战术？把自己送进大军的包围中。
Krutov: Charging headfirst, alone, into the wolf's den—your tactical brilliance continues to astound.

格鲁托夫：伊戈尔——我那一如既往目中无人、自大自负的“朋友”。
Krutov: You haven't changed a bit, my friend. Arrogant and ignorant in equal measure.

伊戈尔：独自？不……
Igor: Alone? Heh, I'm afraid not.

伊戈尔：正好，我有些新朋友想要和你打声招呼。
Igor: Meet my new allies.

军长侧首与伊戈尔对视，二者同一时间颔首确认了战术。他翻身上马，对天鸣枪。
He and Commander Ivan share a firm nod.

军长伊万：——行动！
Commander Ivan: Move out!

骏马上的少年们高举马刀，用稚嫩的嗓音呼出出征的决心。
The boys rear their horses, their shashkas and voices raised high to the sky.

以术阵为圆心，骑兵军分头冲向了通向村外的坦途。马蹄掀翻了漆黑的士兵，枪与刀推倒了所有拦路的阻碍。
The cavalry splits. Charging down the clear paths leading out of the village, their guns, blades, and hooves shatter the Manus forces.

格鲁托夫：他们的方向——
Krutov: They're heading to ...

曾跟随近卫团南征北战的人只消片刻就读懂了伊戈尔的战术。
As a former member of the Sentinel Unit, it takes him only a moment to grasp Igor's tactic.

格鲁托夫：他们要去破坏我军的补给线！第三特种连！全力拦住骑兵！
Krutov: They're going to cut us off! Third company, stop those riders at once!

托勒密：狮鹫军——把重塑之手的步兵队拖在这里！
Ptolemy: Gryphons, pin down the Manus infantry!

格鲁托夫：托勒密中尉。
Krutov: Oh, Lieutenant Ptolemy.

格鲁托夫露出一个充满恶意的笑容，仿佛在嘲弄一只不自量力的幼兽。
Krutov smiles a cruel smile, as if mocking a cub that has overestimated its strength.

格鲁托夫：我希望你没有再受神经痛的折磨了。
Krutov: I hope you're not suffering too much from the pain where your eye should be.

托勒密：你这个叛徒——
Ptolemy: F**cking traitor!!

染血的马刀横在了格鲁托夫与托勒密之间。
A bloody shashka cuts through the air.

伊戈尔：退下，托勒密，现在还不到时候。
Igor: Hold back, Ptolemy. It's not time yet.

托勒密：……是，父亲。
Ptolemy: Yes, Father.

托勒密的妥协让格鲁托夫的笑意扩大，他以戏谑的神情在前近卫团军官的自尊上反复踩踏。
Ptolemy's surrender widens Krutov's grin. He treads on the pride of his former squadmate with almost gleeful mockery.

格鲁托夫：父亲最乖巧的孩子，需要父亲的帮助才敢开枪。
Krutov: Oh, what a pitiful boy. Can't even hold his gun steady without Daddy's help.

刀身破开了风，刀尖停留在了格鲁托夫身前三寸。
Another blade stops just three inches from Krutov's chest.

伊戈尔：我知道你很想亲手杀死我，格鲁托夫。
Igor: I know you've been dying to kill me, Krutov.

伊戈尔：现在，我来了，这是你唯一的机会。
Igor: Now's your chance.

12TH-22 顿河悲歌 / Elegy for the Don

见证了哥萨克百年历史的红柳树断了。
The red willow that has watched over the Cossacks for over a century lies fractured.

而本该温厚、坚实的大地在神秘术作用下化作黏稠的泥淖，死死咬住了伊戈尔的双腿。
The ground that should have been firm and warm has turned to a sticky mire, trapping Igor by the legs.

伊戈尔：……
Igor: ...

血顺着肌肉的纹路向下流淌，从死亡女巫处借来的力量为这具混血神秘学家的身体带来了超乎想象的负荷。
Blood courses through his already throbbing veins as the power borrowed from Baba Yaga puts an almost unbearable burden on his mixed-blood arcanist body.

伊戈尔：你的神秘术变强了。
Igor: You've grown stronger.

他如困兽般寸步难行，只能眼睁睁看着敌将的身影一步一步碾近。
Pinned like a hunted beast, he can only watch as the enemy commander approaches.

格鲁托夫：伊戈尔将军。
Krutov: Hm. Admiral Igor.

格鲁托夫在距离伊戈尔几步之遥的地方停下了。
Krutov stops a few paces away.

格鲁托夫：用过那个传送术阵后，你还能喘气，已经是奇迹了吧。
Krutov: Still catching your breath from the teleport ritual?

伊戈尔以沉重的喘息回答了他，但格鲁托夫知道，即使是在最后一刻，他也无法让这头骄傲的老狮子低头求饶。
Igor only glares, his chest heaving. Krutov knows this proud old lion will not plead, not even in his last moments.

格鲁托夫：我会给予你一场仁慈的解脱。
Krutov: Don't worry. I'll soon put you out of your misery.

格鲁托夫：但在这之前，我需要你回答我一个问题……
Krutov: But first, answer me one question.

拇指扳倒击锤，枪口对准伊戈尔的前额。
He cocks his gun, lining it up between Igor's eyes.

格鲁托夫：被困骨骸庭院时，是你救下了我们所有人。
Krutov: Back when we were chained in the Bone Garden, you saved us.

格鲁托夫：你与雅加婆婆——那个象征着死亡与巫术的女巫做了什么交易，才换得一群本该成为奴隶的人重获自由？
Krutov: What deal did you make with Baba Yaga—the old hag of death—to free us from slavery?

格鲁托夫：或者说，你用什么东西——换来了这些力量？这些不该属于一个混血种的力量，甚至让阿尔卡纳都愿意屈尊纡贵，与你做交易。
Krutov: Or rather, what did you trade for those extraordinary powers that even Arcana was willing to bargain for? Powers that don't belong to a mixed-blood like you.

伊戈尔：开枪。
Igor: Just shoot already.

格鲁托夫：事到如今，你还执着于保守当年的秘密吗？看来你早已在死亡与巫术的权柄中迷失了……我的老战友。
Krutov: Still clinging to your secrets? Seems you too have lost yourself to the witchcraft of death, my old comrade.

难以抑制的傲慢与轻蔑蔓延了他的整副面孔。
Scorn and arrogance shadow every inch of Krutov's face.

格鲁托夫：那就把这些东西带进坟墓吧。
Krutov: Fine, then take your secrets to the grave.

格鲁托夫：再见。
Krutov: Farewell.

阳光让他感到刺眼。
A flash of sunlight glints in his eyes.

不……那不是阳光。
No. That's not sunlight.

格鲁托夫：什——
Krutov: What?

格鲁托夫本能地抬头看向光源。
He instinctively looks up toward the light.

炼金辉光管被抛至空中，被激活的活性溶液正向外散发着热烈如恒星的光。
A Blazefuse cylinder is hurtling through the air, its active solution burning like a tiny sun.

“——砰！”
*bang*

隐匿在暗处的独眼狙击手射出了打碎太阳的子弹。
A one-eyed sniper fires, shattering it.

格鲁托夫：啊、啊……啊！！！
Krutov: Ugh! Ah. Aahhh!

滚烫的炼金溶液淋在了半边脸上，肌肉被炙烤的独特香气传入鼻腔后，痛觉才姗姗来迟。
Scalding alchemical fluid splashes over half of Krutov's face, shrieks of pain mingling with the smell of cooking flesh.

托勒密：需要吗啡吗，格鲁托夫上尉？
Ptolemy: Any morphine to ease the pain, Captain?

失去控制的地面再度变得坚实起来，独眼的狮鹫军官放下枪，在父亲双腿即将被永远封入冻土前搀起了他。
Freed from Krutov's incantation, the ground begins to harden again. Ptolemy lowers his gun and pulls his father up before his legs are sealed for good.

两人并肩而立。
They stand side by side.

托勒密：谢谢您，父亲。
Ptolemy: Thank you, Father.

托勒密：如您所言，只有愤怒能让他放下防备——但这太冒险了，这枚子弹应该直接穿过他的心脏！
Ptolemy: Just as you predicted, in his anger, he dropped his guard. But I still think I should've aimed for his heart instead!

伊戈尔：我承诺过，会把亲手复仇的机会留给你。
Igor: An eye for an eye. That was my promise.

他越过托勒密的肩膀，看向昔日的战友。
He glances past Ptolemy's shoulder at the man he once fought beside.

格鲁托夫跪在地上，灼伤的脸埋在手里，烧焦的肉与冰冷的皮质手套粘连在一起。
Krutov kneels, his burned face buried in his hand, the charred skin sticking to his cold leather gloves.

伊戈尔：没有凡人能跨越永恒，格鲁托夫。我早已向你说过这句话。
Igor: No mortal can transcend eternity, Krutov. I already told you this.

伊戈尔：重塑之手的确能赐予人非凡的力量，但那只是一块有毒的诱饵，与他们牵扯过深的人最终都会成为牺牲品。
Igor: The power Manus Vindictae offers is nothing but a poisoned chalice. Drinking it down will only lead to your doom.

格鲁托夫：……不……
Krutov: No ...

格鲁托夫：……我和你不一样，伊戈尔。你太软弱，在追求力量的路上临阵脱逃。
Krutov: I'm no weakling like you, Igor! I won't flinch from the pursuit of strength!

军阀首领的身躯微微颤抖。
His whole body is quivering.

格鲁托夫：我不会犯下和你一样的错误。
Krutov: I won't make the same mistake you did!

托勒密：等等，他手里的是什么？
Ptolemy: Wait, what's he holding?

捂紧面孔的双手与被毁坏的皮肤之间，悄然出现了一件熟悉得令人不安的手形器物。
Between his hands and ruined flesh, a familiar dark mask appears.

格鲁托夫：原谅我的无礼，从此刻起，我将永远赞颂你的美名……
Krutov: Forgive my earlier ignorance, Your Holiness. From this moment on, I will eternally praise Your name.

托勒密：该死的！
Ptolemy: Goddammit!

托勒密对准格鲁托夫扣下扳机，子弹却在靠近目标的那一刻撞上了厚重的冰壳。
Ptolemy fires at Krutov, but the bullet hits a wall of ice before it reaches him.

见子弹无效，托勒密向仍在原地喃喃呓语的受试炼者踏出一步。
Krutov shakes and murmurs to himself as he undergoes the trial. Ptolemy paces forward, readying himself to tear the mask from him.

托勒密：我去打碎他的面具——
Ptolemy: I'll smash that mask to pieces!

伊戈尔：不，退后！
Igor: No, stay back!

伊戈尔警觉地扣住养子肩膀，把他拉到了身后。一道锋利的冰墙切开了托勒密方才站立处的空气。
Igor grabs his shoulder and pulls him back. A sharp wall of ice slices through the air in front of him.

格鲁托夫：……我听见了，这些声音——我早该知道这一切的真相，我早该聆听这些优美的词句……呃——
Krutov: I hear it. I hear Your wise words! I should've listened to you long ago. I should've seen the truth of this world! Argh!

他嘶叫着放下了掩面的手，灼烧的蜡泪从颧骨淌至锁骨——那是熔化的皮肉，随动作拉伸出的琥珀色黏丝。
Krutov lowers his hands, the melted flesh of his face drooping like soft wax in sticky amber threads.

格鲁托夫：哈……哈，复苏之母……
Krutov: Heh. Heh. Mother of Resurrection.

手形的面具捧住了他的双眼。环绕着格鲁托夫的冰冷漩涡不断向外扩张。
With the hand-shaped mask cradling his eyes, a whirlwind of chilling air begins to spread from Krutov.

伊戈尔：寒冷……原来如此。
Igor: This cold, it's ... I see.

伊戈尔：格鲁托夫通过了试炼，重塑之手的术士一定藏在附近，她将偷走的冬天全部交给了格鲁托夫。
Igor: Krutov has passed the mask trial. That Manus ritualist must be hiding nearby. She's given him the power to contain the entire stolen winter on his own.

托勒密：什么？怪不得飞行巫师始终没能彻底摧毁顿河的天候术式，难道从一开始格鲁托夫就是……
Ptolemy: What? So that's why the Flying Witches couldn't fully stop the ritual. Who'd have thought Krutov was ...

伊戈尔拔出骑兵刀，金属在骤然降低的温度中颤抖了一瞬，刀身因寒冷而覆上一层钻石般的霜。
Igor draws his shashka. It trembles in the sudden cold, frost forming in diamonds along its blade.

伊戈尔：通知红弩箭中尉，术阵最后的节点找到了。
Igor: Inform Lieutenant Lilya at once. We've found the final rite.

坚冰如活物般噬咬着众人的手腕，向着躯干蔓延。只有那些因连续射击而滚烫的枪管，仍在寒潮中倔强地蒸腾着白气。
Living ice swirls and bites at their wrists, climbing up their arms to their torsos. Only their red-hot gun barrels are able to fight it off.

托勒密：该死……！这家伙控制不住天候术式了！
Ptolemy: Damn it! This bastard won't hold back the winter any longer!

托勒密：别停下射击！
Ptolemy: Keep shooting!

格鲁托夫单膝跪倒在地，托勒密射出的子弹却尽数被前仆后继的士兵阻拦，目标转眼间被黑色潮水般的重塑士兵淹没。
Manus soldiers, one after another, throw themselves into the gunfire before they reach the collapsed Krutov. Soon, Krutov is submerged in a black tide of soldiers.

托勒密甩开转轮，倒出几枚空弹壳。
Ptolemy swings open his gun cylinder and empties the spent shells.

托勒密：可恶……他跑去了哪里？！
Ptolemy: Damn it! Where'd he run off to?

托勒密：喂，女巫！这些人是哪里来的——外面的骑兵军到底有没有干活？！不会怕死跑了吧——
Ptolemy: Hey, Flying Witch! How'd those Manus scum appear all of a sudden? Did the cavalry all turn tail and run?

红弩箭：闭上你的臭嘴！
Lilya: Shut your trap!

气温骤跌，直逼冰点。她呵出的白雾还未成形便被寒风撕碎，飞行的高度也随着稀薄的空气一寸一寸往下坠。
A flurry of condensation clouds from her mouth. The thinness of the stinging cold air has pulled her lower.

红弩箭加速绕行一圈，撞开几个向着战场中心包围而来的敌人，降落在战场中心。
Lilya runs a circle around the battlefield, knocking aside some straggling enemies, before landing in a small clearing at its center.

红弩箭：敌人已经开始溃退了。骑兵军在追击残余的匪军，但是不知道重塑之手的军队是在哪里消失的。
Lilya: The cavalry are chasing down whatever's left of Krutov's bandits. As for the Manus, I got no clue how they managed to disappear like that.

红弩箭：重塑之手一定布置了自己的传送术阵，飞行中队正在寻找术式地点。
Lilya: Must've used some kind of teleport ritual. The Alphas are looking for it now.

托勒密：刚才还有很多重塑之手的士兵，现在全部消失不见。他们的术阵肯定就在村子里。
Ptolemy: There were a lot of them, so the ritual site must be nearby, probably somewhere in the village.

红弩箭：村里的房屋和居民太多，反而限制了空中的搜查进度。你们应该快点派人去进行地面搜查。
Lilya: If that's the case, the Alphas can't do much—too many buildings. You better have your men do a grid search.

托勒密：不能地毯式轰炸吗？
Ptolemy: How about we carpet-bomb them out?

红弩箭：那打完仗以后他们住哪儿？更何况你的队伍还分散在村里——你的脑子里全是冰碴子？
Lilya: What about the villagers, huh? What about your own men? Is your brain frozen?

伊戈尔：我会派出地面部队的，但他们的速度不如你快，中尉。
Igor: A unit will be dispatched to perform a ground search, but they won't be as fast as you, Lieutenant.

红弩箭一阵语塞，最后她“啧”了一声，跨上了飞行器。
She has no words. After a moment, she clicks her tongue and climbs onto her broom.

红弩箭：按照之前重塑之手补充兵力的方向看，他们的传送术阵也许是在靠南边的位置……嘶，好冷。
Lilya: Based on the direction of their reinforcements, the teleport ritual site must be in the south of the village. Brrrr, freezing my butt off here.

红弩箭：啧，究竟藏在哪里，运走这么多人的神秘术阵，不可能不留下任何痕迹……
Lilya: Mm! Where is the damn thing? A whole army went through it. No way it'd just disappear without a trace.

红弩箭：**[斯拉夫粗口]！
Lilya: Damn it!

镜面反射的光斑让飞行女巫的眼睛反射性眯了起来，红弩箭猛地转了个方向拉高上天，以避免一头栽进某个屋顶。
Lilya squints as a glare from somewhere on the ground almost blinds her. She banks hard, just barely avoiding a roof.

红弩箭借着云层的遮挡避开这晃眼的反光，但那光斑就像长了腿似的，一路改变方向追着她。
She tries to hide in the clouds, but the glare follows her every turn.

红弩箭：到底是什么人这么不分场合，让我找到了迟早要轰炸那**[飞行中队粗口]一顿……
Lilya: I swear, if I catch the ground-duster who dares dazzle me right now, I'll give him a missile to the face.

红弩箭：……
Lilya: ...

红弩箭：轰炸……
Lilya: Missile ... to the face ...

红弩箭：对了——下次拿着望远镜的时候别对天瞎看。
Lilya: And Sergey, if you shine the light off that telescope into my eyes one more time ...

红弩箭：要是反光再晃到我的眼睛，我就用导弹轰你。
Lilya: The last thing you'll see is a missile to the face. Understood?

谢尔盖：好、好吧，我下次一定不会了。
Sergey: Ahh. Understood, Lieutenant.

红弩箭：谢尔盖？！
Lilya: Sergey?!

她戴上护目镜，降下高度，眯起眼睛直视光斑的源头。
She pulls down her goggles, drops lower, and searches for the light's source.

一架残破不堪的望远镜，丢了半边镜筒，让它像个格外严肃的万花筒。
It's a pair of binoculars, half shattered, looking like a sorry children's kaleidoscope.

一个伤痕累累的年轻骑兵，穿着出土文物一般狼狈破烂的芝诺军服。
They're in the hands of a wounded young rider in Zeno uniform, looking just as tattered.

谢尔盖：嘿——中尉——
Sergey: Hey! Lieutenant—!

他努力地蹦跳着吸引她的注意力，像只格外有活力的草原野兔，一只手仍然坚持不懈地指向某个方向。
He waves as he jumps, lively as a grassland hare, one hand pointed.

红弩箭：他在指哪里？——马厩？他想要我看马厩做什么？
Lilya: What's he pointing at? Uhm, the stable? Why?

红弩箭：……马厩后面有什么东西——格鲁托夫？！
Lilya: There something in the stable? Wait! It's got to be Krutov!

在飞行女巫鹰般锐利的眼中，一瘸一拐的格鲁托夫正在术士的搀扶下走进马厩。
She spots a limping Krutov being led into a stable by the ritualist.

红弩箭：我看到了，快躲开，小子！
Lilya: I see them, Sergey! Stay back!

随着爆炸尘埃一同撒向空中的还有被炸开的冰晶。它们迅速上浮，融进了糖霜似的云朵中。
Ice and dust scatter in the explosion.

飞行女巫降落在马厩的废墟边缘。在她落地之前，谢尔盖就已经像鼹鼠一般在马厩的废墟中挖来挖去。
By the time Lilya lands near the ruined stable, Sergey is already digging through the wreckage like a mole.

红弩箭：——离那儿远点！格鲁托夫和重塑的术士可能还被埋在下面。
Lilya: Didn't I tell you to stay away? Krutov and that ritualist could still be alive down there.

谢尔盖：不对……不对呀？
Sergey: No. It can't be. How?

谢尔盖从满地的碎屑中钻出来，拍掉身上的灰尘，飞快地跑到中尉身边。
Sergey climbs out, brushes himself off, and runs to the lieutenant.

谢尔盖：他们不在这下面，这马厩就这么点大的地方，愣是连尸体都没找着。
Sergey: The place is tiny, but I don't see them, not even a trace.

红弩箭：——啧。又让他们跑了。
Lilya: Tsk, they got away again.

红弩箭愤懑地踢开脚边的一小颗蘑菇。
Lilya kicks a small mushroom at her feet in frustration.

红弩箭：有可能是连续的短距离传送术。飞行中队还会往其他方向搜索，可能她们会有所发现吧。
Lilya: Probably used multiple short-range teleport rituals. Damn! Hopefully the Alphas find something elsewhere.

红弩箭：还有，你怎么在这里？
Lilya: So, how did you end up here?

谢尔盖：之后再说吧，中尉，我还活着，这就行了！
Sergey: We can save that for later, Lieutenant. All that matters now is that I'm alive!

谢尔盖：我差点以为自己就交待在这儿了。
Sergey: For a moment, I honestly thought that this would be it for me.

他口齿不清地追问着。
He almost stumbles over his words to get his next question out.

谢尔盖：城里还好吗？军长和其他骑兵军在哪里？
Sergey: How are things in the city? What's happened to Commander Ivan and the rest of the Corps?

谢尔盖：我看匪军和重塑之手的人都跑了，其他人怎么样了？
Sergey: It looks like the bandits and the Manus are gone. What's going on?

谢尔盖：——求你了，给我说说吧，我们到底打赢了吗？
Sergey: Come on, tell me, did we win?

飞行女巫抱着胸，一时之间不知道该从何说起。
Lilya crosses her arms, not knowing where to begin.

她拿出久未启封的酒壶，猛灌了一口。
She takes a long drink from a flask she hasn't opened in a long time.

红弩箭：……呼。
Lilya: *sigh*

冬日回归大地，一阵出奇的寂静也与飘落的雪花一同落下。
Winter returns. And with it, the eerie silence of snow.

谢尔盖：……
Sergey: ...

遥远的声音代替了对战争结局的回答——
A distant sound answers for her.

人们互相呼唤，疲劳的马儿喷着鼻息，远方草场的“沙沙”声与顿河水流清亮的颤音混在一起。
Hollered voices, snorting horses, and the stirring of the long grass all echo on the banks of the shimmering Don.

红弩箭：他们做到了自己能做的……
Lilya: They did what they could.

有的人试图纠正鲜血淋漓的错误，可错误无法被纠正，但仍然可以阻止罪孽继续蔓延。
Some sins can never be redeemed. Yet, it is not too late to keep them from spreading, from taking root again.

——即为自己而战，也为故土而战。
For one's own sake, and for the sake of home and family.

有的人用血肉之躯去对抗钢铁，用肉体堵住施术的术杖。
Bare fists struck steel behemoths; soft flesh warded off fell sorcery.

他们也许不够强大，却也拼命换来了他人的生命得以存续。
Their brittle lives were laid down so that others might be spared.

生者们仰望天空，见证迟来的第一场雪。
And the living lift their eyes as the first snow falls.

时间开始转动，冬天马上就要来了。
Time finds its rightful course once more. Winter has come.

红弩箭：庆幸吧，这一次，是我们赢了。
Lilya: Luckily, we won, for this round, at least.

12TH-23 遥远的路程 / The Long Road Ahead

玛尔纱：我在东线的任务已经结束。在我写下这封信的不久前，别列格勒城及其周边发生了一场我没有预想过的战斗。
Marsha: My mission on the Eastern Front is over, but the battle that took place here has left an indelible impression on me. It still strikes me like lightning.

玛尔纱：刚学会用枪的普通人藏在城市的街垒后，顽强地抵抗着匪军与重塑之手的进攻，最终让别列格勒免于沦陷。
Marsha: In the city of Bereggrad, civilians, barely knowing how to handle a gun, gave their all to defend their homes from bandits and Manus Vindictae.

玛尔纱：屹立不倒的城市为野战部队争取到了施展战术的空间，骑兵军与他们的盟友得以放开手脚，击败敌军主力。
Marsha: Their unyielding defense of the city streets bought crucial tactical space for the Zeno Cavalry Corps and their allies on the field, allowing them to strike the enemy's main force without restraint.

玛尔纱：一部分居民不幸罹难，但更多人在这场战役中生还。他们保卫家乡的英勇事迹将在这片土地上永远流传。
Marsha: Some lost their lives, but many more will live because of their sacrifice. I am certain those names will be remembered on this steppe forever.

玛尔纱：对了，我在这儿见到了卡戎，我猜你也会感到惊讶。可惜，时间仓促，还有太多事无法在信中写完。
Marsha: As an aside, I ran into Charon here—what are the odds of that? It's a shame I don't have time to share more stories with you in just one letter.

玛尔纱：真希望有一天能当面给你讲我在东线的故事。我马上会回基金会总部，亲爱的朋友，同样期待你平安的消息。
Marsha: I hope one day to tell you all about them in person. And don't worry about me, my dear Marianne: I'll soon return to the Foundation headquarters. I look forward to hearing from you.

叶尔莫莱：只有这一封信吗？
Yermolai: That the only letter you want to send?

骑士把匆匆写好的信折好，装进信封，郑重其事地印下了基金会的火漆。
The knight folds her letter, seals it in an envelope, and presses the Foundation's wax seal on it with solemn care.

玛尔纱：我不知道你会到这儿来，没有想到有机会送信过去。
Marsha: I would've written more if I knew you'd be delivering them personally.

玛尔纱：你说你还会回一趟西线，那就拜托你把这封信带回蒙佩。会有人来取的。
Marsha: If you're returning to the Western Front, please bring this letter to Montpaix. Someone there will pick it up.

叶尔莫莱：噢，你是说那个石像鬼。别送蒙佩了，她早就不在那一带活动了。
Yermolai: Ah, you mean that Gargoyle girl, right? She's not hanging around Montpaix anymore.

玛尔纱：你知道她的动向？
Marsha: Huh? Do you know where she went?

叶尔莫莱：不算知道，但在别的地方见过她几次。
Yermolai: Can't say that I do, but I have run into her a few times since.

“猎犬”的表情像是被一阵不存在的冬日寒气挠了一下后背。
Hound looks as though a chill has just run up his spine.

叶尔莫莱：第一次是在卢森堡。当时我正在那儿找一些东西。在我发现她的时候，枪口已经顶上了我的后脑勺。
Yermolai: First time was in Luxembourg. I was out looking for something when she decided to press the muzzle of her gun against the back of my head.

叶尔莫莱：我以为她是来讨债的，毕竟在299高地发生的事情并不愉快。要我说，刻雷乌斯欠她一份包含物质回报的感谢信。
Yermolai: I thought she was still holding a grudge over what happened at Hill 299. I wouldn't blame her. After all, Creius owes her a hell of a lot more than a little thanks.

叶尔莫莱：但她只是想“和‘Ⅻ’小队的人谈谈”。
Yermolai: But turns out she just wanted to have a chat with a member of the "XII."

玛尔纱：你们说了什么？
Marsha: What did you talk about?

叶尔莫莱：大概是立了一些规矩。有时候，她的行动目标会和我们小队重合，这时候就要划分一下界限。
Yermolai: Something about setting rules. Said she doesn't mind helping out when her objectives overlap with ours.

叶尔莫莱：她会为我们提供帮助，条件是我们要向她分享在行动中获知的所有信息。她办事很利索，就是缺乏幽默感。
Yermolai: On the condition that we share with her each and every piece of information we have. Must've been serious, right? Doesn't seem like the kind of person who appreciates a joke.

玛尔纱：可能只是你的幽默感太糟糕了。
Marsha: Maybe just your jokes.

叶尔莫莱：哈。总之，虽然我不知道她的具体动向，但要再找到她一次应该并不困难，尤其是手上还有你给她的信。
Yermolai: Ha, could be. Anyway, I don't know her exact whereabouts, but finding her again shouldn't be too hard. I'm sure she wouldn't wanna miss your letter.

玛尔纱：那么，你怎么会被派到这里来？
Marsha: Thanks. So, why were you sent here?

叶尔莫莱：刻雷乌斯要我来做一些“收尾工作”……啧，什么脏活累活都是我来干了。
Yermolai: Creius wanted me to do some "mopping up." Lucky me, always stuck with the chores.

叶尔莫莱：我得观察骑兵军在战斗结束后的政治倾向有没有异常，确定他们和伊戈尔斩断了联系……啊，还有“乌鸫”。
Yermolai: Watching to see if the Zeno corps here shows any "unusual political tendencies" after the battle. Making sure they've cut contact with Igor. Oh, and Blackbird!

他从怀中拿出一封文书，交给玛尔纱。后者带着一丝犹豫，展开折好的纸张。
He pulls a document from his coat and hands it to Marsha. After a pause, she carefully opens it.

玛尔纱：“梅蕾尔，接到此信后立刻前往顿河地区，隐藏身份秘密调查‘金色饥荒’。刻雷乌斯。11月……10日？”
Marsha: "Merel, head to the Don River region immediately. Cover your tracks and investigate the Golden Famine there. Creius. November ... 10th"?

玛尔纱：这是梅蕾尔逃跑之前的命令，也就是说，她并不是逃亡？
Marsha: That was before Merel's desertion. Then, she didn't run away after all?

叶尔莫莱：这日期当然是假的。你把“乌鸫”的消息传回去之后，刻雷乌斯就在我眼前写了这封“密令”。
Yermolai: Nah, the date's fake. Creius wrote up this "secret order" right in front of me after your report.

叶尔莫莱：我出发的时候，签名上的龙血印章都还没有干透。
Yermolai: The seal on the signature hadn't even dried when I set out.

一些补办的文书工作，也许无伤大雅。
A little paperwork filed after the fact. Should be harmless.

玛尔纱：好吧……你确定这些事应该告诉我吗？
Marsha: I see. Are you sure you should've told me this?

叶尔莫莱的脸色变得很快，他出人意料地沉下脸来。
Yermolai's face darkens unexpectedly.

叶尔莫莱：我们是一个队的队友。
Yermolai: We're on the same team.

叶尔莫莱：之后一定还会有比这更糟的事，如果不能互相照应，我们迟早全都栽沟里，能懂吗？
Yermolai: If we can't trust each other, we'll all end up in the ditch when s**t hits the fan. Know what I mean?

玛尔纱：……我明白你的意思了。梅蕾尔还在休息，要我把她叫来吗？
Marsha: You make a good point. Merel's still resting. Should I call for her now?

梅蕾尔：我……我在这儿。
Merel: I-I'm here.

被一纸“密令”暂时解救的逃兵站在玛尔纱身后，她双手搭住骑士的肩甲，只探出半边脑袋。
The deserter, spared for now by this "secret order," peeks out from behind Marsha with a sheepish look on her face.

叶尔莫莱越过骑士警戒的目光，对躲在后面的梅蕾尔扬了扬下巴。
Yermolai tilts his chin at her.

叶尔莫莱：有保姆照顾你的日子结束了，“乌鸫”。虽然基金会不一定会来找你麻烦，但队内的惩罚可不能少。
Yermolai: Your days of fluttering under a babysitter's wings have come to an end, Blackbird. You may be off the Foundation's hook, but I'm afraid some form of internal punishment within the squad is inevitable.

梅蕾尔：队内惩罚？
Merel: Internal punishment?

梅蕾尔闻言缓缓走出一个后撤步。
Hearing this, Merel takes a slow step back.

叶尔莫莱：还想跑。
Yermolai: Don't think you can get away again.

像抓兔子一样，男人将梅蕾尔从骑士身后揪出来。
Like catching a rabbit, the man pulls Merel out from behind the knight.

梅蕾尔：哎呀——
Merel: Naah!

玛尔纱：喂，你小心点！
Marsha: Hey, go easy on her!

叶尔莫莱：之后她就跟我走了，玛尔纱。刻雷乌斯要我给她打上跟踪药剂。
Yermolai: I'll be keeping tabs on her from now on, Marsha. Even got a tracking serum. Creius's order.

玛尔纱：跟踪药剂？
Marsha: Tracking serum?

叶尔莫莱：不知道哪儿的书呆子们研制的新玩意儿，需要实验样本。正好给这小老鼠打上，以免她再开溜。
Yermolai: Yeah, goof-juice invented by some eggheads. Still in development, actually. Our little runaway will make the perfect lab rat.

梅蕾尔：我不会了，相信我，我一定不会再跑了！我保证！
Merel: I won't run again. Trust me. I swear!

叶尔莫莱：安静点，想让所有人都知道你干了什么吗？还是说想尝一尝苦哑巴药剂？
Yermolai: Keep that voice down. You trying to tell the entire world you're a deserter? Or you looking for a taste of Dumbitter Potion?

梅蕾尔：……不想。
Merel: N-No.

她不情不愿地咬住嘴唇。
She bites her lip.

玛尔纱轻轻拍了拍她的肩膀。
Marsha gives her a light pat on the shoulder.

玛尔纱：别担心，回去的路上我们还会在一起。
Marsha: Relax. I'll be traveling back with you.

安德烈森：咴。
Andreas: *neigh*

梅蕾尔：嗯？
Merel: Huh?

黑色的战马从街道另一侧匆匆跑来，在马儿身旁的是它熟悉的旅伴。
A black warhorse trots over from down the street, his old friend beside him.

卡戎：梅蕾尔，很高兴你选择回到自己的朋友身边，希望你未来的旅途一路平安。
Charon: It is good that you've returned to your friends, Merel. May your journey ahead be a safe one.

卡戎：谢谢你为我提供的援助，玛尔纱，这个过程一定给你带来了很大的痛苦，一直以来我都为此自责……
Charon: And thank you, Marsha. Tending to this broken body must have taken a great toll on you. I am sorry for any pain it caused.

玛尔纱：别往心里去，卡戎，你能恢复就好。我自己会把握使用神秘术的分寸的。
Marsha: Please, don't think of it that way, Charon. I can handle my arcane skills. I'm just relieved that you're back on your feet.

叶尔莫莱：是你，收尸人。知道你也在东线的时候，我很意外。帕拉维扬告诉我，是你隐瞒了梅蕾尔的行踪。
Yermolai: Gotta say, I was surprised to hear you'd made it out this way, gravedigger. Paravyan told me it was you who covered Merel's tracks.

梅蕾尔：等、等等！卡戎和这件事儿没有关系！是我坚持要他这么做的。
Merel: W-Wait! Leave Charon out of this! I asked, I mean, I forced him to help me!

叶尔莫莱：你着什么急？难道你不是为了遵守长官的命令，才要求卡戎为你隐藏行踪的吗？
Yermolai: What's got you so worked up? All you did was follow Creius's orders and cover your tracks, right?

梅蕾尔：呃……是的，不，真的是这样吗？
Merel: Umm, yeah, no, wait, did I?

叶尔莫莱：就是这样。给我记好了，以后不管什么人问你，你都要这么回答。
Yermolai: Yeah, you did, and keep that in mind if anyone asks.

梅蕾尔：好的……好的。
Merel: O-Okay.

一旁的亡者花了很长时间也没有弄明白“Ⅻ”小队的队员们在说什么，最终只好放弃寻找答案。
Charon, struggling to follow the conversation among the "XII" Squad, gives up trying.

卡戎：死亡是平等的，对死亡的恐惧也是平等的。回避死亡是生者的本能，希望你能理解她的行为。
Charon: Life must flee death. It is our most basic instinct. Death is impartial, unstoppable. No creature should be punished for running from its shadow.

叶尔莫莱：我完全理解。放心吧，梅蕾尔不会有事的，保证她平平安安。
Yermolai: Sure, sure. Don't worry. I'll make sure our friend here stays safe and sound.

卡戎：我所期望的莫过于此。那么，再见，各位。
Charon: A small hope in this gray world. Now, there is more work to be done.

玛尔纱：你又要离开了吗，卡戎？
Marsha: You're leaving again, Charon?

梅蕾尔：你可以跟我一起回——
Merel: Why don't you join us at the—

“基金会”三个字卡在她的喉咙里。
"Foundation" catches in her throat.

梅蕾尔：算了。
Merel: N-Never mind.

梅蕾尔：希望以后还能见到你，卡戎。当然，不是在战场上。我不想再看见更多的尸体了。
Merel: I hope I see you again, Charon, though maybe not on another battlefield. I'd be happy to never see another corpse in my life.

梅蕾尔：还有你，安德烈森。
Merel: I'll miss you too, Andreas.

梅蕾尔踮起脚，抱住了安德烈森的脖子，脸颊蹭上粗糙的鬃毛。
Merel stands on tiptoes, wrapping her arms around Andreas's neck, and presses her cheek to his rough mane.

梅蕾尔：再见了，我的朋友们。和你们一起的旅途很愉快……当然，落水的那部分除外。
Merel: Goodbye, friends! I've made so many happy memories with you, well, aside from the drowning.

梅蕾尔：我会一直想念你们的。
Merel: I'll miss you from the bottom of my heart!

安德烈森：咴……
Andreas: Neigh ...

卡戎：希望我们会在更和平的年代相见。
Charon: May our reunion come in a more peaceful time.

亡者轻挽缰绳，与他的马儿一同走出城市。
Leading Andreas by the reins, Charon makes his way out of the city.

他们消失在冬日的草原，赶赴下一场没有终点的苦旅。
They disappear into the winter grassland, returning to the long, hard road they must walk.

12TH-24 启程日 / The Day of Departure

别列格勒万人空巷，所有人都拥抱着挤在街道里。士兵用豪饮纪念胜利，民众用欢歌庆祝幸存。
The streets of Bereggrad are packed. The people hug and laugh, and the soldiers drink and sing to their hard-won victory.

但深埋修道院下，不属于这个时代的建筑依然保持沉默。
But deep below the church, in a room from another age, there is nothing but silence.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

白色大理石椅光滑冷硬，指腹按压在扶手上时，遥远的呼唤似乎又穿越了时间与距离。
The white marble chair is smooth and cold. The touch of a fingertip sends a distant call across time and space.

维尔汀：真的是你吗？
Vertin: Is it really you?

维尔汀：呃……！
Vertin: Ah!

落座瞬间，不属于自己的疼痛穿透了皮肤屏障。
She sits, and a pain prickles through her skin, a pain that is not her own.

维尔汀：你经历了什么？
Vertin: What have you been through?

维尔汀：你在哪儿？
Vertin: Where are you?

不好意思，我想我们的声音有些叨扰到她了。她需要休息。
Shh. We should let her get some rest.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀。
Vertin.

维尔汀：……你是谁？
Vertin: Who are you?

我们在不同的命途之上追逐着各自的答案。
We all walk our own paths, seeking our own answers.

但在未来，我们一定会再见的。
But our paths will surely cross again.

？？？：司辰？
???: Timekeeper?

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

身体离开大理石椅的瞬间，感知迅速从回忆中抽离，被粗暴地塞回了现实世界。
She gets to her feet, tearing her from those memories and thrusting her back into the real world.

踏入这片纯白中的脚步声，听起来有些谨慎。
The footsteps that follow carry a note of caution.

伊戈尔：看来我终于能进入这片空间了……这里的白色实在有些刺眼。
Igor: This room had always been locked to me, but now ... Tch. It is blindingly white.

维尔汀：……伊戈尔，你来了。
Vertin: Mr. Igor.

伊戈尔：如果我是你，就不会随意坐上这把椅子。
Igor: I wouldn't sit in that chair. Not unless you know it to be necessary.

维尔汀：兀尔德曾在这张椅子上坐过，我也想尝试一下，也许会有所发现。
Vertin: Urd sat here. I wanted to try it myself.

伊戈尔：还有什么新发现吗？
Igor: Find anything useful?

维尔汀：琥珀屋里还有一些遗留的实验资料，给我提供情报的人也许想要得到这些东西。
Vertin: Some documents on the experiment. The person who told me about this room might be interested.

维尔汀：至于兀尔德……我想，最重要的信息已经在我第一次踏入的时候传递完毕了。
Vertin: But if you mean to ask about Urd specifically, I haven't learned anything more than I did on my first visit.

维尔汀：对于在这间屋子里发生的事，你知道多少？那些在兀尔德身上做实验的人——他们要从她身上得到什么？
Vertin: You were there. What do you know about the experiments in this room? What did they want from her?

理智被挤压，语气随之不知不觉间加快，对答案的迫切渴望逐渐在头脑中占了上风。
Her usually reasoned words come quickly, driven by her hunger for answers.

维尔汀：你们对她究竟做了什么？
Vertin: What did you do to her?

伊戈尔：鸽子屋对兀尔德做了什么，我想你的心里已经得出了答案。
Igor: The things the Pax House did to Urd ... I'm sure you've pieced it together somehow.

伊戈尔：第二次“暴雨”后，基金会建立了“暴雨”应急系统。
Igor: After the second "Storm," the Foundation led an effort to build an emergency response system.

伊戈尔：但两次时代的消失和对重塑之手的无知让高层意识到，我们无法靠自己结束“暴雨”。
Igor: But after Manus Vindictae reared their head and in the wake of the vanishing of two eras, we realized no system could stop the "Storm."

伊戈尔：我们需要兀尔德。
Igor: We needed Urd.

维尔汀：你们找到过她，却发现她已经成了另一个人。一个调查记者，或者是一个无国界医生，都不是你们需要的。
Vertin: And you tracked her down, only to find she'd become someone else, an investigative journalist, a humanitarian doctor, anything but the identity you were hoping for.

维尔汀：所以，你们一直在尝试一种方法，强迫盲眼女士成为兀尔德——1999年的兀尔德。
Vertin: You tried every method to force that version of her, a blind woman you had no need of, into becoming Urd again, the one from 1999.

伊戈尔：我们……或者，你可以说，鸽子屋，认为……
Igor: We, or the Pax House, believed that ...

伊戈尔：无论“暴雨”的本质是重塑之手利用灵界捏造了新的灵魂，还是他们通过影响物质宇宙，造成了世界性的记忆与记录偏差……
Igor: No matter the nature of the "Storm," whether Manus Vindictae forged new psyches from the realm of souls or twisted the entire material world to warp memories on a universal scale ...

伊戈尔：解决问题的关键都在于找回最初的兀尔德女士——在“暴雨”安全区建立这间回环实验室，包括开展“灌体”实验，都是为了实现这个目标。
Igor: The key to every question about the "Storm" was tied up in Urd, the original Urd. The Loop Laboratory and the vessel ensoulment experiments conducted here were dedicated to finding that key.

维尔汀：你也想通过找回她来结束这一切吗？
Vertin: Was that your goal to find her and end all this?

伊戈尔：……
Igor: ...

年迈的将军闭了闭眼，似是回忆，又似回避。
The old admiral closes his eyes, either to recall or avoid.

维尔汀：伊戈尔，你也想要重返“暴雨”降临前的时代吗？
Vertin: Igor, do you also want to return to the era before the "Storm"?

答案没有第一时间被给出，伊戈尔靠近白色石屋的一角，像是在寻找什么。
No reply comes. Igor moves to a corner as if searching for something.

伊戈尔：他们果然没来得及带走，和实验资料一起，全都留在了这里……
Igor: Just as I suspected, they didn't have time to evacuate with these materials.

伊戈尔从一堆软盘中翻出一本厚如字典的白色书册。
From a pile of disks, he lifts a white book as thick as a dictionary.

伊戈尔：拿着。
Igor: Take it.

维尔汀：好重……
Vertin: It's heavy.

指腹传来了大理石般冷硬的触感。
Its surface is as cold and hard as marble.

伊戈尔：这是四十三个灵魂的重量。
Igor: The weight of 43 souls combined.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

伊戈尔：我在世界范围内定位、秘密绑架“暴雨”后身份错位的人，换取片刻喘息。
Igor: The souls of those whose identities were "displaced" after the "Storm." I abducted them from all around the world—a way to regain my footing among the ranks.

伊戈尔：我曾经相信，甚至对基金会报以“希望”。我希望“灌体”未来能带回我所珍视的人们。
Igor: I placed my trust, my hope even, in the Foundation, believing that these experiments would one day bring back the people I loved.

维尔汀：可是你最终还是选择了背叛。
Vertin: But you chose to walk away.

伊戈尔：我收殓了四十三具失去灵魂的躯壳。
Igor: 43. Each soul left behind a husk. I buried every one of them.

伊戈尔：而在“暴雨”后我举办过的葬礼次数，远超于此。
Igor: I've buried so many people since the "Storm." I've lost count. I stopped counting.

长者从大衣中掏出了一个黑色的立方体，暗念了一句咒文，它便在手中悠悠悬浮了起来。
He takes the black cube from his coat and murmurs an incantation. It floats above his palm.

伊戈尔：阿尔卡纳的存在并未随肉体湮灭而消失。
Igor: Arcana's body was annihilated, but Her presence endures.

伊戈尔：我能感受到祂无处不在，如同能量的流动……这对神秘学家血脉并不浓厚的我而言，是一份强大的证明。
Igor: Even with my modest lineage, I feel Her presence everywhere, at all times.

伊戈尔：我向祂索求一份跨越暴雨的“奇迹”，这份“奇迹”最初确实让我的军队越过了一次“暴雨”。
Igor: She bestowed on me a "boon" that let my army cross the "Storm." It worked, as She promised.

伊戈尔：但离开南极后，我就无法再次让它生成足以庇佑一人以上的术阵——以它为“路标”寻找新的庇护所，费了我们相当大的精力。
Igor: But after leaving Antarctica, the barrier that "boon" created could shelter only one person. I did still use it as a beacon to find a new sanctuary, but it cost us dearly in time and effort.

伊戈尔：格鲁托夫正是抓住了我们建立庇护所的这段时间，才有了机会在顿河为非作歹。
Igor: Meanwhile, Krutov seized the opportunity to wreak havoc along the Don.

伊戈尔突然笑了笑，停止将神秘术能量灌入“奇迹”。
A bitter smile colors Igor's face, and he stops channeling arcane energy into the "boon."

伊戈尔：这是阿尔卡纳对我的嘲弄——一个混血神秘学家，岂能妄称诺亚。
Igor: This is Arcana's mockery of me—the mixed-blood arcanist who dared mimic Noah.

维尔汀：但现在，你已经利用它找到了属于你自己的方舟。
Vertin: But you managed to build your own ark, didn't you?

对方苦笑一声，不置可否。
He gives a dry laugh that is neither a yes nor a no.

下一秒，伊戈尔将这一份“奇迹”稳稳放在了白色书册之上。
Then he sets the "boon" down on the white book.

“奇迹”躺在白色书册上。伸手触碰时，无处不在的线在触碰它的瞬间绷直，进而消弭在空气中。
When she reaches out to it, the ever-present threads pull taut, then fade into the air.

维尔汀：……？
Vertin: ...?

伊戈尔：我想，你才是带领人们走出洪水的救世主。它真正的主人是你。
Igor: You are the true savior destined to lead us from the flood. Take it.

伊戈尔：回到主题吧，司辰。我已经兑现了诺言，带你找到了回环实验室，也把一些基金会不愿公布的事告诉了你。
Igor: Back to our deal, Timekeeper. I brought you to this laboratory as promised and told you secrets the Foundation would rather keep hidden.

伊戈尔：……价码再加上现在这一份“奇迹”，我想这能为我从你那里换取态度的转变。
Igor: Along with this "boon," I believe I have done enough to earn your favor.

维尔汀：你需要我提供什么？
Vertin: What is it that you want?

伊戈尔：在未来能与你合作的可能性。在必要的时候，我希望我们能互相帮助。
Igor: Only that you consider me a partner in the future, so that we may help each other when the need arises.

维尔汀：我仍是圣洛夫基金会的司辰，你在用生命和自由赌我的态度。
Vertin: I'm still the Timekeeper of the St. Pavlov Foundation. You're betting your life and freedom on nothing more than my favor.

伊戈尔：无妨，这不是我第一次扔下赌注。我坚信你与我都怀有对阿尔卡纳同等的敌意。
Igor: Not my first gamble. I have confidence. You and I share the same enemy in Arcana.

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

伊戈尔：还有一件事，格鲁托夫已经戴上面具，接受了试炼，变得比以往任何时候都更危险。
Igor: There's another matter. Krutov has passed the mask trial. He is more dangerous than ever before.

伊戈尔：而在打扫战场时，我们没有在红柳树村或是其他地方发现格鲁托夫的尸体。
Igor: We defeated him at Tamarovka, but there was no sign of his body.

维尔汀：你的意思是……
Vertin: So you're suggesting ...

伊戈尔：重塑之手缺乏有现代军事素养的将领，我认为格鲁托夫未来会成为突破基金会防线的关键人物。
Igor: Manus Vindictae lacks leaders with modern military training. I suspect Krutov will become key to their future conflicts with the Foundation.

把独处时间还给了年轻的基金会职员，长者避开街头人们的欢庆，离开了别列格勒。
Having left the Timekeeper to her devices, Igor slips past the street celebrations and leaves Bereggrad.

莫莉德尔：父亲。
Moldir: Father.

伊戈尔：如你所言，莫莉德尔。司辰和基金会大多数人都不一样。
Igor: As you said, Moldir, the Timekeeper is unlike most of her colleagues.

通讯器那头传来一声轻笑，狮鹫军副官回想起了上一个时代在冰原上的经历。
A soft laugh comes through the communicator. The events at the South Pole are still fresh in her mind.

莫莉德尔：是的。一位神奇的年轻女士，就我在南极期间与司辰小队的“合作”来看，我相信她会走得比基金会更远。
Moldir: She is a truly extraordinary young woman. Based on my collaboration with her team in Antarctica, I'm sure she has prospects beyond the Foundation.

莫莉德尔：我希望你们的会谈取得了好的结果。
Moldir: I hope your meeting brought something of value.

伊戈尔：的确有意外收获。
Igor: It did, to my surprise.

伊戈尔：把在各地执行任务的人召回庇护所，加快人员整备。
Igor: Recall all personnel on the field to the sanctuary. We need to accelerate recruitment and redeployment.

意料外的答复让莫莉德尔哑然了片刻。
Moldir is temporarily rendered silent by the abruptness of this order.

莫莉德尔：是，父亲。
Moldir: Yes, Father.

伊戈尔：如果附近村庄的居民有意加入我们，均予以收容。我们需要尽可能留存生的力量。
Igor: Let the residents of any nearby villages join us if they wish. We need all the strength we can muster.

莫莉德尔：所有人？
Moldir: All of them?

伊戈尔：平民，士兵，人类，神秘学家。
Igor: Civilian or soldier, human or arcanist—take them all in.

将军以不容置疑的坚定态度做出回应。
The admiral answers with unwavering conviction.

伊戈尔：在我回来之前，看好托勒密，别让他惹事。
Igor: And keep an eye on Ptolemy until I return.

伊戈尔：如果我没有回来，狮鹫军的指挥将全权转交于你。
Igor: And should I not return, command of the Gryphon Legion will be transferred to you.

莫莉德尔：父亲？
Moldir: Father?

伊戈尔站在流向地平线尽头的顿河河边，最后一次将目光投向这座古老的城市，然后挂断了通讯器。
Igor, standing on the bank of the Don, gives the old city one last glance and ends the call.

？？？：急着回家吗，老头？
???: What's the rush, old man?

枪口挑开了白发，紧紧贴在伊戈尔的后脑上。
A gun muzzle presses to the back of Igor's head.

伊戈尔：红弩箭中尉，你果然来了。
Igor: I've been expecting you, Lieutenant Lilya.

红弩箭：我很高兴你知道托勒密是个混蛋，这意味着你还不算是个最糟糕的“父亲”。
Lilya: So you recognize that Ptolemy is a good-for-nothing bastard, then? At least you're a better father than you are a soldier.

红弩箭：但很遗憾，做个好父亲不能赦免你的罪和你造成的流血。
Lilya: But being a half-decent father won't save you from the crimes you've committed or the lives you've taken.

红弩箭：我说过，我会亲手把你押上军事法庭。
Lilya: I said it before, I'll say it again: I will personally escort you to the judgment seat.

12TH-25 罪与罚 / Crime and Punishment

芝诺骑兵Ⅰ：这杯是为了芝诺骑兵军！
Zeno Cavalryman I: Raise your glass to the Zeno Cavalry Corps!

斯捷尔诺娃：敬骑兵军，敬飞行中队，敬别列格勒！
Sternova: To the Corps! To the Flying Witches! And to Bereggrad!

高举的橡木酒杯相互碰撞，清澈的澄黄酒液乘着泡沫跳出杯盏。
Oak mugs meet in a toast, golden liquor overflowing at their rims.

阿尔法4号：敬我们！
Alpha Four: To everyone!

芝诺骑兵Ⅱ：哦……这酒不像村里人自己酿的萨莫贡。
Zeno Cavalryman II: Hmm, this is nothing like the samogon we brew in the village.

阿尔法4号：更烈？
Alpha Four: Too fiery for you?

芝诺骑兵Ⅱ：差远了！
Zeno Cavalryman II: Not fiery enough!

骑兵一口气牛饮了整杯啤酒，豪爽地大笑起来。
He drains his mug and lets out a hearty laugh.

芝诺骑兵Ⅱ：再来一杯！
Zeno Cavalryman II: Hit me!

红弩箭笑着坐在欢庆的人群中，脸颊虽然已经挂上微醺的红色，但眼睛仍如鹰一般盯着营帐外塞契的大门。
Lilya sits with the celebrants, cheeks flushed, but her eyes still sharp on the sich gates outside the tent.

直到看见狮鹫军团的士兵们三两结伴离开，她才啐了一口，提起飞行扫帚向外走去。
When she sees the Gryphon soldiers leaving in twos and threes, she spits, picks up her broom, and strides out.

阿尔法4号：你要去哪儿，中队长？你可是庆功宴的主角。
Alpha Four: Where are you going, Commander? You're the star of this party!

红弩箭：拜托别这么叫我，太肉麻了。还是像以前一样，叫我红弩箭。
Lilya: Come on, quit with the titles. Lilya's just fine.

红弩箭：我回城里给你们再取些酒。
Lilya: I'm just going to get some more drinks from the city.

谢尔盖：哦——酒后飞行！
Sergey: Oho, flying under the influence? You sure?

红弩箭：报警抓我。
Lilya: Catch me if you can.

引擎喷出橘色尾焰，仍被命名为红色38的新式飞行扫帚转眼间冲入了云层，消失在众人眼前。
The engine flares orange. Her new broom, carrying Lilya and the name Red 38, shoots into the clouds and disappears.

军长疑惑地看着飞行器尾迹冲向别列格勒，才掀开门帘走进了营帐。
The commander examines the trail toward Bereggrad with a puzzled look. Then he lifts the tent flap and steps inside.

军长伊万：红弩箭中尉去哪里了？
Commander Ivan: Where's Lieutenant Lilya off to?

斯捷尔诺娃：回别列格勒拿酒去了。
Sternova: The city. Said she'll bring back more drinks.

军长掂了掂手中酒瓶的重量，陷入沉思。
Weighing the bottle in his hand, he lapses into silence.

伊戈尔：你期望中的审判恐怕不会发生，中尉。
Igor: I'm afraid there won't be any judgment for me, Lieutenant Lilya.
