红弩箭：凭什么这么笃定？你有自信永远不被送上基金会的审判庭？
Lilya: Oh yeah? What's got you so confident?

伊戈尔：重塑之手和基金会的战争还很漫长，在结束之前，抓捕我的命令根本不会下达。
Igor: This war between Manus Vindictae and the Foundation will grind on for a long time to come. They won't give the order to arrest me until it ends.

枪口向前顶了顶，撞在神秘学家的后脑上——不比钢铁坚硬，也不似棉花柔软。
The gun presses harder against his head.

神秘学家与人类的骨结构无异，在子弹面前，这是一处致命的弱点。
An arcanist's skull is like any other. It has no defense against a bullet.

伊戈尔：芝诺害怕引起士气崩溃与外部质疑，于是装模作样地把我们的照片挂上纪功廊。
Igor: They might call us traitors, but still, our names and faces are listed as martyrs in Zeno's Hall of Merit. They know that others doubt, and they fear for their morale.

伊戈尔：当然，现在谁都知道我没有身亡。但逼迫一个可能的第三方成为敌人，对基金会的战略没有任何好处。
Igor: They know I still live, of course. Even so, the Foundation gains nothing from making an enemy of me, so long as I remain a potential ally.

威胁未能引起长者的恐慌，伊戈尔神情自若，平静地回应着身后压抑不住怒火的红弩箭。
The threat brings him no fear. He only answers her anger with measured calm.

伊戈尔：而我在圣保罗所犯下的罪行，已经让基金会与芝诺的各个派别之间出现摆上台面的嫌隙。
Igor: And as a result of my actions in São Paulo, the rift between the Foundation and the various factions of Zeno has been laid bare.

红弩箭：嫌隙……
Lilya: Rift?

在这场由重塑之手推动的战争中，本应作为主要战力的芝诺被联合指挥部派往了遥远的东线。
Zeno should have been at the front lines of this war with Manus Vindictae, yet the joint command sent them to the Eastern Front.

飞行女巫知道他是对的。
Lilya knows he speaks the truth.

红弩箭：如果由基金会主导对你的审判，那将被芝诺视作挑衅。
Lilya: Huh. So if the Foundation put you on trial, it'd be like they're spitting in Zeno's face.

她忍不住斜眼望向天空。
She looks up at the sky despite herself.

几名被她安排了巡逻任务的飞行巫师正从别列格勒上方驶过，基金会灰白的制服让她们有如掠空的白鸽。
The Flying Witches she put on patrol pass overhead. Their gray and white Foundation uniforms make them look like fluttering doves.

红弩箭：鸽子屋会出面的。
Lilya: But the Pax House will intervene.

伊戈尔：即便它的出面会导致基金会与芝诺之间的信任彻底破产？
Igor: Even if their direct intervention would sever all trust between the Foundation and Zeno?

红弩箭：信任……破产？
Lilya: Sever all trust? How?

伊戈尔：芝诺希望所有人遗忘组织在圣保罗受到的屈辱，基金会也不愿意自己在芝诺中安插眼线的事被端上台面。
Igor: The last thing Zeno wants is to relive the shame of São Paulo. Likewise, the Foundation has no desire to reveal how deep their network goes.

伊戈尔：鸽子屋一旦介入，组织间微妙的平衡就难以继续维持。
Igor: If the Pax House intervenes, that delicate balance will crumble.

红弩箭：等等，你刚刚说的眼线，难道说那些在圣保罗被你“放弃”的人……
Lilya: Wait, network? Do you mean the soldiers you "dealt with" in São Paulo?

伊戈尔：有十名人类士兵，四名神秘学家拒绝同我们离开。
Igor: Ten humans and four arcanists refused to join our rebellion.

伊戈尔：其中三人是早已暴露在我们视野中的内应，余下的……
Igor: Three were spies we had long sniffed out. As for the rest ...

伊戈尔闭了闭眼，不再为自己辩驳。
Igor closes his eyes. He won't defend himself any further.

红弩箭：——
Lilya: Ahhh!

红弩箭：他们曾是你的战友！
Lilya: Bulls**t! They were all our comrades, every one of them!

颤抖的手指微微拉动扳机。
A trembling finger tightens on the trigger.

红弩箭：与你并肩，与你的近卫团共进退，同喝最后一滴水，分食最后一口干粮的人们！
Lilya: They fought together with you! Shared their canteens and rations with you!

红弩箭：用任务把他们支走，打晕他们，给他们下药。你明明有无数种方式带着你信任的人偷偷离开！
Lilya: You could've sent them off somewhere! Could've arrested them, knocked them out, put them to sleep! You had a million ways to pull off your rebellion without killing them!

红弩箭：——为什么杀害他们！
Lilya: You chose to murder them! Why?

苍老的呼吸没有因质问而变得更急促，只是更加沉重。
The old man's breath doesn't hasten, but his chest heaves.

伊戈尔：天使兄弟会的人在盯着我们。
Igor: The Apostles Brotherhood was watching.

伊戈尔：为了换取可控的未来，减少无意义的牺牲，这是必要的流血。
Igor: To reach a future free from meaningless sacrifices, some cost must be paid.

红弩箭：你把他们当成了向重塑之手投诚的筹码。
Lilya: So, you used them, ended them so you could go on with the Manus!

伊戈尔：……
Igor: ...

伊戈尔：是的。
Igor: Yes.

红弩箭：你必须为此付出代价。
Lilya: You'll pay for what you did!

伊戈尔：这是我的罪孽，我不会否认或回避它。偿还的日子终究会到来的。
Igor: I've committed many crimes. I will not run from them. I will be ready to surrender my life when the day comes.

伊戈尔：不过，在那之前，我还是能为司辰提供她需要的援助，如同在顿河的这一次。这只是一个开始。
Igor: But it has not come. Until it does, I will continue to assist the Timekeeper. Her fight is only just beginning.

此刻，草原寂静得连风都沉了下来。只有年轻飞行员的呼吸愈发沉重。
The wind drops and the grassland falls still. Only the young pilot's breath grows heavier.

红弩箭：……
Lilya: ...

红弩箭：该死的！！
Lilya: Motherf**ker!

左轮手枪被她烦闷地扔开，疯长的野草将武器拢入怀中，在转轮中扎下了根。
She flings the revolver to the ground, the wild grass swallowing it.

红弩箭：你什么态度？说死就死？你的死代表不了任何东西！
Lilya: Of all the goddamned arrogance! You're ready to die? No, your death won't fix anything!

红弩箭：而且你带走的那些人又怎么办？你甚至还欠洛佩拉一个交代！
Lilya: What about everyone who decided to follow you, huh? What about Lopera? You owe her an explanation!

红弩箭：该死，你说得没错，伊万。
Lilya: Damn it! You were right about this old fart, Ivan.

红弩箭：这老头已经疯了，疯得该被送去小梅斯梅尔那儿狠狠电一电。
Lilya: He's got a screw loose in the brain. Someone should send him to Mesmer Jr. to sort him out!

军长从土坡后走了出来，显然从最开始就隐匿在了审判现场。
The commander steps out from behind a rise. Clearly he has been watching, unseen, from the start.

他注视着伊戈尔，透过对方沧桑的眼睛寻找过去的痕迹。
He studies Igor, searching for a trace of the past in his weathered eyes.

军长伊万：你确实是个疯子，伊戈尔。
Commander Ivan: You are a madman, Igor.

军长伊万：除了重塑之手，这世上哪儿还有敢同时跟芝诺与基金会叫板的神秘学家？
Commander Ivan: Except Manus Vindictae, who else dares challenge Zeno and the Foundation?

军长伊万：而你现在也彻底得罪了重塑之手。你的新军团已经骑虎难下了。
Commander Ivan: And now, even the Manus march against you. Your Legion walks amid tigers.

伊戈尔转向这位老友，态度自若，仿若深陷泥潭的人并不是自己。
Igor turns to his old friend with an unusual calm, as if he weren't sinking into a mire.

伊戈尔：骑虎难下？不……
Igor: Amid tigers? No.

伊戈尔：我的军团会成为一匹翱翔于世界的狮鹫。
Igor: My Legion soars high above, like the indomitable gryphon.

伊戈尔：我的孩子们会用利爪撕碎所有敌人，用羽翼庇护彼此，拉着方舟不断越过时间。
Igor: My children will rend their foes with claws and guard their friends with wings, and they will bear the ark safely through the currents of time.

红弩箭：收收你的雄心壮志。
Lilya: Don't flatter yourself.

红弩箭啐了一声。
Lilya spits.

红弩箭：说得倒轻巧，那些罪可没办法一笔勾销。
Lilya: Nothing you do will ever be enough to atone for what you've done.

军长伊万：的确，没有任何方式能弥补他造成的流血。但也没有任何人能否定他在南极和别列格勒做的一切。
Commander Ivan: Agreed. Still, none can deny his deeds in Antarctica and Bereggrad.

红弩箭：南极……
Lilya: Antarctica ...

红弩箭：我听头儿提过，是你的副官帮助乌尔里希绕过了重塑之手的布防。
Lilya: I heard from the captain that Ulrich bypassed the Manus troops thanks to Lieutenant Moldir.

红弩箭：你暗示的？
Lilya: That your order?

伊戈尔：这是莫莉德尔自我意志下的选择，我并未阻拦她，但也不必将这份高光算在我身上。
Igor: No. This was Moldir's choice. I did not intervene, true, but I cannot take any credit for it.

红弩箭：你这老头……
Lilya: *sigh* Stubborn old fart.

红弩箭：这是最后一次机会。
Lilya: If you step even one toe out of line, you're dead.

红弩箭跨上扫帚，启动引擎前回头看向伊戈尔。
She mounts her broom. Before starting the engine, she looks back at Igor.

她指了指在云层中穿梭的飞行巫师们。
She points up at the Flying Witches in the clouds.

红弩箭：我们会看着你——我会牢牢盯着你。
Lilya: We'll be watching you. I will be watching you.

伊戈尔缓缓点头作为回应。
Igor responds with a slow nod.

一股无名火卡在胸腔里难以释放，红弩箭从鼻腔里发出了“哼”的一声，把引擎转速拉到最大，发泄似地冲上了天。
A shapeless anger sits in Lilya's chest. She snorts and tears into the sky.

军长伊万：我们年轻的时候和她一模一样。
Commander Ivan: We were just like her once.

军长伊万：不容许眼里有沙子，看不惯的东西就用自己的手去摆正，觉得是错误的就亲自去纠正。
Commander Ivan: Young, unable to ignore anything we saw as unjust, compelled to personally right every wrong.

伊戈尔：但没有因此冒着生命危险独自行动过……噢。
Igor: But we never put our lives on the line like her, did we? Ah, wait.

他眉上的疤痕随笑意动了动，眼中流露出怀念。
The scar on his brow moves with his smile. Memory does live in those old eyes.

伊戈尔：你有过。
Igor: You did.

军长伊万：你也是。
Commander Ivan: So did you.

军长伊万：我不知道人到了你这个岁数还会有所变化，伊戈尔。这种变化……也不是我认为理想的方向。
Commander Ivan: I never thought an old cat like you would change his spots. Not a change I favor, mind.

伊戈尔：人和河流一样，一成不变的结果是腐烂。它要找到通往海洋的道路。
Igor: A river turns foul when it halts. We must all find our way to the ocean.

伊戈尔向河边走了两步，靴后的马刺在河滩软泥上划出笔直的线。
Igor steps toward the river, his boot spurs cutting lines in the soft mud at the bank.

伊戈尔：是你劝她把子弹退出来的？
Igor: I suspect you were the one that persuaded the lieutenant to leave her gun unloaded.

军长伊万：你帮了我们一把。
Commander Ivan: I owed you for what you did for the Corps.

军长烦闷地抓了一把自己的头发，走到伊戈尔身边。
The commander runs an agitated hand through his hair and joins Igor.

军长伊万：有烟吗？
Commander Ivan: Got a cigarette?

伊戈尔：戒了。99年之后。
Igor: I quit back in 99.

事业有成、声名显赫的芝诺骑兵军军长薅了一把河边的草。
The famed commander of the Zeno Cavalry pulls a handful of grass from a nearby tuft.

军长伊万：你知道红柳树村一战后，现在骑兵军里有多少孩子想和你走吗？
Commander Ivan: Do you have any idea how many of my silly pups wish to follow you after Tamarovka?

伊戈尔：我找到了一块足够大的净土，这其中也有你和骑兵军的位置。
Igor: I've found a place, somewhere big enough to welcome you and the Corps.

军长伊万：我还不想成为芝诺和基金会的双重通缉犯。
Commander Ivan: I'm not ready to have a bounty on my head.

伊戈尔：但你为我这个“通缉犯”说情了，你是怎么说服红弩箭中尉的？
Igor: But you spoke in this bounty target's defense. What did you say to Lieutenant Lilya?

军长伊万：用一颗子弹了结你，还是让你永远活在背负鲜血的痛苦里。
Commander Ivan: I gave her a choice: end your life with a bullet, or let you live bearing the pain of your guilt.

伊戈尔：你怎么能确定我不是一个冷血的，不会感受到痛苦的叛徒？
Igor: Did you ever consider that I might just be a cold-hearted tyrant? That I feel no guilt at all?

伊戈尔：就像你说的，“暴雨”后，我们都变了很多。
Igor: We've all changed since the "Storm."

军长伊万：遗书，老朋友。
Commander Ivan: I read your letter, old friend.

军长伊万：这是死亡的力量，它比任何吐真剂都来得强大。
Commander Ivan: No truth serum could tell me more than it did.

军长伊万：“我玷污了我们曾最引以为傲的荣耀。”
Commander Ivan: "I tarnished with my own hands the honor we once held dear."

军长伊万：“莫莉，请告诉洛佩拉……”
Commander Ivan: "Molly, please tell Lopera that—"

军长执信的手边裂开一道漆黑的神秘术辉光，自黑暗而来的巨口叼住信纸，咀嚼着把信拖回了虚无中。
A dark arcane glow appears by the letter. A shadowy mouth emerges from it, chews it down, and drags it into the void.

伊戈尔手中的罐子闪烁了一瞬，一只萤火虫悠悠坠落在瓶底。
The jar in Igor's hand flickers. A firefly dims and falls to the bottom.

军长伊万：认真的吗？让你老态龙钟的身体变得更脆弱，只为了保护这点隐私？
Commander Ivan: Really? Running your old bones deeper into the ground just to protect your privacy?

伊戈尔：哈，隐私，我以为你不知道这个词是什么意思呢。
Igor: Ha, privacy. I thought you'd never heard of the word!

军长伊万：我可不是故意的。这两天士兵们嚷嚷着想把遗书领回去。是你自己没有写好名字，才让这封信落了下来。
Commander Ivan: I didn't mean to pry. The soldiers were getting their letters. Yours was the only one with no name.

军长伊万：……
Commander Ivan: ...

军长伊万：明天一早，我会带骑兵军离开顿河，他们很多人都不会再有机会回到家乡。
Commander Ivan: We ride out come morning. We all know that many of us will never return.

军长伊万：就此别过之前，你还有一次去骑兵军塞契的机会。
Commander Ivan: You still have a chance to come to the sich before we leave.

伊戈尔：你想让我带走那些年轻人？
Igor: You want me to take those young soldiers in?

军长伊万：这不该是他们的战争。
Commander Ivan: This was never meant to be their war.

红弩箭的飞行器在天空留下一道久不消散的痕迹。
Lilya's aircraft has left a lingering line across the sky.

军长伊万：他们理应见到下一个春天。
Commander Ivan: They deserve to see the new spring.

五天后
Five days later

伊里内伊：位于基金会内部，无需额外提起外出申请，但又绝对保密的场所。你比我想象中更谨慎，司辰。
Irinei: Located in a Foundation facility, completely confidential, and no field mission application required. You're more thoughtful than I expected, Timekeeper.

维尔汀：消失太久总归会有人起疑，我们的时间很紧迫，伊里内伊委员。
Vertin: Let's make the most of our time, Mr. Irinei, before our absence draws unnecessary attention.

伊里内伊：我理解了，那就让我们长话短说。
Irinei: Then let's cut to the chase.

伊里内伊：关于你在琥珀屋实验室回收的情报——关于“灌体”实验。
Irinei: About the vessel ensoulment experiments conducted in the Amber Room laboratory.

伊里内伊：你知道了多少？
Irinei: What have you learned?

维尔汀：……
Vertin: ...

维尔汀：很遗憾，除了最基本的实验步骤外……
Vertin: I managed to recover documents detailing the experiment's main procedures. However ...

维尔汀：实验室里没有留下更多与兀尔德有关的信息。
Vertin: I didn't find anything signiﬁcant about Urd.
